While the Six Psalms are being read, the priest says these
prayers:

The First Prayer
We thank You, Lord our God, for You have raised us up
from our beds, and have filled our mouths with a word of
praise that we might worship You and call upon Your holy
Name, and we beseech You by Your compassion with which
You have always treated our life: also now send help to those
who stand before the countenance of Your holy glory and
await Your rich mercy; and grant, that with fear and love, they
may always offer worship, to praise Your ineffable goodness.
For to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, is due all glory,
honor, and worship, now and ever and forever. Amen.
98

Weekday and Lenten Matins

The Second Prayer
From the night our spirit rises early unto You, our God,
for Your commandments are a light upon the earth. Give us
understanding that we may be perfected in righteousness and
holiness in fear of You, for it is You Whom we glorify as our
true God. Incline Your ear and hear us, O Lord, and remember
all present and praying with us by name, and save them by
Your might. Bless Your people and sanctify Your inheritance.
Give peace to Your world, to Your churches, to the priests,
to the government (or to our God-protected king), and to all
Your people.
For blessed and glorified is Your all-honored and sublime
Name, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever and forever.
Amen.

The Third Prayer
From the night our spirit rises early to You, O God,
for Your commandments are light. Teach us, O God, Your
righteousness, Your commandments, and Your statutes.
Enlighten the eyes of our understanding so that we never fall
asleep in sins unto death. Drive out all gloomy darkness from
our hearts. Give us the Sun of Justice, and by the seal of Your
Holy Spirit preserve our life unassailed. Direct our steps in the
way of peace. Grant us to see the dawn and the day in joy that
we may send up our morning prayers to You.
For Yours is the might, and Yours are the kingdom, and
the power, and the glory, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now
and ever and forever. Amen.

99

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

The Fourth Prayer
O Master God, holy and beyond understanding, Who
commanded light to shine out of darkness, Who have given
us rest in the sleep of night and have raised us up for the
glorification and supplication of Your goodness, we entreat
You of Your own tender compassion; also accept us who
now worship You and give thanks to You as much as it is in
our power, and grant us all our petitions which are for our
salvation. Show us to be sons of light and of the day and
heirs of Your eternal good gifts. Remember, O Lord, in the
multitude of Your mercies all Your people, both those who
are praying with us as well as all our brethren on land, at
sea, [in the air,] and in every place of Your dominion who are
in need of Your love for mankind and help; and grant Your
great mercy to all so that, being preserved in safety in soul and
body, with confidence we may give glory to Your wondrous
and blessed Name.
For You are a merciful, gracious God and You love
mankind, and we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy
Spirit, now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Fifth Prayer
Treasury of Blessings, Ever-flowing Fountain, Holy
Father, Wonderworker, All-powerful and Almighty One, we
all worship You and pray to You, imploring Your mercies and
compassions to help and protect our lowliness. Remember,
O Lord, Your servants. Receive the morning prayers of us all
like incense before You, and let none of us be found unfit,
but encompass us all with Your mercies. Remember, O Lord,
those who keep vigil and sing of Your glory, and of Your onlybegotten Son and our God, and of Your Holy Spirit. Be their
Helper and Defender. Accept their supplications upon Your
100

Weekday and Lenten Matins

heavenly and spiritual altar.
For You are our God, and to You we give glory, to the
Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever. Amen.

The Sixth Prayer
We give thanks to You, Lord God of our salvation, for You
do all things for the well-being of our life that we may always
look to You, the Savior and Benefactor of our souls; for You
have given us rest in that time of the night that has passed
and have raised us up from our beds and appointed us in the
worship of Your honorable Name. Therefore, we pray You, O
Lord, give us grace and power that we may be made worthy
to sing to You with understanding and to pray unceasingly in
fear and trembling, working out our salvation with the help
of Your Christ. Remember also, O Lord, those who cry out to
You in the night. Hear them and have mercy, and crush under
their feet invisible and hostile enemies.
For You are the King of peace, and the Savior of our souls,
and we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now
and ever and forever. Amen.

The Seventh Prayer
God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, Who have
raised us from our beds and gathered us at this hour of prayer,
give us grace in the opening of our mouths and receive our
thanksgivings according to the ability of our power, and teach
us Your statutes. For we do not know how to pray as we
ought, unless You, O Lord, instruct us by Your Holy Spirit.
Therefore, we pray to You: remit, pardon, forgive if we have
sinned in any way unto this very hour by word or deed or
thought, voluntarily or involuntarily; for if You, O Lord,
101

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

should mark our guilt, Lord, who would survive? But with
You is found redemption. You alone are holy, the powerful
Helper, Defender of our life, and our songs are always of You.
May the might of Your kingdom be blessed and glorified,
Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Eighth Prayer
Lord our God, Who have banished from us the slothfulness
of sleep, and have summoned us together by a holy calling
to lift up our hands also in the night and confess to You
the righteousness of Your judgments: Receive our prayers,
petitions, confessions, and nocturnal worship; and grant us, O
God, a faith unashamed, confident hope, and a love without
pretense. Bless our comings and goings, our deeds, works,
words, thoughts; and grant us to come to the beginning of
the day, praising, singing, and blessing the greatness of Your
ineffable power.
For blessed is Your all-holy Name, and glorified is Your
kingdom, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever and
forever. Amen.

The Ninth Prayer
Lord our God, Who have given mankind remission of
sins through repentance, and have shown us the repentance
of the prophet David that led to pardon as a model of
acknowledgement and confession of sins: You, Yourself, O
Master, according to Your great mercy have mercy on us who
have fallen into so many and so great offenses, and in Your
compassion blot out our offenses. For against You have we
sinned, O Lord, Who know both the hidden and secret things
of the human heart, and Who alone have power to forgive
sins. A pure heart You have created in us and have established
102

Weekday and Lenten Matins

us with Your guiding Spirit, and have shown us the joy of
Your salvation; do not cast us from Your face. But, as You are
good and love mankind, be well-pleased that we may offer
to You a sacrifice of righteousness and oblation on Your holy
altars even until our last breath.
Through the mercy and compassion and loving-kindness
of Your only-begotten Son with Whom You are blessed,
together with Your all-holy and good and life-creating Spirit,
now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Tenth Prayer
O God, our God, Who by Your will have brought into
being the spiritual and rational Powers, we pray You and
we implore You: Receive our hymns of glorification which
together with all Your creatures we offer according to our
strength, and grant us in return the rich gifts of Your lovingkindness. For to You bows every knee in heaven and on earth
and in the infernal regions, and everything that has breath and
all creation sings Your incomprehensible glory. For You alone
are the true and most-merciful God.
For all the heavenly Powers praise You, and we give glory
to You, to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit,
now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Eleventh Prayer
We praise You, we sing to You, we bless You, and we
give thanks to You, God of our fathers, for You have brought
us through the shades of night and have shown us again the
light of day. But we pray Your loving goodness: cleanse our
sins, and accept our prayer in Your great tender goodness,
for we flee to Your refuge, O merciful and all-powerful God.
Make the true Sun of Justice shine in our hearts, enlighten
103

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

our mind, and guard all our senses, so that walking nobly in
the way of Your commandments as in the day, we may attain
to life eternal, for with You is the fountain of life, and may
we be deemed worthy to come to the enjoyment of Your
unapproachable light.
For You are our God, and to You we give glory, to the
Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever. Amen.

In peace, let us pray to the Lord.

[Psalm 117]
The Lord is God and has revealed Himself to us; blessed

Verse 1: Give thanks to the Lord for He is good; for His

Verse 2: They encircled me, compassed me about; in the

eyes.
Then we say the appointed troparion twice and the
theotokion in the same tone. If two troparia are appointed, the
first is always said twice, then the second and the theotokion
are said.

Trinitarian Hymns, Tone 1:
Through bodily forms, we have come to the spiritual and
immaterial understanding of the bodiless powers, and by the
singing of the thrice-holy hymn, we have received the light of
the Divinity in three Persons. Let us sing with the cherubim to
our only God: Holy, holy, holy are You, O our God:
Glory:
With all the powers of heaven let us sing as the cherubim,
and offer the thrice-holy hymn of praise to the Most High:
Holy, holy, holy are You, O our God, through the prayers of
all Your saints, have mercy on us.
Now and ever:
Awakening from sleep we worship You, O blessed One,
and offer the angelic hymn to You, O powerful One: Holy, holy,
holy are You, O God, through the prayers of the Theotokos,
have mercy on us.

Through the prayers of the Theotokos, have mercy on us.

Trinitarian Hymns, Tone 5:
This is the time for praise and the hour of prayer; let us
unceasingly cry to the Lord: Holy, holy, holy are You, O God:
Glory:
With unworthy lips we dare to represent the heavenly
hosts and sing to You, O eternal Trinity: Holy, holy, holy are
You, O God. Through the prayers of all Your saints, have
mercy on us.
Now and ever:
O Christ, You dwelt in the virginal womb without being
separated from the bosom of the Father; accept our praise
with the angels: Holy, holy, holy are You, O God. Through the
prayers of the Theotokos, have mercy on us.

Trinitarian Hymns, Tone 6:
The six-winged powers with immaterial lips sing the
thrice-holy hymn with unceasing voice to You, our God, and
110

Weekday and Lenten Matins

we on earth with unworthy lips render praise to You: Holy,
holy, holy are You, O God:
Glory:
Before You stand the cherubim with fear and the seraphim
trembling in awe, offering the thrice-holy hymn with unceasing
voices, and we sinners also cry out with them: Holy, holy,
holy are You, O God. Through the prayers of all Your saints,
have mercy on us.
Now and ever:
Let us glorify the three Persons in one God, united without
confusion, and let us take up the hymn of the angels as we
sing: Holy, holy, holy are You, O God. Through the prayers of
the Theotokos, have mercy on us.

Trinitarian Hymns, Tone 7:
To the unapproachable Divinity and the unique Trinity, let
us offer the thrice-holy praise of the seraphim, and with fear
let us sing: Holy, holy, holy are You, O God:
Glory:
Shaking off both laziness and sleep, arise and offer praise
to the Creator, and in fear, O soul, sing to Him: Holy, holy,
holy are You, O God. Through the prayers of all Your saints,
have mercy on us.
Now and ever:
Your great glory is praised by the cherubim, O Lord, and
the angels adore Your divine majesty; accept from our sinful
lips as we praise You on earth: Holy, holy, holy are You, O
111

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

God. Through the prayers of the Theotokos, have mercy on
us.

Trinitarian Hymns, Tone 8:
Lifting our hearts to heaven, let us imitate the heavenly
orders, and let us fall down with fear before the Judge, as we
sing the hymn of victory and say: Holy, holy, holy are You, O
God:
Glory:
The cherubim dare not raise their eyes to You as they
joyfully sing the divine words of the thrice-holy hymn; and
we also cry out with them: Holy, holy, holy are You, O God.
Through the prayers of all Your saints, have mercy on us.
Now and ever:
Overwhelmed by the weight of our many sins, we dare
not raise our eyes to heaven; with souls and bodies bowed
before You, we sing together with the angels: Holy, holy, holy
are You, O God. Through the prayers of the Theotokos, have
mercy on us.

From Pascha to the Leave-taking,
after the Stichologia we say:
Having beheld the resurrection of Christ let us worship the
holy Lord Jesus Who alone is sinless. We bow to Your cross,
O Christ, and we glorify and praise Your holy Resurrection.
You are our God, and besides You we recognize no other,
and we call upon Your Name. Come, all you faithful, and let
us bow to the holy Resurrection of Christ since, through the
cross, joy has come to all the world. Ever blessing the Lord,
let us extol His Resurrection since He, having suffered the
crucifixion, has destroyed Death by His death.
_________________________________________________
[Morning Praise]
After this, Psalm 50:

Have mercy on me, God, in Your kindness.
In Your compassion blot out my offence.
O wash me more and more from my guilt
and cleanse me from my sin.
My offences truly I know them;
my sin is always before me.
Against You, You alone, have I sinned;
what is evil in Your sight I have done.
That You may be justified when You give sentence
and be without reproach when You judge
O see, in guilt I was born,
a sinner was I conceived.
114

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Indeed You love truth in the heart;
then in the secret of my heart teach me wisdom
O sprinkle me with hyssop then I shall be clean;
O wash me, I shall be whiter than snow.
Make me hear rejoicing and gladness,
that the bones You have crushed may thrill.
From my sins turn away Your face
and blot out all my guilt.
A pure heart create for me, O God,
put a steadfast spirit within me.
Do not cast me away from Your presence,
nor deprive me of Your Holy Spirit.
Give me again the joy of Your help;
with a spirit of fervour sustain me,
That I may teach transgressors Your ways
and sinners may return to You.
O rescue me, God, my helper,
and my tongue shall ring out Your goodness.
O Lord, open my lips
and my mouth shall declare Your praise.
For in sacrifice You take no delight,
burnt offering from me You would refuse,
My sacrifice, a contrite spirit.
A humbled, contrite heart, You will not spurn.
In Your goodness, O Lord, show favor to Zion:
Rebuild the walls of Jerusalem.
Then You will be pleased with lawful sacrifice,
115

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

(burnt offerings wholly consumed),
then You will be offered young bulls on Your altar.

Save Your people, O God, and bless Your inheritance.

Christian people of the true faith and send down upon us Your

Theotokos and Ever-Virgin Mary; through the power of the

the great ecumenical teachers and hierarchs: Basil the Great,
Gregory the Theologian, and John Chrysostom; of our father
among the saints, Nicholas the Wonderworker, archbishop of
Myra in Lycia; of the holy Cyril and Methodius, equals-tothe-apostles, teachers of the Slavs; of the holy well-believing
great prince Vladimir, equal-to-the-apostles; of our holy

and Theodosius of the Monastery of the Caves; and of all our

ancestors of God, Joachim and Anna; of Saint Name (whose
church it is), Saint (Name), whose memory we celebrate; and
of all the saints; we pray You, O most merciful Lord, hear us
sinners praying to You, and have mercy on us.

The Canticle of the Theotokos
from the Holy Gospel according to Luke
The ancient verse: We extol the Theotokos in hymns!
My soul magnifies the Lord, and my spirit rejoices in
God, my Savior.
And after each of the following sing the verse: More
honorable than the cherubim, and beyond compare more
glorious than the seraphim; who, a virgin, gave birth to God
the Word, you, truly the Theotokos, we magnify.
Because He has regarded the humility of His handmaid,
for behold, from henceforth all generations shall call me
blessed, sing the verse.
Because He Who is mighty has done great things for me,
and holy is His Name, and His love is from generation to
generation to those who fear Him, sing the verse.

Weekday and Lenten Matins

He has shown might with His arm; He has scattered the
proud in the conceit of their heart, sing the verse.
He has put down the mighty from their seat and has

He has received Israel, His servant, being mindful of His

After the Ninth Ode:
It is truly proper to glorify you, O Theotokos, the everblessed, immaculate, and the mother of our God. More

HYMNS OF LIGHT
If it is the Forty Day Fast, the Hymns of Light are said
three times according to the appointed tone.
This is said at the conclusion of the Hymns of Light:
On Monday, to the first repetition:
Through the protection of Your incorporeal powers, and
save me.
On Tuesday:
Through the prayers of Your Forerunner, O Lord, and
save me.
On Wednesday and on Friday:
Through the power of Your cross, O Lord, and save me.
On Thursday:
Through the prayers of Your holy apostles and holy
Bishop Nicholas, and save me.
The second, at Glory: at the ending always say:
Through the prayers of all Your saints, and save me.
And the third, at Now and ever: at the ending say:
Through the prayers of the Theotokos, and save me.
120

Weekday and Lenten Matins

And in the Sixth Tone, at the beginning of the Hymn of Light,
instead of:
Through the protection of Your incorporeal powers:
If it is Tuesday, this is said:
Through the prayers of Your Forerunner, O Lord: and the
rest of the Hymn is said to the conclusion.
And on Wednesday and on Friday, instead of:
Through the protection of Your incorporeal powers: at the
beginning this is said:
Through the power of Your cross, O Lord, send forth Your
eternal light to our souls.
And on Thursday, this:
Through the prayers of Your holy apostles and holy
Bishop Nicholas, O Lord, send forth Your eternal light to our
souls.
At the second, at Glory: this is said at the beginning of the
Hymn of Light:
Through the prayers of all Your saints, O Lord, send forth
Your eternal light to our souls.
At the third, at Now and ever: this is said at the beginning
of the Hymn of Light:
Through the prayers of the Theotokos, O Lord, send forth
Your eternal light to our souls.
121

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Tone 1
Send light, O Lord, to purify my soul from all sin, (through
the protection of the incorporeal powers), and save me.

Tone 2
Send forth Your eternal light, O Christ God, and mystically
enlighten the eyes of my heart, (through the protection of the
incorporeal powers), and save me.

Tone 3
Send forth Your light, O Christ God, and enlighten my
heart, (through the protection of the incorporeal powers), and
save me.

Tone 4
Send light on Your world and purify my truly darkened
soul from all sin, (through the protection of the incorporeal
powers), and save me.

Tone 5
O Light-giving Lord, send forth Your light and enlighten
my heart, (through the protection of the incorporeal powers),
and save me.

Tone 6
(Through the protection of the incorporeal powers), O
Lord, send forth Your eternal light to our souls.

122

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Tone 7
Raise me, O Lord, to sing Your praises, and teach me
to do Your will, O Holy One, (through the protection of the
incorporeal powers), and save me.

Tone 8
You Yourself are the light, O Christ, enlighten me with
this very light, (through the protection of the incorporeal
powers), and save me.

EXAPOSTILARIA FOR THE ENTIRE WEEK
Monday
According to: O Women, hear:
(Ženy uslyšite:  
)
Archangels and angels, principalities and dominions,
powers and virtues, thrones, and many-eyed cherubim and
six-winged seraphim, pray for us, that we be delivered from
affliction and unquenchable fire.
Or this:
As God, You adorned the heavens with the stars and
enlightened all the earth with the angels. O Creator of all
things, save us who sing to You.
123

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Theotokion:
You are my help, O most pure one, the strong support and
protection of the world, and I bow down to you and cry out:
Deliver me from all affliction and from the eternal fire, for in
you, O Virgin, is all my hope.

Tuesday
O most glorious prophet, and the Forerunner of grace, you
preached salvation through repentance for all and pointed out
the Lamb Who takes away the sins of the world, O blessed
one. Now pray to him to have mercy on the world.
Or this:
Let us all extol John the Forerunner, and the Baptizer of
the Savior, the prophet born of a prophet, the son of the desert
and born of Elizabeth.

Theotokion:
All the prophets prefigured you, O Virgin; David called
you a mountain, an ark, a lamp, a ladder, a manna-bearing
hand, and a life-budding staff. We also acknowledge you
fittingly as the Theotokos.

Wednesday and Friday
According to: O Women, hear:
)
(Ženy uslyšite:  
Invincible weapon and support of faith, O cross divine,
we sing to you and bow low before you in faith. You are the
refuge and glory of Christians, the guardian of the true faith
and pride of martyrs. It is indeed proper that we glorify you.
124

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Or this:
The cross is the defense of all the universe. The cross is
the beauty of the Church. The cross is the strength of rulers.
The cross is the support of all who believe. The cross is the
glory of angels but the wounding of demons.

Stavrotheotokion:
The most pure one, standing before the cross and seeing
her Son without sin dead on the wood, lamenting, and
shedding a mother’s tears, and cried: “What is this wonder,
that they have delivered the Creator of the world to be nailed
to a cross?”

Thursday
O apostles of the Lord: Peter and Paul, Andrew, James,
Bartholomew, and Matthew, James, Philip, Thomas, and
Simon, Luke, and John, and Mark: we, the faithful praise all
of you.
Or this:
According to: O Women, hear:
(Ženy uslyšite:  
)
To all who run beneath the sun, you have preached the
truth of Christ’s holy incarnation from the Virgin, you have
turned the people from error and enlightened them, and have
taught all to revere the Holy Trinity, O apostles of the Savior.

125

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Or another:
O holy twelve, glory of the apostles, with the precious
Nicholas, bishop of Myra, pray unceasingly to the Savior for
us.

Theotokion:
O Virgin untouched by temptation, with the wise apostles
and the hosts of martyrs, and with the wise Nicholas, pray
unceasingly to Christ that we be delivered from all danger,
and with boldness we may trust in you, O Maiden.

Friday
Rejoice, most holy cross, impregnable wall around the
world, refuge of the afflicted and protection of those in danger,
victory of kings and guard of armies, defeat of barbarians and
crown of apostles, and salvation of the faithful!
Or this:
The cross is the defense of all the universe. The cross is
the beauty of the Church. The cross is the strength of rulers.
The cross is the support of all who believe. The cross is the
glory of angels but the wounding of demons.

Stavrotheotokion:
Seeing You nailed to the cross, the most pure one cried
and moaned and uttered: “How can the Sun of glory set? O
primal Light, how could it be that You are nailed to a cross,
that You are pierced with a spear in Your side? This is for the
salvation of the human race, my Son and my God!”
126

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Saturday
O praiseworthy prophets, blessed apostles, righteous
patriarchs, unique succession of hierarchs, assembly of
venerable and righteous men and women, holy martyrs, pray,
all of you, with the Mother of God to the Lord to have mercy
on Your servants.
Or this:
O Source of all, as God You adorned heaven with stars.
You enlightened the whole earth with angels. Save those who
sing to You.
Another Hymn of Light for the departed:
As God You rule over the living and the dead. Give rest
to Your servants in the chosen place. Although they may have
sinned, O Savior, they did not abandon You.

Theotokion:
You are the delight of the angels, the joy of the sorrowful,
the protection of Christians, and the Virgin Mother of the
Lord. Help us, and deliver us from eternal pain.

THE PRAISES
If, on the one hand, it is a saint celebrated with the Great
Doxology, Let everything that lives and that has breath is
sung, and the rest, as directed for Sunday Matins.
If, on the other hand, it is an ordinary day, immediately
the psalms.
127

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Psalm 148
Praise the Lord from the heavens,
Praise Him in the heights.
Praise him, all His angels,
Praise him, all His host.
Praise Him, sun and moon,
Praise Him shining stars.
Praise Him highest heavens
and the waters above the heavens.
Let them praise the name of the Lord.
He commanded; they were made.
He fixed them for ever,
gave a law which shall not pass away.
Praise the Lord from the earth,
sea creatures and all oceans,
fire and hail, snow and mist,
stormy winds that obey His word;
all mountains and hills,
all fruit trees and cedars,
beasts, wild and tame,
reptiles and birds on the wing;
all earth’s kings and peoples,
earth’s princes and rulers;
young men and maidens,
old men together with children.

128

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Let them praise the name of the Lord
for He alone is exalted.
The splendor of His name
reaches beyond heaven and earth.
He exalts the strength of His people.
He is the praise of all His saints,
of the sons of Israel,
of the people to whom He comes close.

Psalm 149
Sing a new song to the Lord,
His praise in the assembly of the faithful.
Let Israel rejoice in its Maker,
let Zion’s sons exult in their king.
Let them praise His name with dancing
and make music with timbrel and harp.
For the Lord takes delight in His people.
He crowns the poor with salvation.
Let the faithful rejoice in their glory,
Shout for joy and take their rest.
Let the praise of God be on their lips
And a two-edged sword in their hand,
to deal out vengeance to the nations
And punishment on all the peoples;
To bind their kings in chains
And their nobles in fetters of iron;

129

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

On Six: to carry out the sentence pre-ordained: this honor
is for all His faithful.

Psalm 150
Praise God in His holy place, praise Him in His mighty
heavens.
On Four: Praise Him for His powerful deeds, praise His
surpassing greatness.
O praise Him with sound of trumpet, praise Him with lute
and harp.
Praise Him with timbrel and dance, praise Him with
strings and pipe.
O praise Him with resounding cymbals, praise Him
with clashing of cymbals. Let everything that lives and that
breathes give praise to the Lord.

[The Doxology]
Glory to God in the highest, and to people on earth peace
and good will. We praise You, we bless You, we worship You,
we glorify You, we thank You for Your great glory. Lord God,
heavenly King, Father Almighty; Lord, only-begotten Son,
Jesus Christ, and Holy Spirit. Lord God, Lamb of God, Son of
the Father, You take away the sin of the world, have mercy on
us. You take away the sins of the world, hear our prayer. You
are seated at the right hand of the Father, have mercy on us.
For You alone are holy, You alone are Lord, Jesus Christ, to
the glory of God the Father. Amen.
I will bless You every day, and praise Your Name forever.
O Lord, You have been our refuge from one generation
to the next. I said: Lord, have mercy on me, heal my soul
for I have sinned against You. O Lord, I have fled to You for
refuge. Teach me to do Your will, for You, O Lord, are my
God. In You is the source of life and in Your light we see light.
Extend Your mercy to those who know You.
Then:
Make us worthy, O Lord, to be kept sinless this morning.
Blessed are You, O Lord, the God of our fathers, and
praiseworthy and glorious is Your Name forever. Amen.
May Your mercy, O Lord, be upon us who have placed
our hope in You. Blessed are You, O Lord; teach me Your
commandments. Blessed are You, O Master; make me
understand Your commandments. Blessed are You, O Holy
One; enlighten me with Your commandments.
O Lord, Your mercy is forever; despise not the work of
Your hands. To You is due praise; to You is due a hymn; to
You is glory due, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever. Amen.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Let us complete our morning prayer to the Lord.
Choir: Lord, have mercy.
Protect us, save us, have mercy on us and preserve us, O
God, by Your grace.
Choir: Lord, have mercy.
That this whole day may be perfect, holy, peaceful, and
without sin, let us beseech the Lord.
After each of the following petitions, the choir sings:
Grant this, O Lord.
For an angel of peace, a faithful guide and guardian of our
souls and bodies, let us beseech the Lord.
For the pardon and remission of our sins and offenses, let
us beseech the Lord.
For what is good and beneficial to our souls and for peace
in the world, let us beseech the Lord.
That we may spend the rest of our life in peace and
repentance, let us beseech the Lord.
For a Christian, painless, unashamed, peaceful end of our
life, and for a good account before the fearsome judgmentseat of Christ, let us beseech the Lord.
Commemorating our most holy, most pure, most blessed
and glorious Lady, the Theotokos and Ever-Virgin Mary, with
all the saints, let us commit ourselves and one another and our
whole life to Christ our God.

Weekday and Lenten Matins

Choir: To You, O Lord.

For You are a merciful and gracious God, and You love

Choir: Amen.
Priest: Peace be to all.
Choir: And to your spirit.
Deacon: Bow your heads to the Lord.
Choir: To You, O Lord.

Holy Lord, You dwell on high and look upon the lowly,
and with Your all-seeing eyes You watch over all creation.
To You we bend our neck in heart and body and we pray
to You, stretch forth Your invisible hand from Your holy
dwelling place and bless us all. If we have sinned voluntarily
or involuntarily forgive us as a good God Who loves mankind
and gives us earthly and heavenly gifts.
He says aloud:
For it is Yours to have mercy on us and to save us, O God,
and we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now
and ever and forever.
Choir: Amen.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

[Psalm 89]

Verse 2: Let the favor of the Lord, our God, be upon us;

(Name), for our God-loving Bishop (Name), for those who

fathers, and for all our brothers and sisters in Christ.
In monasteries:
Again we pray for our holy father (Name), Pope
of Rome, and for our most reverend Archbishop and
Metropolitan (Name), for our God-loving Bishop (Name),
for our most venerable hieromonks: Proto-archimandrite
(Name), Archimandrite (Name), Proto-hegumen (Name), and
Hegumen (Name), for those who serve and have served in
this holy monastery, for our spiritual fathers, and for all our
brothers and sisters in Christ.
Again we pray for our government (or for our Godprotected Emperor or King whose realm it is Name for his
health and salvation) and for all in the service of our country.
Again we pray for the people here present who await Your
great and abundant mercy, for those who show us mercy, and
for all Christians of the true faith.
The priest exclaims:
For You are a merciful God and You love mankind, and
we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and
ever and forever.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

It is good to give thanks to the Lord, and to sing praises

Weekday and Lenten Matins

The priest:
Heavenly King, strengthen our government (or our Godprotected Emperor or our King Name), confirm the faith, calm
the nations, give peace to the world, preserve well this city
(or village, or this holy monastery). Grant our fathers and

The priest reads the prayer of Saint Ephrem the Syrian:
Lord and Master of my life, spare me from the spirit
of indifference, despair, lust for power, and idle chatter.
Prostration.
Instead, bestow on me, your servant, the spirit of integrity,
humility, patience and love. Prostration.
Yes, O Lord and King, let me see my own sins, and not
judge my brothers and sisters, for You are blessed, forever and
ever. Amen. Prostration.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Bow.
And again the entire prayer of Saint Ephrem with one
prostration after its conclusion.
And after the prostrations, the First Hour.

Weekday and Lenten Matins

THE DAILY DISMISSALS
Monday
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save us
through the prayers of His most pure Mother; through the
protection of the honorable and heavenly angelic powers;
through the prayers of the holy, glorious, and illustrious
apostles; of the holy (Name/s), the patron[s] [patroness] of
this church; of the holy (Name/s of the saint/s whose day it
is); and through the prayers of all the saints; for Christ is good
and loves mankind.

Tuesday
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save
us through the prayers of His most pure Mother; and of the
honorable and glorious prophet, Forerunner, and baptist John;
of the holy, glorious, and illustrious apostles; and the rest.

Wednesday and Friday
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save us
through the prayers of His most pure Mother; by the power of
the precious and life-creating cross; through the prayers of the
holy, glorious, and illustrious apostles; and the rest.

Thursday
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save us
through the prayers of His most pure Mother; and of the holy,
glorious, and illustrious apostles; of our holy father Nicholas
the Wonder-worker, archbishop of Myra; and the rest.

139

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Saturday
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save us
through the prayers of His most pure Mother; by the power
of the precious and life-creating cross; through the protection
of the honorable and heavenly angelic powers; through the
prayers of the honorable and glorious prophet, Forerunner,
and baptist John; of the holy, glorious, and illustrious apostles;
of our holy father Nicholas the Wonder-worker, archbishop
of Myra; of the holy, glorious, and victorious martyrs; of
our venerable and God-bearing fathers; of the holy and just
ancestors of God, Joachim and Anna; and the rest.

SUNDAY AND FESTAL MATINS
After the blessing, Sunday and Festal Matins begin the
same as Daily Matins, refer to pages 85 to 105.
After the Great Ektenia, refer to page 106, the following is
sung in the tone of the troparion of the day:
[Psalm 117]
The Lord is God and has revealed Himself to us; blessed
is He Who comes in the Name of the Lord.
Verse 1: Give thanks to the Lord for He is good; for His
love endures forever.
Verse 2: They encircled me, compassed me about; in the
Lord’s Name I crushed them.
Verse 3: I shall not die, I shall live and recount the deeds
of the Lord.
Verse 4: The stone which the builders rejected has become
the cornerstone. This is the work of the Lord, a marvel in our
eyes.
After The Lord is God, we say the appointed troparion
twice and the theotokion in the same tone. If two troparia are
appointed, the first is always said twice, then the second and
the theotokion are said.
Then the stichologia of the Psalter.
141

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

After the completion of the first stichologion, the deacon
or the priest does the Little Ektenia:
Again and again let us pray to the Lord in peace.
Choir: Lord, have mercy.
Protect us, save us, have mercy on us and preserve us, O
God, by Your grace.
Choir: Lord, have mercy.
Commemorating our most holy, most pure, most blessed
and glorious Lady, the Theotokos and Ever-Virgin Mary, with
all the saints, let us commit ourselves and one another and our
whole life to Christ our God.
Choir: To You, O Lord.
Exclamation:
For Yours is the might, and Yours are the kingdom and the
power, and the glory, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and
ever and forever.
Choir: Amen. And the Sessional Hymn according to the
order.
After the Second Stichologion: Again and again: and the
rest.
Exclamation:
For You, O God, are good and You love mankind, and to
You we give glory, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever.
Choir: Amen. And the Sessional Hymn according to the
order.
After this, on Feasts and, if prescribed, on Sunday is sung:

THE POLYELEOS
Psalm 134
Praise the name of the Lord, praise him, servants of the
Lord.
Versicle: Alleluia Three times.
Who stand in the house of the Lord in the courts of the
house of our God.
Praise the Lord for the Lord is good. Sing a psalm to His
name for He is loving.
For the Lord has chosen Jacob for Himself and Israel for
His own possession.
For I know that the Lord is great, that our Lord is high
above all gods.
The Lord does whatever He wills, in heaven, on earth, in
the seas.
He summons clouds from the ends of the earth; makes
lightning produce the rain; from His treasuries He sends forth
the wind.
The first-born of the Egyptians He smote, of man and
beast alike.
Signs and wonders He worked in the midst of your land,
O Egypt, against Pharaoh and all his servants.
Nations in their greatness He struck and kings in their
splendor He slew.
Sihon, king of the Amorites, Og, the king of Bashan, and
all the kingdoms of Canaan.
He let Israel inherit their land; on His people their land
He bestowed.

143

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Lord, Your name stands forever, unforgotten from age to
age.
For the Lord does justice for His people; the Lord takes
pity on His servants.
Pagan idols are silver and gold, the work of human hands.
They have mouths, but cannot speak; they have eyes but
they cannot see.
They have ears but they cannot hear; there is never a
breath on their lips.
Their makers will come to be like them and so will all
who trust in them!
Sons of Israel, bless the Lord! Sons of Aaron, bless the
Lord!
Sons of Levi, bless the Lord! You who fear Him, bless
the Lord!
From Zion may the Lord be blessed, He Who dwells in
Jerusalem!

Psalm 135
O give thanks to the Lord for He is good, for His love
endures for ever.
Versicle: Alleluia. Three times.
Give thanks to the God of gods, for His love endures for
ever.
Give thanks to the Lord of lords, for His love endures for
ever.
Who alone has wrought marvelous works, for His love
endures for ever.
Whose wisdom made the skies, for His love endures for
ever.

144

Sunday and Festal Matins

Who fixed the earth firmly on the seas, for His love
endures for ever.
It was He Who made the great lights, for His love endures
for ever.
The sun to rule in the day, for His love endures for ever.
The moon and stars in the night, for His love endures for
ever.
The first-born of the Egyptians He smote, for His love
endures for ever.
He brought Israel out from their midst, for His love
endures for ever.
Arm outstretched, with power in His hand, for His love
endures for ever.
He divided the Red Sea in two, for His love endures for
ever.
He made Israel pass through the midst, for His love
endures for ever.
He flung Pharaoh and his force into the sea, for His love
endures for ever.
Through the desert His people He led, for His love endures
for ever.
Nations in their greatness He struck, for His love endures
for ever.
Kings in their splendor He slew, for His love endures for
ever.
Sihon, king of the Amorities, for His love endures for

And Og, king of Bashan, for His love endures for ever.
He let Israel inherit their land, for His love endures for

On His servant their land He bestowed, for His love

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

He remembered us in our distress, for His love endures

To the God of heaven give thanks, for His love endures

TROPARIA OF THE RESURRECTION

Tone 5.
Verse: Blessed are You, O Lord; teach me Your
commandments.
The assembly of angels were amazed when they beheld
You, O Savior, among the dead. Destroying the power of
Death, You raised Adam with You and freed everyone from
Hades.
The radiant angel standing in the tomb said to the myrrhbearing women: “O disciples, why do you mingle tears of pity
with fragrant spices? Behold the tomb and understand that the
Savior is risen from the dead.”
Very early in the morning, the myrrh-bearing women
hastened with lamentation to Your tomb. But an angel stood
before them and said: “The time for lamenting is no more. Do
not weep but announce the resurrection to the apostles.”
O Savior, the myrrh-bearing women coming to Your tomb
with fragrant spices were weeping, and an angel spoke to them
saying: “Why do you think the living to be dead? For, as God,
He is risen from the tomb.”

[Morning Praise]
After this, Psalm 50:
Have mercy on me, God, in Your kindness.
In Your compassion blot out my offence.
O wash me more and more from my guilt
and cleanse me from my sin.

150

Sunday and Festal Matins

My offences truly I know them;
my sin is always before me.
Against You, You alone, have I sinned;
what is evil in Your sight I have done.
That You may be justified when You give sentence
and be without reproach when You judge
O see, in guilt I was born,
a sinner was I conceived.
Indeed You love truth in the heart;
then in the secret of my heart teach me wisdom
O sprinkle me with hyssop then I shall be clean;
O wash me, I shall be whiter than snow.
Make me hear rejoicing and gladness,
that the bones You have crushed may thrill.
From my sins turn away Your face
and blot out all my guilt.
A pure heart create for me, O God,
put a steadfast spirit within me.
Do not cast me away from Your presence,
nor deprive me of Your Holy Spirit.
Give me again the joy of Your help;
with a spirit of fervour sustain me,
That I may teach transgressors Your ways
and sinners may return to You.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

and my tongue shall ring out Your goodness.
O Lord, open my lips
and my mouth shall declare Your praise.

burnt offering from me You would refuse,
My sacrifice, a contrite spirit.
A humbled, contrite heart, O God, You will not spurn.
In Your goodness, O Lord, show favor to Zion:
Rebuild the walls of Jerusalem.
Then You will be pleased with lawful sacrifice,
(burnt offerings wholly consumed).
then You will be offered young bulls on Your altar.

The Canticle of the Theotokos
My soul magnifies the Lord, and my spirit rejoices in

More honorable than the cherubim, and beyond compare
more glorious than the seraphim; who, a virgin, gave birth to

for behold, from henceforth all generations shall call me
blessed.
Because He Who is mighty has done great things for me,
and holy is His Name, and His love is from generation to
generation to those who fear Him.

Sunday and Festal Matins

He has received Israel His servant, being mindful of His
love, as He spoke to our Fathers: to Abraham and to his seed
forever.

in the appointed Tone

Psalm 148

Verse: To You is due a hymn, O God!

He commanded: they were made.

gave a law which shall not pass away.

sea creatures and all oceans,

Sunday and Festal Matins

all mountains and hills,

The splendor of His name
reaches beyond heaven and earth.
He exalts the strength of His people.

of the sons of Israel,

His praise in the assembly of the faithful.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

To bind their kings in chains

and good will. We praise You, we bless You, we worship You,

For You alone are holy, You alone are Lord, Jesus Christ, to
the glory of God the Father. Amen.
I will bless You every day, and praise Your Name forever.
Make us worthy, O Lord, to be kept sinless this morning.
Blessed are You, O Lord, the God of our fathers, and praiseworthy and glorious is Your Name forever. Amen.
May Your mercy, O Lord, be upon us who have placed
our hope in You. Blessed are You, O Lord, teach me Your
commandments. Blessed are You, O Master, make me
understand Your commandments. Blessed are You, O Holy

Today salvation has come to the world. Let us sing to Him
Who is risen from the tomb, the Source of our life, Who has
crushed Death by death, and bestowed on us victory and great
mercy.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

THE ORDER OF THE HOURS
ORDER OF THE FIRST HOUR
Come, let us worship our King and God.
Come, let us worship Christ, our King and God.
Come, let us worship and bow before the only
Lord Jesus Christ, the King and our God.
Then, the psalms:

Psalm 5
To my words give ear, O Lord,
give heed to my groaning.
Attend to the sound of my cries,
my King and my God.
It is You Whom I invoke, O Lord.
In the morning You hear me;
in the morning I offer You my prayer,
watching and waiting.
You are no God Who loves evil;
no sinner is Your guest.
The boastful shall not stand their ground
before Your face.
181

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

You hate all who do evil;
You destroy all who lie.
The deceitful and bloodthirsty man
The Lord detests.
But I through the greatness of Your love
have access to Your house.
I bow down before Your holy temple,
filled with awe.
Lead me, Lord, in Your justice,
because of those who lie in wait;
make clear Your way before me.
No truth can be found in their mouths,
their heart is all mischief,
their throat a wide-open grave,
all honey their speech.
Declare them guilty, O God.
Let them fail in their designs.
Drive them out for their many offenses;
for they have defied You.
All those You protect shall be glad
and ring out their joy.
You shelter them; in You they rejoice,
those who love Your name.
It is You Who bless the just man, Lord;
You surround him with favor as with a shield.
182

Order of the First Hour

Psalm 89
O Lord, You have been our refuge
from one generation to the next.
Before the mountains were born
or the earth or the world brought forth,
You are God, without beginning or end.
You turn men back into dust
and say: ‘Go back, sons of men.’
To Your eyes a thousand years
are like yesterday, come and gone,
no more than a watch in the night.
You sweep men away like a dream,
like grass which springs up in the morning.
In the morning it springs up and flowers;
by evening it withers and fades.
So we are destroyed in Your anger
struck with terror in Your fury.
Our guilt lies open before You;
our secrets in the light of Your face.
All our days pass away in Your anger.
Our life is over like a sigh.
Our span is seventy years
or eighty for those who are strong.
And most of these are emptiness and pain.
They pass swiftly and we are gone.

183

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Who understands the power of Your anger
and fears the strength of Your fury?
Make us know the shortness of our life
that we may gain wisdom of heart.
Lord, relent! Is Your anger for ever?
Show pity to Your servants.
In the morning fill us with Your love;
we shall exult and rejoice all our days.
Give us joy to balance our affliction
for the years when we knew misfortune.
Show forth Your work to Your servants;
Let Your glory shine on their children.
Let the favor of the Lord be upon us:
Give success to the work of our hands.
Give success to the work of our hands.

Psalm 100
My song is of mercy and justice;
I sing to You, O Lord.
I will walk in the way of perfection.
O when, Lord, will You come?
I will walk with blameless heart
within my house;
I will not set before my eyes
whatever is base.
184

Order of the First Hour

I will hate the ways of the crooked;
they shall not be my friends.
The false-hearted must keep far away;
the wicked I disown.
The man who slanders his neighbor in secret
I will bring to silence.
The man of proud looks and haughty heart
I will never endure.
I look to the faithful in the land
That they may dwell with me.
He who walks in the way of perfection
shall be my friend.
No man who practices deceit
shall live within my house.
No man who utters lies shall stand
before my eyes.
Morning by morning I will silence
all the wicked in the land,
uprooting from the Lord’s city
all who do evil.
Glory: now and ever:
Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia. Glory to You, O God. Three
times. Three bows.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
185

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

the troparion of the day, or of the feast, or of the saint. Now

What shall we call you, O Full of Grace? A Heaven, for
you gave rise to the Sun of Justice? A Paradise, for you have
brought forth the Flower of incorruption? A Virgin, for you
have remained undefiled? A pure Mother, holding in her holy
arms the Son Who is the God of all? Intercede with Him for
the salvation of our souls.

and teach my heart, O Master. O Word of the Father, give me

But on Sunday we say the Hypakoj of the current tone.
Lord, have mercy. 40.
O good God, in all times and in all places You are
worshiped and glorified both in heaven and on earth. You
are long-suffering and most-merciful. You love the just and
show mercy to the sinner, calling all to salvation through the
promise of blessings to come. Do You, the same Lord, at this
hour receive our supplications and direct our lives in the path
of Your commandments. Sanctify our souls; purify our bodies;
set aright our minds; cleanse our thoughts; deliver us from all
affliction, evil and illness; surround us with Your holy angels
so that, guided and guarded in their camp, we may attain
oneness of faith and the knowledge of Your unapproachable
glory, for You are blessed forever and ever. Amen.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Glory: now and ever:
188

Order of the First Hour

More honorable than the cherubim, and beyond compare
more glorious than the seraphim; who, a virgin, gave birth to
God the Word, you, truly the Theotokos, we magnify.
Give the blessing, Father, in the Name of the Lord.
The priest:
[Numbers 6:24-26]
May God be merciful to us and bless us; may He cause
His countenance to shine upon us and have mercy on us.
We: Amen.
_________________________________________________
And if it is the Forty Day Fast, we make three great
prostrations, saying the prayer:
Lord and Master of my life, spare me from the spirit
of indifference, despair, lust for power, and idle chatter.
Prostration.
Instead, bestow on me, Your servant, the spirit of integrity,
humility, patience and love. Prostration.
Yes, O Lord and King, let me see my own sins, and not
judge my brothers and sisters, for You are blessed, forever and
ever. Amen. Prostration.
Then twelve small bows, saying at each bow:
O God, be merciful to me, a sinner.
O God, cleanse me of my sins and have mercy on me.
O Lord, forgive me for I have sinned without number.
189

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

And again, this prayer a final time:
Lord and Master of my life: to the end: forever and ever.
Amen. And one great prostration.
Then, Trisagion. Most Holy Trinity: Our Father: Lord,
have mercy. 12.
_________________________________________________
And the prayer:
O Christ the True Light, Who enlighten and sanctify
everyone who comes into the world, mark us with the light of
Your countenance so that we may see the unapproachable light.
Let our life be straight along the path of Your commandments,
through the prayers of Your most pure Mother and of all Your
saints. Amen.
The priest:
Glory to You, O Christ God, our hope, glory to You.
Choir: Glory: now and ever: Lord, have mercy. Three
times. Give the blessing.
The priest says the little dismissal:
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save us
through the prayers of His most pure Mother; of our venerable
and God-bearing fathers; and through the prayers of all the
saints; for Christ is good and loves mankind.
Choir: Amen.

190

ORDER OF THE THIRD HOUR
The priest:
Blessed is our God, always, now and ever and forever.
And we: Amen.
Glory to You, our God, glory to You!
Heavenly King, Comforter, Spirit of Truth, eerywhere
present and filling all things, Treasury of Blessings and Giver
of Life, come and dwell within us, cleanse us of all stain, and
save our souls, O gracious One.
Holy God, Holy and Mighty, Holy and Immortal, have
mercy on us. Three times.
Glory to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit,
now and ever and forever. Amen.
Most holy Trinity, have mercy on us; Lord, cleanse us of
our sins; Master, forgive our transgressions; Holy One, come
to us and heal our infirmities for Your Name’s sake.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Glory: now and ever:
191

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Our Father, Who art in heaven, hallowed be Thy Name.
Thy kingdom come, Thy will be done on earth as it is in
heaven. Give us this day our daily bread, and forgive us our
trespasses as we forgive those who trespass against us, and
lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil.
Priest: For Thine is the kingdom:
Then, Lord, have mercy. 12.
Glory: now and ever:
Come, let us worship our King and God.
Come, let us worship Christ, our King and God.
Come, let us worship and bow before the only
Lord Jesus Christ, the King and our God.
Then, the psalms:

Psalm 16
Lord, hear a cause that is just,
pay heed to my cry.
Turn Your ear to my prayer;
no deceit is on my lips.
From You may my judgment come forth.
Your eyes discern the truth.
You search my heart, You visit me by night.
You test me and You find in me no wrong.
My words are not sinful as are men’s words.
I kept from violence because of Your word,
I kept my feet firmly in Your paths;
there was no faltering in my steps.

192

Order of the Third Hour

I am here and I call, You will hear me, O God.
Turn Your ear to me; hear my words.
Display Your great love, You Whose right hand saves
Your friends from those who rebel against them.
Guard me as the apple of Your eye.
Hide me in the shadow of Your wings
from the violent attack of the wicked.
My foes encircle me with deadly intent.
Their hearts tight shut, their mouths speak proudly.
They advance against me, and now they surround me.
Their eyes are watching to strike me to the ground
as though they were lions ready to claw
or like some young lion crouched in hiding.
Lord, arise, confront them, strike them down!
Let Your sword rescue my soul from the wicked;
let Your hand, O Lord, rescue me from men,
from men whose reward is in this present life.
You give them their fill of Your treasures;
they rejoice in abundance of offspring
and leave their wealth to their children.
As for me, in my justice I shall see Your face
and be filled, when I awake, with the sight of Your glory.

193

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Psalm 24
To You, O Lord, I lift up my soul.
I trust You, let me not be disappointed,
do not let my enemies triumph.
Those who hope in You shall not be disappointed,
but only those who wantonly break faith.
Lord, make me know Your ways.
Lord, teach me Your paths.
Make me walk in Your truth, and teach me,
for You are God my Savior.
In You I hope all day long
because of Your goodness, O Lord.
Remember Your mercy, Lord,
and the love You have shown from of old.
Do not remember the sins of my youth.
In Your love remember me.
The Lord is good and upright.
He shows the path to those who stray,
He guides the humble in the right path;
He teaches His way to the poor.
His ways are faithfulness and love
for those who keep His covenant and will.
Lord, for the sake of Your name
forgive my guilt, for it is great.
If anyone fears the Lord
He will show him the path he should choose.
His soul shall live in happiness
194

Order of the Third Hour

and his children shall possess the land.
The Lord’s friendship is for those who revere Him;
to them He reveals His covenant.
My eyes are always on the Lord,
for He rescues my feet from the snare.
Turn to me and have mercy
for I am lonely and poor.
Relieve the anguish of my heart
and set me free from my distress.
See my affliction and my toil
and take all my sins away.
See how many are my foes,
how violent their hatred for me.
Preserve my life and rescue me.
Do not disappoint me, You are my refuge.
May innocence and uprightness protect me,
for my hope is in You, O Lord.
Redeem Israel, O God, from all its distress.

Psalm 50
Have mercy on me, God, in Your kindness.
In Your compassion blot out my offence.
O wash me more and more from my guilt
and cleanse me from my sin.
My offences truly I know them;
my sin is always before me.
Against You, You alone, have I sinned;
what is evil in Your sight I have done.
195

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

That You may be justified when You give sentence
and be without reproach when You judge
O see, in guilt I was born,
a sinner was I conceived.
Indeed You love truth in the heart;
then in the secret of my heart teach me wisdom
O sprinkle me with hyssop, then I shall be clean;
O wash me, I shall be whiter than snow.
Make me hear rejoicing and gladness,
that the bones You have crushed may thrill.
From my sins turn away Your face
and blot out all my guilt.
A pure heart create for me, O God,
put a steadfast spirit within me.
Do not cast me away from Your presence,
nor deprive me of Your Holy Spirit.
Give me again the joy of Your help;
with a spirit of fervour sustain me,
that I may teach transgressors Your ways
and sinners may return to You.
O rescue me, God, my helper,
and my tongue shall ring out Your goodness.
O Lord, open my lips
and my mouth shall declare Your praise.
For in sacrifice You take no delight,
burnt offering from me You would refuse,
196

Order of the Third Hour

my sacrifice, a contrite spirit.
A humbled, contrite heart, O God, You will not spurn.
In Your goodness, O Lord, show favor to Zion;
rebuild the walls of Jerusalem.
Then You will be pleased with lawful sacrifice,
(burnt offerings wholly consumed),
then You will be offered young bulls on Your altar.
Glory: now and ever:
Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia. Glory to You, O God. Three
times. Three bows.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
And if, indeed, God the Lord is sung, say: Glory, the
troparion of the day, or of the feast, or of the saint.
Now and ever:
O Theotokos, you are the True Vine who gave birth to the
Fruit of Life: wherefore, we implore you, O Lady, to intercede
together with the apostles and all the saints that we may obtain
mercy for our souls.
_________________________________________________
However, if it is [a period when] Alleluia [is sung],
say these troparia,
Tone 6:
O Lord, You sent down Your All-Holy Spirit on Your
apostles at the third hour. Do not take Him from us, O Good
One, but renew Him in us who pray to You. [Psalm 50: 13,12]
197

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Verse 1: A pure heart create for me, O God, put a steadfast

Verse 2: Do not cast me away from Your presence, nor

To each of these verses we sing in response:
At the third hour: the entire troparion to the end, and a
prostration after each one.
Then, Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
O Theotokos, you are the True Vine: and the rest.
_________________________________________________
[Psalm 67:20-21]
Blessed be the Lord God! May the Lord be blessed day
after day. He bears our burdens, God our Savior. This God of
ours is a God Who saves.
Trisagion. Most Holy Trinity: After Our Father:
The priest: For Thine is the kingdom:
The kontakion of the day, or of the saint, or of the feast.

Blessed are You, O Christ our God. You have shown the
fishermen to be all-wise, sending down upon them the Holy
Spirit. Through them You have caught the whole world in
Your net. O Lover of Mankind, glory to You!
198

Order of the Third Hour

Glory:
When the Most High descended and confused tongues,
He scattered nations. When He distributed the tongues of fire,
He called all to unity. We also, with one voice, glorify the
Most Holy Spirit.
Now and ever:
All-pure Theotokos, you are the hope, protection, and
refuge of Christians; the unassailable wall, the untroubled
harbor for the storm-tossed; but as you save the world by your
unceasing intercession, remember us also, all-praised Virgin.
_________________________________________________
Lord, have mercy. 40.
O good God, in all times and in all places You are
worshiped and glorified both in heaven and on earth. You
are long-suffering and most-merciful. You love the just and
show mercy to the sinner, calling all to salvation through the
promise of blessings to come. Do You, the same Lord, at this
hour receive our supplications and direct our lives in the path
of Your commandments. Sanctify our souls; purify our bodies;
set aright our minds; cleanse our thoughts; deliver us from all
affliction, evil and illness; surround us with Your holy angels
so that, guided and guarded in their camp, we may attain
oneness of faith and the knowledge of Your unapproachable
glory, for You are blessed forever and ever. Amen.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Glory: now and ever:

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

More honorable than the cherubim, and beyond compare

202

ORDER OF THE SIXTH HOUR
Come, let us worship our King and God.
Come, let us worship Christ, our King and God.
Come, let us worship and bow before the only
Lord Jesus Christ, the King and our God.

Psalm 53
O God, save me by Your name;
by Your power uphold my cause.
O God, hear my prayer;
listen to the words of my mouth.
For proud men have risen against me,
ruthless men seek my life.
They have no regard for God.
But I have God for my help.
The Lord upholds my life.
Let the evil recoil upon my foes;
You Who are faithful destroy them.
I will sacrifice to You with willing heart
and praise Your name for it is good;
for You have rescued me from all distress
and my eyes have seen the downfall of my foes.
203

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Psalm 54
O God, listen to my prayer,
do not hide from my pleading,
attend to me and reply;
with my cares I cannot rest.
I tremble at the shouts of the foe,
at the cries of the wicked;
for they bring down evil upon me.
They assail me with fury.
My heart is stricken within me,
death’s terror is on me,
trembling and fear fall upon me
and horror overwhelms me.
O that I had wings like a dove
to fly away and be at rest.
So I would escape far away
and take refuge in the desert.
I would hasten to find a shelter
from the raging wind,
from the destructive storm, O Lord,
and from their plotting tongues.
For I can see nothing but violence
and strife in the city.
Night and day they patrol
high on the city walls.

204

Order of the Sixth Hour

It is full of wickedness and evil;
it is full of sin.
Its streets are never free
from tyranny and deceit.
If this had been done by an enemy
I could bear his taunts.
If a rival had risen against me,
I could hide from him.
But it is You, my own companion,
my intimate friend!
(How close was the friendship between us)
We walked together in harmony
in the house of God.
May death fall suddenly upon them!
Let them go to Hades alive,
for wickedness dwells in their homes
and deep in their hearts.
As for me, I will cry to God
and the Lord will save me.
Evening, morning, and at noon
I will cry and lament.
He will deliver my soul in peace
in the attack against me:
for those who fight me are many,
but He hears my voice.

205

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

God will hear and will humble them,
the eternal judge:
for they will not amend their ways.
They have no fear of God.
The traitor has turned against his friends;
he has broken his word.
His speech is softer than butter,
but war is in his heart.
His words are smoother than oil,
but they are naked swords.
Entrust your cares to the Lord
and He will support you.
He will never allow
the just man to stumble.
But You, O God, will bring them down
to the pit of death.
Deceitful and bloodthirsty men
shall not live half their days.
O Lord, I will trust in You.

Psalm 90
He who dwells in the shelter of the Most High
and abides in the shade of the Almighty
says to the Lord: ‘My refuge,
my stronghold, my God in Whom I trust!’

206

Order of the Sixth Hour

It is He Who will free you from the snare
of the fowler who seeks to destroy you;
He will conceal you with His pinions
and under His wings you will find refuge.
You will not fear the terror of the night
nor the arrow that flies by day,
nor the plague that prowls in the darkness
nor the scourge that lays waste at noon.
A thousand may fall at your side,
ten thousand at your right,
you, it will never approach;
His faithfulness is buckler and shield.
Your eyes have only to look
to see how the wicked are repaid,
you who have said: ‘Lord, my refuge!’
and have made the Most High your dwelling.
Upon you no evil shall fall,
no plague approach where you dwell.
For you has He commanded His angels,
to keep you in all your ways.
They shall bear you upon their hands
lest you strike your foot against a stone.
On the lion and the viper you will tread
and trample the young lion and the dragon.

207

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Since he clings to me in love, I will free him;
protect him for he knows My name.
When he calls I shall answer: ‘I am with you.’
I will save him from distress and give him glory.
With length of days I will content him;
I shall let him see My saving power.
Glory: now and ever:
Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia. Glory to You, O God. Three
times. Three bows.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
And if, indeed, God the Lord is sung, we say: Glory, the
troparion of the day, or of the feast, or of the saint.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Since we have no one in whom to confide because of our
many sins, O Virgin Theotokos, intercede for us with the One
Who was born of you, for a mother’s prayer is a powerful
means for obtaining the Master’s favor. You are most worthy
of veneration, so do not turn away from the pleading of us
sinners; for the One Who willed to suffer in the flesh for our
sake is full of mercy, and His power is sufficient to save us.
_________________________________________________
However, if it is [a period when] Alleluia [is sung] we say
the appointed troparion in Tone 2:
On the sixth day and at the sixth hour You nailed to the
cross the sin that Adam dared to commit in Paradise. Also tear
208

Order of the Sixth Hour

up the written charges of our transgressions, O Christ God,
and save us.
Verse 1: O God, listen to my prayer, do not hide from my
pleading. [Psalm 54:2]
Verse 2: I will cry to God, and the Lord will save me.
[Psalm 54:17]
To each of these verses we sing in response: O Lord, on
the sixth day: the entire troparion to the end, and a prostration
after each one.
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
Since we have no one:
If it is the Forty Day Fast, the troparion of the prophecy,
the prokeimenon, and the paremia are read here.
_________________________________________________
[Psalm 78:8-9]
May Your compassion quickly come to us, for we are
brought very low. Help us, O God, our Savior, because of the
glory of Your Name. Deliver us, O Lord, and cleanse our sins
for Your Name’s sake.
Trisagion. Most Holy Trinity: After: Our Father:
The priest: For Thine is the kingdom:
The kontakion of the day, or of the feast,
or of the saint.

209

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

_________________________________________________
However, if it is the Fast, or if there is no kontakion, we
say these troparia, Tone 2:
O Christ God, You brought about salvation in the middle
of the earth. You stretched out Your all-pure hands on the cross
in order to gather together all the nations, who cry aloud: O
Lord, glory to You!
Glory:
We bow before Your sacred image, O gracious Lord, and
beg forgiveness for our offenses, O Christ our God; for You,
of Your own good will, ascended the cross in Your human
nature to deliver from the enemy’s bondage those whom You
created. Therefore we gratefully cry out to You: By Your
coming to save the world, O Savior, You have filled all with
joy.
Now and ever:
Theotokos, fount of mercy, deem us worthy of compassion.
Look upon a sinful people and as always show your power;
for, placing our trust in you, we cry out to you “Rejoice,” as
once did Gabriel, the commander of angels.
This is said on Monday, on Tuesday, and on Thursday.
But on Wednesday and Friday, instead of: Theotokos,
fount of mercy: this is said:

210

Order of the Sixth Hour

Stavrotheotokion, Tone 2:
You are most-glorious, O Virgin Theotokos, and we sing

made worthy of life, receiving paradise, the ancient delight.
Therefore, giving thanks, we glorify the powerful Christ our
God, and only all-merciful One.

212

Order of the Sixth Hour

After that, this prayer:
[Prayer to God the Father
by Saint Basil the Great]
God and Lord of Powers and Maker of all creation,
through Your compassion beyond our understanding, You
sent down Your only-begotten Son, our Lord Jesus Christ,
for the salvation of our race. Through His honorable cross
He tore apart the written list of our sins and triumphed
over the powers and masters of darkness. Now, O Master
Who love mankind, accept from us sinners these prayers of
thanksgiving and petition, and preserve us from any deadly
fall in the darkness and against every visible and invisible
enemy who may seek our harm. Pierce our bodies with fear
of You, and let not our souls fall into evil words or thoughts,
but, instead, wound them with love for You so that, looking
upon You at all times and guided by the light that emanates
from You, we may contemplate the unapproachable eternal
light. May we ever address our profession and thanksgiving to
You, O eternal Father, with Your only-begotten Son, and Your
all-holy, and good, and life-creating Spirit, now and ever and
forever. Amen.
And if, indeed, God the Lord: is sung, we say the Typical
Psalms here.
However, if Alleluia, say it after the Ninth Hour.
But, when the Ninth Hour follows the Sixth it is begun
like this: Holy God: After Our Father: Lord, have mercy, 12.
Glory: now and ever: Come, let us worship: Three times. And
the psalms, and the rest.
213

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

214

ORDER OF THE NINTH HOUR
After Blessed is our God:
Glory to You, our God, glory to You! Heavenly King:
Trisagion. Most Holy Trinity: Our Father:
Priest: For Thine is the kingdom: Lord, have mercy. 12.
Glory: now and ever:
Come, let us worship: Three times.
Then, the psalms:

Psalm 83
How lovely is Your dwelling place,
Lord, God of hosts.
My soul is longing and yearning,
is yearning for the courts of the Lord.
My heart and my soul ring out their joy
to God, the living God.
The sparrow herself finds a home
and the swallow a nest for her brood;
she lays her young by Your altars,
Lord of hosts, my king and my God.
215

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

They are happy who dwell in Your house,
for ever singing Your praise.
They are happy, whose strength is in You,
in whose hearts are the roads to Zion.
As they go through the Bitter Valley
they make it a place of springs
(The autumn rain covers it with blessings).
They walk with ever growing strength,
they will see the God of gods in Zion.
O Lord God of hosts, hear my prayer,
give ear, O God of Jacob.
Turn Your eyes, O God, our shield,
look on the face of Your anointed.
One day within Your courts
is better than a thousand elsewhere.
The threshold of the house of God
I prefer to the dwellings of the wicked.
For the Lord God is a rampart, a shield;
He will give us His favor and glory.
The Lord will not refuse any good
to those who walk without blame.
Lord, God of hosts,
happy the man who trusts in You!

216

Order of the Ninth Hour

Psalm 84
O Lord, You once favored Your land
and revived the fortunes of Jacob,
You forgave the guilt of Your people
and covered all their sins.
You averted all Your rage,
You calmed the heat of Your anger.
Revive us now, God, our helper!
Put an end to Your grievance against us.
Will You be angry with us for ever,
will Your anger never cease?
Will You not restore again our life
that Your people may rejoice in You?
Let us see, O Lord, Your mercy
and give us Your saving help.
I will hear what the Lord God has to say,
a voice that speaks of peace,
peace for His people and His friends
and those who turn to Him in their hearts.
His help is near for those who fear Him
and His glory will dwell in our land.
Mercy and faithfulness have met;
justice and peace have embraced.
faithfulness shall spring from the earth
and justice look down from heaven.

217

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

The Lord will make us prosper
and our earth shall yield its fruit.
Justice shall march before Him
and peace shall follow His steps.

Psalm 85
Turn Your ear, O Lord, and give answer
for I am poor and needy.
Preserve my life, for I am faithful;
save the servant who trusts in You.
You are my God, have mercy on me, Lord,
for I cry to You all the day long.
Give joy to Your servant, O Lord,
for to You I lift up my soul.
O Lord, You are good and forgiving,
full of love to all who call.
Give heed, O Lord, to my prayer
and attend to the sound of my voice.
In the day of distress I will call
and surely You will reply.
Among the gods there is none like You, O Lord,
nor work to compare with Yours.
All the nations shall come to adore You
and glorify Your name, O Lord,
for You are great and do marvelous deeds,
You Who alone are God.

218

Order of the Ninth Hour

Show me, Lord, Your way
so that I may walk in Your truth.
Guide my heart to fear Your name.
I will praise You, Lord my God, with all my heart
and glorify Your name for ever;
for Your love to me has been great.
You have saved me from the depths of the grave.
The proud have risen against me;
ruthless men seek my life,
to You they pay no heed.
But You, God of mercy and compassion,
slow to anger, O Lord,
abounding in love and truth,
turn and take pity on me.
O give Your strength to Your servant
and save Your handmaid’s son.
Show me a sign of Your favor
that my foes may see to their shame
that You console me and give me Your help.
And again:
Show me a sign of Your favor
that my foes may see to their shame
that You console me and give me Your help.
Glory: now and ever:
Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia. Glory to You, O God. Three
times. Three bows.
219

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Lord, have mercy. Three times.
And if, indeed, God the Lord is sung, say: Glory, the
troparion of the day, or of the feast, or of the saint.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
For our sake You were born of the Virgin, and You
suffered crucifixion, O Good One. You conquered death by
death, and through Your resurrection You revealed Yourself as
God. Do not disdain those whom You have created with Your
own hands, but show forth Your love for mankind, O Merciful
One. Accept the intercession which the Theotokos makes in
our behalf. O our Savior, save a despairing people.
_________________________________________________
However, if it is [a period when] Alleluia [is sung], this
appointed troparion, in Tone 8:
O Christ God, Who at the ninth hour tasted death in the
flesh for our sakes, slay the desires of the flesh and save us.
Verse 1: Lord, let my cry come before You: teach me by
Your word. [Psalm 118:169]
Verse 2: Let my pleading come before You: save me by
Your promise. [Psalm 118:170]
To each of these verses we sing in response: O Christ
God, Who at the ninth hour: the entire troparion to the end,
and a prostration after each one.

[Daniel 3:34-35]

_________________________________________________
However, if it is the Fast, we say these, Tone 8:
Seeing the Author of life hanging on the cross, the Good
Thief cried out with his act of faith. If the One crucified with
us were not God in the flesh, the sun would not have hidden
its rays, nor would the earth have trembled with fear. And
You patiently bear all this; remember me, O Lord, in Your
kingdom.
Glory:
Between two thieves Your cross became the scales of
justice, for one was dragged down to hell by the weight of his
blasphemy, but the other, lightened of his faults, was raised to
the knowledge of the things of God. O Christ God, glory to
You.
Now and ever:
221

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Seeing the Lamb and Shepherd and Savior of the world
on the cross, she who bore Him said weeping: The world
rejoices, for it receives redemption; but my inner being burns
as I see Your crucifixion which You endured for all, O my Son
and my God.
_________________________________________________
Lord, have mercy. 40.
O good God, in all times and in all places You are
worshiped and glorified both in heaven and on earth. You
are long-suffering and most-merciful. You love the just and
show mercy to the sinner, calling all to salvation through the
promise of blessings to come. Do You, the same Lord, at this
hour receive our supplications and direct our lives in the path
of Your commandments. Sanctify our souls; purify our bodies;
set aright our minds; cleanse our thoughts; deliver us from all
affliction, evil and illness; surround us with Your holy angels
so that, guided and guarded in their camp, we may attain
oneness of faith and the knowledge of Your unapproachable
glory, for You are blessed forever and ever. Amen.
Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Glory: now and ever:
More honorable than the cherubim, and beyond compare
more glorious than the seraphim; who, a virgin, gave birth to
God the Word, you, truly the Theotokos, we magnify.
Give the blessing, Father, in the Name of the Lord.

222

Order of the Ninth Hour

The priest:
[Numbers 6:24-26]
May God be merciful to us and bless us; may He cause
His countenance to shine upon us and have mercy on us.
We: Amen.
_________________________________________________
And if it is the Fast and Alleluia was sung, we make three
great prostrations, saying the prayer:
Lord and Master of my life, spare me from the spirit of
indifference, despair, lust for power, and idle chatter.
Prostration.
Instead, bestow on me, Your servant, the spirit of integrity,
humility, patience and love. Prostration.
Yes, O Lord and King, let me see my own sins, and not
judge my brothers and sisters, for You are blessed, forever and
ever. Amen. Prostration.
Then twelve small bows, saying at each bow:
O God, be merciful to me, a sinner.
O God, cleanse me of my sins and have mercy on me.
O Lord, forgive me for I have sinned without number.
And again, this prayer a final time:
Lord and Master of my life: to the end: forever and ever.
Amen. And one great prostration.

223

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then, Trisagion. Most Holy Trinity: Our Father: Lord,
have mercy. 12.
_________________________________________________
After that, this prayer of Saint Basil the Great:
O Master Lord Jesus Christ our God, You patiently
endured our sins and led us to this hour at which You were
hung upon the life-giving wood. You opened a way to
paradise for the penitent thief and crushed death by Your
death. Now forgive the trespasses that we Your servants have
committed, unworthy sinners that we are. We have sinned
indeed and transgressed Your law. We are unworthy even to
lift up our eyes to heaven, for we have abandoned the path of
Your holiness and pursued the desires of our hearts. But now
we implore Your immense goodness: spare us, O Lord, in the
multitude of Your mercies; save us for the sake of Your most
holy Name. Our days were spent in vanity; rescue us from the
hands of our enemy, and forgive our sins. Subdue in us the
cravings of our flesh, so that, after putting off the old self, we
may put on the new and live for You, our Lord and benefactor;
and that, obeying Your commandments, we may reach eternal
repose in the place where all the blessed abide, for You are the
true joy and delight of those who love You, O Christ our God.
We send up glory to You, and to Your eternal Father, and to
Your all-holy, good, and life-creating Spirit, now and ever and
forever. Amen.
Glory: now and ever: Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Give the blessing. And the dismissal.
