337

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then: Lord, have mercy. 12.
And these prayers in order with understanding and
contrition.

The First Prayer,
of Saint Macarius the Great, to God the Father
O eternal God and Ruler of all creation, You have allowed
me to reach this hour. Forgive the sins I committed today by
word, deed, or in thought. Purify me, O Lord, from every
spiritual and physical stain. Grant me, Lord, to pass the
sleep of this night in peace. Grant that I may rise from this
lowly bed to glorify You by my deeds throughout my entire
lifetime, and that I may be victorious over every spiritual and
physical enemy. Deliver me, O Lord, from all vain thoughts
and evil desires, for Yours, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, are
the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, now and ever and
forever. Amen.

The Second Prayer,
to our Lord Jesus Christ, of Saint Antiochus
O Almighty Word of the Father, Jesus Christ, Who alone
are perfect: according to the greatness of Your mercy, do not
abandon me, Your servant, but ever rest in my heart. O Jesus,
Good Shepherd of Your sheep, deliver me from the attacks
of the devil. Do not allow me to become the prey of Satan’s
evil intention, even though I have within me the seeds of
eternal damnation. Instead, O Jesus Christ, Lord God, holy
King Who alone are worshiped, while I sleep protect me by
Your Unwaning Light, the Holy Spirit, through Whom You
sanctified Your disciples. O Lord, grant salvation to me, Your
338

Prayers Before Sleep

unworthy servant, as I lie in my bed. Enlighten my mind by
the light of understanding of Your holy Gospel, my soul by the
love of Your cross, my heart by the purity of Your teaching.
Protect my body by Your sacred passion, my senses by Your
humility, and awaken me in due time for Your glorification.
For You, above all, are glorified with Your eternal Father, and
Your most Holy Spirit, forever. Amen.

The Third Prayer,
to the Most Holy Spirit
O Lord, heavenly King, Comforter, Spirit of Truth,
have compassion and mercy on me, Your unworthy servant.
Forgive me, unworthy as I am, and remit whatever sins I have
committed today both through human frailty and through
acting less than human. Forgive my voluntary and involuntary
sins, those committed knowingly or through ignorance—
which are from my youth and the knowledge of evil—and
those which have arisen from arrogance and despondency.
Forgive me if I have reproached or cursed someone in my
anger, or if I have afflicted grief or have become angry for
some reason. Forgive me if I have lied, or unsuitably slept,
or turned away a poor person who came to me. Forgive me
if I have caused grief for my brother or sister, or judged, or
condemned someone. Forgive me if, while at prayer, my mind
wandered on the glamorous things of this world, or if I thought
about depraved things. Forgive me if I was guilty of acting
foolishly, thought evil, or desired in my heart the property of
another. Forgive me if I have said indecent things or laughed
at the sin of my brother or sister without discerning my own
sins, which are great in number. Forgive me if I have been
neglectful in my prayers, or guilty of some evil action which
I cannot now recall, for I have committed these sins and even
339

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

much greater sins. Have mercy on me, Your dejected and
unworthy servant, O my Master and Creator. Remit, pardon,
and forgive me, for You are good and the Lover of Mankind.
May I, who am dissolute, sinful, and cursed, lie down in peace
to sleep and rest, and I will worship, praise, and glorify Your
most honorable Name with the Father and His only-begotten
Son, now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Fourth Prayer,
of Saint Macarius the Great
What shall I offer to You, or what shall I give to You, O
great Gift-giver, Immortal King, Lord and Lover of Mankind?
Though I was lazy in pleasing You and did nothing good, You
brought me to the end of this day which has passed, effecting
the conversion and salvation of my soul. Be merciful to me,
a sinner and one who is empty of any good deed. Raise up
my fallen soul which has been stained by immeasurable sins.
Take away from me every thought which is wicked in this
life, O sinless One. You alone can forgive my sins which I
have committed against You today, either knowingly or
unknowingly, by word, deed, or thought and with all of my
senses. You alone are my protection. Through Your divine
authority, Your inexpressible love for mankind, and Your
strength, preserve me from every evil circumstance. O God,
cleanse the multitude of my sins. O Lord, grant that I may be
delivered from the snare of the evil one. Save my suffering
soul and illuminate me with the light of Your countenance
when You will come in glory. Now grant that I may fall into a
sleep which is without condemnation and without disturbing
dreams. Keep the mind of Your servant undisturbed, dispelling
from me every satanic action. Enlighten the eyes of my mind
and heart so that I will not fall into a sleep of death. Send me
an angel of peace, a guardian and guide of my soul and body
340

Prayers Before Sleep

that he may deliver me from my enemies, that when I arise
from my bed, I may bring to You prayers of thanksgiving.
Hear me, O Lord, Your sinful and poor servant, made so by my
will and conscience. Grant that when I arise I may meditate
on Your words, and that by Your angels I may drive far from
me all demonic despondency, so that I may glorify and praise
the most holy Theotokos, Mary, whom You gave to us sinners
as an intercessor. For we know that she imitates Your love
for mankind and does not cease to pray for us. Through her
intercession, through the sign of the honorable cross, and for
the sake of all the saints, keep my soul, O Lord Jesus Christ
our God, for You are holy and most glorified forever. Amen.

The Fifth Prayer
O Lord, our God, since You are good and a Lover of
Mankind, forgive the sins which I have committed today by
word, deed, and thought. Give me a peaceful and undisturbed
sleep. Send Your guardian angel to protect and keep me from
all evil. For You are the guardian of our souls and bodies, and
we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and
ever and forever. Amen.

The Sixth Prayer
O Lord, our God, in Whom we believe and Whose Name
we call upon above every other name, grant us, who are about
to sleep, rest of soul and body. Keep us from every disturbance
and dark sensuality. Calm the striving of the passions and
extinguish physical excitements that arise. Grant that we may
lead a chaste life by words and deeds, and upon living a life
of good deeds, we may not fall away from Your promised
blessings, for You are blessed forever. Amen.
341

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

The Seventh Prayer,
to the Most Holy Theotokos,
of Peter the Studite Monk
I, an accursed person, prostrate myself before you, O most
pure Mother of God, and I pray: “O Queen, you know that I
sin unceasingly and anger your Son and my God.” As many
times as I repent in trembling, wondering if the Lord will
not destroy me, yet after a while, I still do the same things.
Seeing this, my Queen, O Theotokos, I pray: have mercy on
me, strengthen me, and give me a sense of doing good. O
my Lady, Theotokos, you know that I despise my evil actions
and that I love the law of God with my whole mind. I do not
understand the origin of that which I hate, O most pure Lady. I
also love, yet transgress, that which is good. O most pure one,
do not permit me to do my will for that is not good, but rather
let the will of your Son and my God be done, so that He might
save, instruct, and grant me the grace of the Holy Spirit. Thus
from now on, I may cease to do acts of uncleanliness to my
soul, and that I may live the rest of my life according to the
commands of your Son. To Him belong all glory, honor, and
might, with His eternal Father, and His most holy, good, and
life-giving Spirit, now and ever and forever. Amen.

The Eighth Prayer,
to the Most Holy Theotokos
O good Mother of the good King, O most pure and blessed
Theotokos, Mary, pour upon my suffering soul the mercy of
your Son and our God. By your prayers guide me to do good
deeds. Grant that I may spend the rest of my life without fault
and attain paradise through you, O Virgin Theotokos; for you
alone are pure and blessed.
342

Prayers Before Sleep

The Ninth Prayer, to the Holy Guardian Angel
O Guardian Angel, protector of my soul and body, to
your care I have been entrusted by Christ. Obtain for me the
forgiveness of the sins committed by me this day. Protect me
from the snares of my enemy that I may never more offend
God by my sin. Pray for me, your sinful and unworthy servant,
that through your help I may become worthy of the grace and
mercy of the most Holy Trinity, and of the Mother of my Lord
God, Jesus Christ, and of all the saints. Amen.
Then, the Kontakion of the Theotokos:
We are yours, O Theotokos. Since you have delivered
us from all tribulations, we give thanks to you by dedicating
our songs of victory to you, O Saving Champion. In your
invincible might, deliver us from all dangers that we may
exclaim to you: Rejoice, full of grace!
Then:
O most glorious, Ever-Virgin Mother of Christ, our God,
offer up our prayers to your Son and our God, so that, through
you He may save our souls.
I place all my hope in you, Mother of God. Protect me
under your patronage.
O Virgin Theotokos, do not turn away from me, a sinner,
for I need your help and intercession. Have mercy on me, for
my soul hopes in you.
Then, the Prayer of Saint Joannicius
The Father is my hope; the Son is my refuge; and the Holy
Spirit is my protection. O Holy Trinity, glory to You!

343

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then: It is truly proper: Glory: now and ever: Lord, have
mercy, Three times. Give the blessing. And the Dismissal:
May the Lord Jesus Christ, Son of God, through the
prayers of Your most pure Mother, of our venerable and Godbearing fathers, and of all the saints, save me, a sinner. Amen.

Prayer of Saint John Damascene
which is to be said while pointing to your bed:
O Master, Lover of Mankind, is this bed to be my grave,
or will You enlighten my wretched soul with another day?
Behold, the grave lies before me; behold, death confronts
me. I fear, O Lord, Your judgment and the endless torments,
yet I do not cease to do evil. My Lord God, I continually
anger You, and Your most pure Mother, and all the heavenly
hosts, and my holy guardian angel. I know, O Lord, that I am
unworthy of Your love for mankind, but am worthy of every
condemnation and torment. But, O Lord, whether I will it or
do not will it, save me. For to save a righteous one is no great
thing, and to have mercy on the pure is nothing wonderful, for
they are worthy of Your mercy. But on me, a sinner, show the
wonder of Your mercy; in this reveal Your love for mankind
lest my wickedness overcome Your ineffable goodness and
merciful kindness, and order my life as You wish.
And when about to lie down in bed,
this:
[Ps. 12: 4, 5] Give light to my eyes, O Christ God, lest I
fall asleep in death, lest my enemies say: “I have overcome
him.”

344

Prayers Before Sleep

Glory:
O God, be the defender of my soul, for I walk through the
midst of many enemies. Deliver me from them, and save me,
O Blessed One, for You love mankind.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Let us with our hearts and lips unceasingly extol the most
glorious Mother of God, holier than the holy angels, and
proclaim that she is truly the Theotokos for she has truly given
birth to God in the flesh and never ceases to intercede for our
souls.
Then kiss your cross, and make the sign of the cross [with
your cross] from the head to the foot of your bed, and likewise
from side to side, saying the Prayer of the Precious Cross:
Let God arise, and let His enemies be scattered, and let
those who hate Him flee from before His face. As smoke
vanishes, so let them vanish as wax melts before the fire. So
let the demons perish in the presence of those who love God
and who sign themselves with the sign of the cross and say
in gladness: Rejoice, most precious and life-creating cross of
the Lord, for you drive away the demons by the power of our
Lord Jesus Christ Who was crucified on you, Who descended
to Hades and trampled on the power of the devil, and gave
us you, His precious cross, for the driving away of every
adversary. O most precious and life-creating cross of the
Lord, help me, together with the holy Lady Virgin Theotokos
and with all the saints, forever. Amen.

345

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Before even lying down on your bed, go through all these
in your thoughts and memory.
Firstly, thus:
Give thanks to Almighty God for having given to you,
during the past day, by His grace, to live and to abide in health.
Secondly:
Lay before yourself your words, and make an examination
of your conscience, a thorough and detailed review of all the
hours of the day, beginning from the time when you arose
from your bed, and call to mind: where you went, what you
did: with whom, and on what, did you converse; and all your
deeds, words, and thoughts from morning until evening recite
to yourself, with all fear remembering and examining.
Thirdly:
If you have done any good this day, this has not happened
of you, but of the same God Who gives all good things to us
who fear Him, to Whom be praise and thanksgiving, and pray
that He confirm you in this good and enable you to accomplish
other good things.
Fourthly:
But if you have done anything evil, of yourself and from
your own weakness or from evil habits and arbitrariness which
result in speech, repent and pray to the Lover of Mankind, that
He may will to grant you forgiveness, and with a firm promise
never to do this evil again.

346

Prayers Before Sleep

Fifthly:
With tears implore your gracious Creator to grant that
the present night be quiet, undisturbed, pure, and sinless;
to grant that the coming day may be devoted entirely to the
glorification of His holy Name.
Finally:
If you find a soft pillow, forsake it, and put a stone in its
place for Christ’s sake; if you sleep in winter, bear it patiently,
saying: some did not sleep at all.
Refer: Patericon, Sermon IV.
Then, make the sign of the cross, and with prayer go to
sleep, thinking of the Day of Judgment and of how you shall
have to stand before God.

Psalm 142
Lord, listen to my prayer:
turn your ear to my appeal.
You are faithful, you are just; give answer.
Do not call Your servant to judgment.
For no one is just in your sight.
The enemy pursues my soul;
he has crushed my life to the ground;
he has made me dwell in darkness
like the dead, long forgotten.
Therefore, my spirit fails;
my heart is numb within me.
I remember the days that are past:
I ponder all your works.
I muse on what your hand has wrought
and to you I stretch out my hands.
351

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Like a parched land my soul thirsts for you.
Lord, make haste and answer;
for my spirit fails within me.
Do not hide your face
lest I become like those in the grave.
In the morning let me know your love
for I put my trust in you.
Make me know the way I should walk:
to you I lift up my soul.
Rescue me, Lord, from my enemies;
I have fled to you for refuge.
Teach me to do your will
for you, O Lord, are my God.
Let your good spirit guide me
in ways that are level and smooth.
For your name’s sake, Lord, save my life;
in your justice save my soul from distress.
In your love make an end of my foes;
destroy all those who oppress me
for I am your servant, O Lord.

Canon of Prayer to the Most Holy Theotokos

From many of my sins my body is weak, and my soul is
weak; I run to you, O Most Gracious, O hope of the hopeless,
help me.
O Lady and Mother of the Redeemer, accept the prayer
of your unworthy servants and intercede with Him, Who was
born from you; O Queen of the universe, be our mediatrix.
Let us diligently sing to you a song now, to the all-chanted
Theotokos, with joy: pray with the Forerunner and all the
saints, O Lady, to our Savior, that He may have mercy on us.
All angelic powers, Forerunner of the Lord, Twelve
Apostles and all saints with the Theotokos offer prayers to the
Savior to save us.
Then: Trisagion: Most Holy Trinity: Our Father:
Priest: For Thine is the kingdom:
And these troparia, Tone 6:
Have mercy on us, O Lord, have mercy on us: since we
have no defense, we sinners offer this supplication to You, our
Master; have mercy on us.
Glory:
Lord, have mercy on us, for in You we place our hope.
Be not exceedingly angry with us, nor mindful of our
transgressions, but look upon us even now with mercy, and
deliver us from our enemies. For You are our God and we are
Your people: we all are the work of Your hands, and we call
upon Your Name.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Now and ever:
Open unto us the doors of mercy, O blessed Theotokos.

of all Christians.
After this, the ektenia:
Have mercy on us, O God, according to Your great mercy,
we pray You, hear and have mercy.
Choir: Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Again we pray to the Lord our God, that He may hear the
prayer of us sinners, and have mercy on His servants (Name),
and protect them from every trial and distress, trouble and
sorrow, and from every spiritual and physical pain, bestowing
on them health and a long life; we all pray: quickly hear us
and have mercy.
Choir: Lord, have mercy. Three times.
Again, let us pray that He preserve this city (or this
village) and this holy church (although if at a monastery:
this holy monastery) and every city, town, and community
from famine, plague, earthquake, flood, fire, civil war, riot,
and foreign invasion; and that our God Who is kindly and the
Lover of Mankind may forgive our sins and hold back His just
wrath, and that He may have mercy on us.
Choir: Lord, have mercy. 12.
Again we pray that the Lord our God may hear the prayer
of us sinners, and have mercy on us.
Choir: Lord, have mercy. Three times.

Canon of Prayer to the Most Holy Theotokos

The priest exclaims:
Hear us, O God our Savior, Hope of all the ends of the

and ever and forever.
Choir: Amen.
The deacon, or the priest:
In humility, bending our necks (and our knees), let us pray
to the Lord.
Choir: Lord, have mercy.

Prayer to the Mother of God
O our most gracious Queen, O Theotokos, our hope,
friend of orphans, defender of strangers, joy of those in
sorrow, protection of those treated unjustly, look upon our
troubles, look upon our grief, help us in our weakness, guide
us who are strangers; you know our offenses, free us from
them as you wish, for we have no other help but you, no other
defender, no good consoler except you, O Mother of God, for
you guard and protect us forever.
Choir: Amen.
Priest: Wisdom.
Choir: More honorable:
Priest: Glory to You, O Christ God:
Choir: Glory: now and ever: Lord, have mercy. Three
times. Give the blessing.

of my soul as I sing:
O Jesus, my King most powerful!
O Jesus, my God Almighty!
O Jesus, my Immortal Master!
O Jesus, my Creator most glorious!
O Jesus, my most kind Teacher and Guide!
O Jesus, my most Gentle Pastor!
O Jesus, my Lord most compassionate!
O Jesus, my Savior most merciful!
O Jesus, enlighten my senses darkened by passions!
O Jesus, heal my body scabbed with sins!
O Jesus, cleanse my mind from vain thoughts!
O Jesus, keep my heart from evil desires!
O Jesus, Son of God, have mercy on me!

Kontakion Twelve:
Grant me Your grace, O Jesus, Absolver of all debts, and
receive me who repent, as You received Peter who denied
You, and call me who am downcast, as You earlier called Paul
who persecuted You, and hear me crying to You: Alleluia!

Ikos Twelve:
Singing of Your Incarnation, we all praise You and
believe like Thomas that, sitting together with the Father, You
are Lord and God, and the Judge of the Living and the Dead.
389

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Allow me to stand at Your right hand and sing:
O Jesus, my Eternal King, have mercy on me!
O Jesus, Aroma of Flowers, shed Your perfume on me.
O Jesus, warming Love, enkindle me!
O Jesus, eternal Temple, shelter me.
O Jesus, Cloak of Light, cover me!
O Jesus, Brilliant Pearl, shine upon me!
O Jesus, Precious Stone, illumine me!
O Jesus, Sun of Holiness, illumine me!
O Jesus, Joyful Light, inspire me!
O Jesus, deliver me from all bodily and spiritual ills!
O Jesus, spare me from falling into the hands of evildoers!
O Jesus, free me from eternal fire and torment!
O Jesus, Son of God, have mercy on me!

Kontakion Thirteen:
O most sweet and most generous Jesus! Receive this our
humble prayer, as You received the widow’s mite and keep
Your faithful people from all enemies, visible and invisible,
from foreign invasion, from disease and hunger, from all
tribulations and mortal wounds, and deliver from future
torments all who cry to You: Alleluia!
This Kontakion is said three times.
And again read the First Ikos:
Creator of Angels and Lord of Angelic Hosts: as You
once opened the ears of the deaf and the mouths of the dumb,
empower my dull mind and tongue to sing to You:

Akathist Hymn To Our Sweetest Lord Jesus Christ

O Jesus, most wonderful, the Astonishment of Angels!
O Jesus, most powerful, the Deliverer of our Forefathers!
O Jesus, most delightful, the Exaltation of Patriarchs!
O Jesus, most glorious, the Stronghold of Kings!
O Jesus, most beloved, the Fulfillment of Prophets!
O Jesus, most marvelous, the Strength of Martyrs!
O Jesus, most peaceful, the Joy of Monks!
O Jesus, most gracious, the Delight of Priests!
O Jesus, most merciful, the Abstinence of Pastors!
O Jesus, most tender, the Happiness of Saints!
O Jesus, most honorable, the Chastity of the Chaste!
O Jesus, Everlasting Salvation of Sinners!
O Jesus, Son of God, have mercy on me!
And again the First Kontakion:
Unconquered King and Lord, Vanquisher of the Nether
World, I, Your creature and servant, sing Your praise for
having delivered me from eternal death. Since Your mercies
are boundless, free me from every harm as I sing: O Jesus,
Son of God, have mercy on me!

Ode 7.
Irmos. When the golden idol was worshiped on the Plain
of Dura, the three youths ignored the command to sin. Cast
into the very center of a furnace, they were showered with
dew. They sang: Blessed are You, O God of our fathers.
O Christ Jesus, no one on earth in any age has sinned as I
have sinned, O my Jesus. Therefore, I call to You, O my Jesus,
O Christ, have mercy on me as I sing: Blessed are You, O God
of our fathers.
391

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

O Christ Jesus, I cry: Nail me down with the fear of You,
O my Jesus, and pilot me to Your calm haven now, O my
compassionate Jesus, so that as one saved, I may sing to You:
Blessed are You, O God of our fathers.
Glory:
O Christ Jesus, ten thousand times have I, the passionate
one, promised You repentance, O my Jesus, but wretch that
I am, I deceived You. Therefore, I cry to You, my Jesus:
Enlighten my soul which remains unfeeling: O Christ, the
God of our fathers, blessed are You.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
You gave birth to Jesus in a wondrous way that was
sublime. Ever pray to Him, Immaculate Lady, to forgive all
my terrible sins against nature, so that when I am saved, I can
sing: Blessed are you who gave birth to Christ in the flesh.

Ode 8.
Irmos. For God has descended into a fiery furnace. He
went down to the Hebrew youths, and turned the flame into
dew. Let us sing, all you works of the Lord, and exalt Him
above all, forever.
O my Jesus, I beg You, as You delivered the sinful woman
from a multitude of sins, deliver me, also, O Jesus. O Jesus,
my Christ, cleanse the impurity of my soul, O my Jesus.
O Jesus, having yielded to irrational pleasures, I have
become irrational, O my Jesus; and wretch that I am, I have
truly become like the beasts, O Savior. Therefore, O Jesus,
deliver me from irrationality.
392

Akathist Hymn To Our Sweetest Lord Jesus Christ

Glory:
Having fallen, O Jesus, into the hands of soul-corrupting
thieves, I have been stripped now of my divinely-woven
garment, O my Jesus, and I am lying all bruised with wounds.
O my Christ, pour on me oil and wine.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
O Theotokos Mary, you gave birth to my Jesus and my
God in a mysterious way. Ever pray to Christ to save your
servants and those who sing to you from misfortune, O Virgin
inviolate.

Ode 9.
Irmos. God the Word, Who came forth from God, and
Who by ineffable wisdom came to renew Adam after his
grievous fall to corruption through eating, and Who ineffably
took flesh from the Holy Virgin for our sake, Him do we the
faithful with one accord magnify with hymns.
I have surpassed Manasseh, the publican, the harlot, the
prodigal, and the thief, my Jesus, by my wanton and perverted
deeds. O compassionate Jesus, but do forestall me, O my
Jesus, and save me.
By my passions, O my Jesus, have I, the wretched one,
surpassed all those from Adam who have sinned both before
the Law and in the Law, O Jesus, and after the Law and Grace,
O my Jesus. But by Your judgments save me, O my Jesus.
Glory:
May I not be cast from Your mystical glory, O Jesus. May
I not be herded onto the left side, sweetest Jesus. May I be
393

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

given the restful joy at Your right side, O Jesus my Christ, the
merciful One.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Only pure and immaculate Virgin Mary, O Theotokos
who have borne Jesus, implore Him to save those who hasten
to you  from danger, temptation, and future fire, since He is
your Son and your Creator.

Hymn of Light:
O Jesus, Giver of wisdom and understanding, Nourisher
of beggars, Protector of orphans, Physician of those in pain,
heal and illumine my heart, O Jesus, which is covered with
the scars of sins and the wounds of passions, O Jesus, and
save me.

Theotokion:
Illumine my mind with the brilliance which radiated from
you, Virgin. Enlighten my heart. Dispel the sinful darkness,
and drive away the gloom of laziness.
At the stichera at the Praises, Tone 4:
Jesus our Savior, the angels in heaven sing Your wondrous
Name, and we sinners on earth praise Your Name with mouths
of clay so that You may have mercy on us.
Your Name is most honored, O Savior, where You sit at
the right of the Father, yet here on earth Your immaculate
incarnation is glorified. But those in hell who see Your descent
are shamed. O Christ God, deliver us from them and save us.

Akathist Hymn To Our Sweetest Lord Jesus Christ

Habakkuk perceived with fear Your wonderous deeds in a
vision. With the passage of years, O Jesus, You were revealed
to prodigals and thieves. Yet, wretch that I am, I remain in
slothfulness, but perhaps from now on you might give me
understanding and fear of You, O Compassionate One, and
great mercy.
Glory: Now and ever: Theotokion:
O Theotokos, you are a strong deliverer of those who hope
in you; lead me to the quiet haven of divine desire through
your maternal courage that you have for your Son, O Bride

Prayer to our Lord Jesus Christ
To You, O Lord, the only Good One Who do not remember
evils, I confess my sins; I fall down before You, unworthy as I
am, crying out: I have sinned, O Lord, I have sinned, and I am
not worthy to look upon the height of heaven because of the
multitude of my iniquities. But, my Lord, O Lord, grant me
tears of compunction, You Who alone are good and merciful,
so that with them I may entreat You to cleanse me of all sin
before the end, for the place that I must pass through when I
have separated from this body is frightful and terrible, and a
multitude of dark and inhuman demons await me, and there is
no one to come to my help or to deliver me. For this reason,
I fall down before your goodness: do not deliver me up to
those who wrong me, nor let my enemies triumph over me, O
Good Lord, nor let them say: ‘you have come into our hands,
and you have been delivered up unto us.’ Neither, O Lord,
forget Your compassions, and do not render to me according
to my iniquities, and do not turn Your countenance away from
me, but do You, O Lord, chasten me—but with mercy and
395

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

compassion, and do not let my enemy rejoice over me but
quench his threatening against me and bring to nothing all his
deeds. And grant me an unsullied way to You, O Good Lord,
because, having sinned, I have not had recourse to any other
physician, and have not stretched out my hands to a strange
god. Therefore, do not reject my supplication, but hear me
in Your goodness, and strengthen my heart in Your fear, and
let Your grace be upon me, O Lord, like a fire consuming the
impure thoughts within me. For You, O Lord, are the Light
above all lights, the Joy above all joys, the Repose above all
repose, and the Salvation that remains forever and ever. Amen.

Akathist Hymn
to the Most Holy Theotokos
At O Lord, I have cried, the stichera in Tone 6.
According to:Wholly consecrated:
)
(Vse otloživše:  
Gabriel stood before you, O Maiden, revealing the plan
from of old. He greeted you and said: Rejoice, Unsown Land;
rejoice, Unburnt Bush; rejoice, Unfathomable Depth; rejoice,
Bridge leading to heaven and Ladder raised on high whom
Jacob saw; rejoice, Divine Jar of Manna; rejoice, Release
from the curse; rejoice, Restoration of Adam, the Lord is with
you.
The inviolate Maiden said to the angelic Commander:
You appear to me as a man but what you say to me is beyond
human words, for you are telling me that God will be with me
and that He will dwell in my womb. Tell me, how can I become
the spacious container and holy temple of the One Who is
borne aloft on the cherubim? Do not entice me deceitfully, for
I have never known pleasure, nor have I experienced wedlock.
How then shall I bear a child?
The bodiless one said: Whenever God so wills, the order of
nature is overcome, and supernatural things are accomplished.
Believe that what I say is true, all-holy and all-spotless one.
She cried out: Let it be done to me according to your word and
397

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

I will give birth to the fleshless One Who borrows flesh from
me, for He alone is able, by sharing in it, to restore human
nature to its ancient dignity.
Glory: now and ever: Tone 2:
[composed by Theophanes]
The eternal mystery is revealed today. The Son of God
becomes Son of man. By sharing what is imperfect, He
makes me share what is perfect. Of old, Adam disobeyed; he
wished to become God, but failed. Now God becomes man
that He might make Adam god. Let creation rejoice, let nature
sing for joy: for the Archangel stands before the Virgin with
great respect and greets her with good news that takes away
our sorrow. O our God, Who took flesh in Your merciful
compassion, glory to You!
At the aposticha, Tone 1:
According to: The ranks of heaven:
(Nebesnych Činov:  

)

Gabriel flew down from the vault of heaven and came to
Nazareth. Standing before the Virgin Mary, he cried to her:
Rejoice! You shall conceive a Son, more ancient than Adam,
the Maker of all things and the Deliverer of those who cry to
you: Rejoice, pure Virgin.
Verse: Hear, O daughter, and see, and incline your ear.
Gabriel brought from heaven good tidings to the Virgin,
and he cried out to her: Rejoice! You shall conceive in your
womb Him Whom the world cannot contain, Who yet shall
be contained in you; and you shall be the bearer of Him Who
shone forth from the Father before the Morning Star.
398

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Verse: The wealthy will seek your aid.
The co-eternal Word of the Father without beginning, not
being parted from the things on high, has now descended here
below, in His infinite compassion taking pity upon fallen men;
and assuming the poverty of Adam, He has put on a form that
is alien to Him.
Verse: Let all the earth bow to you, and sing to you.
Eternally from the Father, and in time from a mother, the
ever-subsisting Word revealed Himself to the world. He took
on the form of a slave. He became flesh, without losing His
divinity. He was conceived in a womb without seed and He
raises Adam.
Glory: now and ever: Tone 2:
[composed by Cosmas the Monk]
Gabriel today announces the good tidings to her who is
full of grace: Hail, O unwedded Maiden who have not known
marriage. Be not struck with dismay by my strange form, nor
be afraid. I am an archangel. Once the serpent beguiled Eve,
but now I announce to you the good tidings of joy, O Most
Pure, you shall remain a virgin and yet shall bear the Lord.
Then the troparion, Tone 8:
When he grasped the meaning of the mystical command,
the bodiless one stood instantly in Joseph’s tent. He said to the
woman who knew not wedlock: He Who bowed the heavens
when He came down is contained entirely in you without
change. Seeing Him in your womb taking the form of a slave,
I am amazed as I exclaim: Rejoice, O Unwedded Bride.

A CANON OF THANKSGIVING TO THE MOST
HOLY THEOTOKOS
Which has this foundation verse:
Harbor of joy, rejoicing is due to you alone.

A Composition of Joseph.
Tone 4. Ode 1.
Irmos. I will open my mouth. It will be filled by the
Spirit, and I will offer words of praise to the Queen Mother. I
will celebrate solemnly in radiance. In rejoicing, I will sing of
these wonders.
When the great Archangel saw you, O immaculate one, as
the living book of Christ, sealed by the Spirit, he cried unto
you: Rejoice, vessel of joy, through whom the curse of our
first-mother is loosed.
Rejoice, O virgin bride of God, the uplifter of Adam and
death-knell of Hades; rejoice, O all-blameless one, the palace
of the only King; rejoice, the fiery throne of the Almighty.
Glory:
Rejoice, the Unwithering Rose; Rejoice, who bear the
fragrant Apple; rejoice, for you gave birth to the agreeable
fruit and the fragrant aroma of our King; rejoice, O bride and
maiden ever pure, who brings salvation to the world.
Now and ever:
400

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Rejoice, treasury of purity, who raises us up when we had
fallen; rejoice royal lily, whose fragrance fills the faithful;
rejoice, sweet-smelling incense and most precious perfume.

Ode 3.
Irmos. O Theotokos, life-giving source of blessings, grant
strength to those united in faith who sing hymns of praise to
you. In your glory, grant them the crowns of victory.
You have made the wheat of heaven spring up in the
untilled field; rejoice, mystical table who bore the Bread of
Life; rejoice, sovereign Virgin, never-failing spring of lifegiving water.
Rejoice, for you gave birth to the Victim without blemish;
rejoice, Mother of the Lamb Who takes away the sin of the
world; rejoice, fervent mediator.
Glory:
Rejoice, brilliant dawn, who alone bore Christ our Sun;
rejoice, tabernacle of the Light, Who dispelled the darkness
of death and dispersed the gloom of demons.
Now and ever:
Rejoice, only gate through whom the Word alone has
passed; by giving birth, O Virgin, you shattered the gates
and bolts of Hades; rejoice divine entryway of the redeemed
people, O Virgin.

Ode 4.
Irmos. Jesus, the true God, Who sits in glory upon the
divine throne, now appears riding on a swift cloud; and with
his pure hand He saves those who cry: Glory to Your power,
O Christ.
401

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

With our hymns and our voices, we, the faithful, sing to
you, O Virgin, worthy of our praise; Rejoice, fertile mountain,
uplifted by the Spirit; rejoice, golden candlestick and vessel
containing the manna, savory sweetness for the faithful.
Rejoice, intercessor for the world and most pure Queen;
rejoice, ladder leading from earth to grace; rejoice, bridge
leading from death to life all the faithful who honor you with
their hymns.
Higher than the heavens, in your womb you held the
earth’s Pillar and Foundation, and you did not suffer pains of
childbirth, O Maiden. Rejoice, O sea-shell that dipped in your
own pure blood the purple robe dyed for the King of heaven.
Glory:
Rejoice, for you gave birth to our Lawgiver, O Queen; He
freely wiped out our sins; rejoice, unfathomable ocean, and
indescribable peak; unwedded spouse through whom we are
deified.
Now and ever:
For the world, you have woven a crown not made by
human hands; we sing to you and cry out: Rejoice, holy
Virgin and protectress of all, unshakeable rampart, fortress
and sacred refuge.

Ode 5.
Irmos. All nations marveled at your divine glory, for you,
O Virgin who have not known wedlock, carried within your
womb the God of all, the eternal Son to Whom you gave birth;
He grants salvation to all who sing your praises.
402

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Rejoice, for you gave birth to the Way of Life; rejoice,
for you saved the world from the deluge of sin; rejoice, Bride
of God, hearing and speaking about Whom thrills; rejoice,
dwelling of the Creator and Lord.
Rejoice, most pure one, fortress and rampart of humans;

Rejoice, fiery chariot of the divine Word; rejoice, Queen

Glory:
Strengthened by your power, we cry out in faith: Rejoice,

Now and ever:
Rejoice, spacious tabernacle of the Word of God; rejoice,

who always proclaim you blessed, O Theotokos.

Ode 6.
Irmos. Come, O you faithful, and clap your hands as we
celebrate this holy and solemn feast of the Theotokos. Glorify
Him Who was born of her.

403

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Rejoice, nuptial chamber of the divine Word, the reason
for the deification of us all; rejoice, O immaculate Virgin,

The dew has fallen from you, the flame of polytheism has

Glory:

Now and ever:

that burns without being consumed; rejoice, bright cloud
covering the faithful with its never-ending shadow.
After this the Kontakia and Ikosi to the Theotokos in Tone 8:

Kontakion One:
To you, our defender and leader in battle, O Theotokos,
we your servants, delivered from our sufferings, offer hymns
of victory and thanksgiving. But you, invincible in power, set
us free from every peril, that we may cry to you: “Rejoice, O
Bride and Maiden ever-pure!”

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Ikos One:
An Archangel was sent from heaven to greet the
Theotokos, and as he saw You assuming a body at the sound
of his bodiless voice, O Lord, he stood rapt in amazement and
cried to her in these words:
Rejoice, O you through whom joy will shine forth;
rejoice, O you through whom the curse will disappear!
Rejoice, O Restoration of the fallen Adam;
rejoice, O Redemption of the tears of Eve!
Rejoice, O Height beyond the reach of human thought;
rejoice, O Depth, impenetrable even for angelic eyes!
Rejoice, O you who have become a kingly throne;
rejoice, O you who carry Him Who carries all!
Rejoice, O Star who manifest the sun;
rejoice, O Womb of the Divine Incarnation!
Rejoice, O you through whom creation is renewed;
rejoice, O you through whom the Creator is adored!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Two:
The holy one, seeing herself in all her purity, says to
Gabriel boldly: “Your strange words seem difficult for my soul
to accept; for how do you speak of a birth from a conception
without seed, exclaiming: Alleluia!”

Ikos Two:
Trying to grasp the meaning of this mystery, the Virgin
asked the holy messenger: “How is it possible that a son be
born from a virginal womb? Tell me.” And he answered her
with awe, crying out in these words:

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Rejoice, O Hidden sense of the ineffable plan;

Rejoice, O Beginning of the miracles of Christ;

Rejoice, O Celestial Ladder by whom God came down;
rejoice, O Bridge leading earthly ones to heaven!
Rejoice, O Wonder, ever-thrilling to the angels;

Rejoice, O you who surpass the wisdom of the wise;

Kontakion Three:
When the power of the Most High overshadowed the
one who had never known the nuptial bed, her fruitful womb
conceived, and she became for all a delicious field for those
who wished to reap salvation by singing: Alleluia!

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

rejoice, for you have prepared a haven for the souls!

Kontakion Four:
Filled with a storm of contradictory thoughts, the wise
Joseph was greatly disturbed: until then, he had seen you a

Ikos Four:
The shepherds heard the angels singing hymns of praise
to the coming of Christ in the flesh. And running to Him as
to a shepherd, they saw Him as a spotless Lamb grazing at
Mary’s breast. They sang a hymn to her and said:
Rejoice, O Mother of Lamb and Shepherd;
rejoice, O Fold of rational sheep!
Rejoice, O Protection against unseen foes;
rejoice, O Key to the doors of paradise!
Rejoice, for the heavenly rejoice with the earthly;

Rejoice, O Steadfast Foundation of faith;

Kontakion Five:
When the Magi saw the Star moved by God, they followed
its glittering light. Using it as a beacon, they found through it

Ikos Five:
The sons of Chaldea saw in the Virgin’s hands the One

rejoice, O you who saved us from the mire of evil deeds!

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Kontakion Six:
The Magi, having become God-bearing heralds, returned
to Babylon, conforming to Your command, announcing You,
the Christ, to all, and leaving Herod as a fool who did not
know how to sing: Alleluia!

Ikos Six:
Illuminating Egypt with the light of truth, You cast away
the darkness of error. For the idols, unable to stand Your might,
fell down, and those who had been delivered from them cried
out to the Theotokos:
Rejoice, O Restoration of mankind;
rejoice, O Downfall of the demons!
Rejoice, O you who crushed the error of deceit;

Rejoice, O Sea who drowned the symbolic pharaoh;
rejoice, O Rock who quenched those who thirst for life!
Rejoice, O Pillar of fire who guided those in darkness;
rejoice, O Shelter of the world, wider than the clouds!
Rejoice, O Food who took the place of manna;
rejoice, O Servant of holy delight!
Rejoice, O Land of the promised good;
rejoice, O you who flow with milk and honey!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Seven:
As Simeon was about to leave this present deceitful world,
You were entrusted to him as an infant, but You made Yourself
known to him as the Perfect God. Wherefore, he marveled at
Your wisdom beyond words, and cried out: Alleluia!
409

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Ikos Seven:
The Creator displayed a new creation to us who had come
from Him: He came forth from a womb that had received no
seed, and He left it intact as it had been, so that at the sight of
this marvel, we would sing to her and cry out:
Rejoice, O Blossom of incorruption;
rejoice, O Crown of self-mastery!
Rejoice, O you who displays the radiance of resurrection;
rejoice, O you who displayed the life of angels!
Rejoice, Tree of glorious fruit on which the faithful feed;
rejoice, Shady Tree where many are sheltered!
Rejoice, O you who carried the Redeemer of the captives;
rejoice, O you who gave birth to the Guide of the lost!
Rejoice, O you who unsettled even the just judge;
rejoice, Forgiveness for many who have stumbled!
Rejoice, O Robe of boldness for those without hope;
rejoice, O Love surpassing all desire!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Eight:
Now that we have seen this strange birth, let us estrange
ourselves from the world and turn our minds to heaven:
indeed, it is for this that the God Most High appeared on earth
as a lowly man, desiring to draw up to heaven those who cry
out to Him: Alleluia!

Ikos Eight:
While fully present amid those below, The Uncircumscribed Word was in no way absent from those above: for
what happened was a divine condescension, and not a moving
410

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

from one place to another; and it was a birth from a Virgin
inspired by God, who heard these words:
Rejoice, O Space of the spaceless God;
rejoice, O Gate of the sublime mystery!
Rejoice, O Message unsure to men without faith;
rejoice, O Glory most certain to those who believe!
Rejoice, O Sacred Chariot of the One above the cherubim;
rejoice, Perfect Dwelling of the One above the seraphim!
Rejoice, O you who reconciled opposites;
rejoice, O you who combined maidenhood and
motherhood!
Rejoice, O you through whom transgression was erased;
rejoice, O you through whom paradise was opened!
Rejoice, O Key to the Kingdom of Christ;
rejoice, O Hope for the ages of bliss!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Nine:
The whole order of the Angels marveled at the great work
of Your becoming Man: for they saw the One Inaccessible
as God become a Man Accessible to All, living with us and
hearing all cry out: Alleluia!

Ikos Nine:
O Theotokos, we see the best of speakers become as mute
as fish in your regard, for they could not explain how you
could give birth while remaining a virgin. As for us, while
marveling at the mystery, we cry out to you with faith:
Rejoice, O Container of God’s Wisdom;
rejoice, O Treasury of His Providence!
411

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Rejoice, O Reproof of foolish philosophers;
rejoice, O Confusion of speechless wise men!
Rejoice, for you perplexed the inquisitive minds;
rejoice, for you dried up the inventors of myths!
Rejoice, for you ripped the Athenians’ meshes;
rejoice, for you filled the fishermen’s nets!
Rejoice, O Retriever from the abyss of ignorance;
rejoice, O Lamplight of Knowledge to many!
Rejoice, O Ship for those who seek salvation;
rejoice, O Harbor for the sailors of life!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Ten:
Desiring to save the world, the Creator of All came down
to it of His own will. Being at the same time our Shepherd
and our God, He appeared among us, a man like us. And so
the like called upon the like, and as God He heard: Alleluia!

Ikos Ten:
O Virgin Theotokos, you are the Strength of Virgins
and of all those who have recourse to you. For the Maker of
Heaven and Earth covered you with His shadow, O Pure One,
and came to dwell in your womb, and taught us all to cry out
to you:
Rejoice, O Pillar of Virginity;
rejoice, O Gateway of salvation!
Rejoice, O Principle of spiritual recreation;
rejoice, O Dispenser of God’s bounties!
Rejoice, for you restored those born in shame;
rejoice, for you gave wisdom to the mindless!
Rejoice, O you who stopped the corruptor of minds;
412

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

rejoice, O you who bore the Sower of Chastity!
Rejoice, Holy Chamber of virginal wedlock;
rejoice, O you who join the faithful with God!
Rejoice, O gracious foster-mother of virgins;
rejoice, O Bridesmaid of holy souls!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Eleven:
Every hymn falls short when it attempts to sing the
multitude of Your mercies: we could sing to You as many
songs as there are grains of sand, O Holy King, without ever
doing anything worthy of what You have given to those who
cry out to You: Alleluia!

Ikos Eleven:
We see the holy Virgin as a brilliant luminary enlightening
those who live in darkness; for having kindled the Immaterial
Light, she leads men to the knowledge of God and fills their
minds with radiance, so that she is worthily praised in these
words:
Rejoice, O Beam of the mystical sun;
rejoice, O Radiance of the Light without setting!
Rejoice, Lightening-flash that brightens the souls;
rejoice, Thunder-clap that strikes down the foes!
Rejoice, for you have raised the many-lighted Star;
rejoice, for you have opened the many-coursed Stream!
Rejoice, O you who traced the living model of the pool;
rejoice, O you who erased the stain of sin!
Rejoice, Flowing Water that cleanses the conscience;
rejoice, Holy Vessel overflowing with joy!
Rejoice, O Fragrance of the sweetness of Christ;
rejoice, O Life of the mystical banquet!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!
413

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Kontakion Twelve:
Because He wished to grant release from all the ancient
debts, the One Who pays men’s dues came down Himself to
those who had spurned His grace; He tore up their obligations,
and heard from all of them this cry: Alleluia!

Ikos Twelve:
By singing to your maternity, we all exalt you as a Spiritual
Temple, O Theotokos! For the One Who dwelt within your
womb, the Lord Who holds all things in His hands, sanctified
you, glorified you and taught all men to sing to you:
Rejoice, O Tabernacle of God the Word;
rejoice, Holy One, superior Holy of Holies!
Rejoice, O Ark that the Spirit has gilded;
rejoice, Inexhaustible Treasure of Life!
Rejoice, Precious Crown of rightful authorities;
rejoice, Sacred Glory of reverent priests!
Rejoice, Unshakable Tower of the Church;
rejoice, Unbreachable Wall of the Kingdom!
Rejoice, O you through whom the trophies are raised;
rejoice, O you through whom the enemies are routed!
Rejoice, O Healing of my body;
rejoice, O Salvation of my soul!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

Kontakion Thirteen
O Mother worthy of all praise, you who have given birth to
the Word, the Holiest of the Holy, accept this present offering,
deliver all men from every affliction, and save from the future
punishment those who cry out to you: Alleluia!
This Kontakion is said three times.
414

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

And the First Ikos is read again:
An Archangel was sent from heaven to greet the
Theotokos, and as he saw You assuming a body at the sound
of his bodiless voice, O Lord, he stood rapt in amazement and
cried to her in these words:
Rejoice, O you through whom joy will shine forth;
rejoice, O you through whom the curse will disappear!
Rejoice, O Restoration of the fallen Adam;
rejoice, O Redemption of the tears of Eve!
Rejoice, O Height beyond the reach of human thought;
rejoice, O Depth, impenetrable even for angelic eyes!
Rejoice, O you who have become a kingly throne;
rejoice, O you who carry Him Who carries all!
Rejoice, O Star who manifest the sun;
rejoice, O Womb of the Divine Incarnation!
Rejoice, O you through whom creation is renewed;
rejoice, O you through whom the Creator is adored!
Rejoice, O Bride and Maiden ever-pure!

And again the First Kontakion:
To you, our defender and leader in battle, O Theotokos,
we your servants, delivered from our sufferings, offer hymns
of victory and thanksgiving. But you, invincible in power, set
us free from every peril, that we may cry to you: “Rejoice, O
Bride and Maiden ever-pure!”

Ode 7.
Irmos. The three youths courageously walked about in
the flaming furnace, preferring to worship the Creator rather
than created things, and they sang out in joy: Blessed are You
and praised above all, O God of our fathers.
415

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

We sing of your praises and cry out to you: Rejoice, chariot
of the spiritual Sun; you are truly the vine who produced the
sweet grape Whose wine brings joy to the faithful who glorify
you.
You have given birth to the One Who heals all wounds;
rejoice, divine bride, mystical branch which blossomed with
immortality; rejoice, O Queen who fill us with joy and make
us inheritors of life.
The tongue of orators is perplexed when it seeks to praise
you, O Theotokos; you are exalted more than the seraphim in
giving birth to Christ our King; intercede with Him to save
from all danger the faithful who venerate you.
Glory:
The ends of the earth proclaim you blessed, and they
sing with love: Rejoice, holy book in which the hand of the
Father has inscribed His Word; we ask you to beseech Him to
inscribe your servants in the Book of Life, O Theotokos!
Now and ever:
We, your servants, beseech you and we bow our hearts
before you: incline your ear, O Purest One, and save us from
the abyss of temptations; protect your people from the darts of
the Enemy, O holy Theotokos.

Ode 8.
Irmos. The three Youths in the furnace were saved by the
Offspring of the Theotokos. He Who was foretold has been
born on earth, and He joins together all creation to sing to
416

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

you: All you works of the Lord, bless the Lord and praise Him
above all forever!
You have received the Word into your womb; you have
borne the One Who bears the world in His hand; with your
milk, you nourished the One Who nourishes the whole world.
Therefore, we sing to Him: All you works of the Lord, bless
the Lord and praise Him above all forever!
Moses recognized the burning bush in the great mystery
of your childbearing; the Youths clearly prefigured it when
they stood in the midst of the flames without being consumed;
O holy and most pure Virgin, we bless you above all forever!
Once stripped through the deceit of the Serpent,
through your childbearing we have regained the garment of
immortality; we who once sat in the darkness of sin, now
have seen the Light dwelling in your womb; O Virgin and
tabernacle of light, we praise you above all forever!
Glory:
Through you the dead regain life, for you have conceived
the personification of Life; those who are mute begin to speak,
those with leprosy are purified, sickness is driven back, and
the multitude of evil spirits is overcome, through you, O
Virgin, the salvation of mortals.
Now and ever:
You, who gave birth to the Salvation of the world, the
One through which we ascended from the earth to the height,
rejoice, All-Blessed One, the cover and fortress, wall and
stronghold, O Pure, for those who sing: All you works of the
Lord, bless the Lord and praise Him above all forever!
417

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Ode 9.
Irmos. May every child of the earth exult in spirit and
hold aloft the burning lamp; may the angels in heaven praise
with joy the holy feast of the Mother of God and sing to her:
Rejoice, O blessed and Ever-Virgin, holy Theotokos.
Deliver us from the unending trials, from the chains of
the Enemy and every other scourge that justly threatens us
because of our sins that we may sing to you: Rejoice; for we
are the faithful who have become participants in your joy.
You are our confidence and our light; therefore, we cry
out to you: Rejoice, unsetting star, who have brought our Sun
into the world; rejoice, pure Virgin, for you open Eden which
had formerly been closed to us; vessel of myrrh who have
received the inexhaustible ointment poured out upon you.
Let us stand with fear in the house of God and say:
Rejoice, Queen of the universe; rejoice, Mary, Lady of our
hearts; rejoice, O all-fair and all-pure one, rejoice, pillar of
fire, leading mortals to their heavenly homeland.
Glory:
Rejoice, Ever-Virgin dove, who gave birth to the God of
goodness; rejoice, glory of all the saints and crown of martyrs,
the adornment of the just and the salvation of all our souls.
Now and ever:
Spare your inheritance, O Lord, closing your eyes to all
our sins; favorably accept the intercession of the one who
bore You on earth, O Christ, when, in Your sovereign love,
You deigned to clothe yourself in human nature.

Akathist Hymn to the Most Holy Theotokos

Hymn of Light.

(Ženy uslyšite:  

)

Dance for joy; sing for gladness; Gabriel appeared to the
Virgin. He brought joy, the joy of the annunciation to the city
of Nazareth. Rejoice, pure and immaculate intercessors for

At the Stichera at the Praises, Tone 4:
According to: As valiant among the martyrs:
(Jako dobl’a:  
)
The great mystery, which even the angels do not know, is
entrusted to the archangel Gabriel; and now he comes to you,
O most pure and fair dove, and he cries out with the One Who
renews the human race: Rejoice, all-holy Lady, through my
word, prepare to receive the Word of God into your womb.
A bright palace is prepared for You, O Lord; it is the womb
of the most pure Virgin. You come to dwell there in Your love
for us, to draw us up from the slavery to death, and to restore
our former beauty; we are waiting for Your Salvation!
The archangel comes to you visibly, O most pure Virgin,
and he says: Rejoice, for you redeem the ancient curse; rejoice,
restoration of fallen humanity; rejoice, chosen one, who alone
are acceptable to the Lord; rejoice, mystical throne of the Sun;
accept the Infinite One Who comes to dwell in your womb.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Glory: now and ever: Tone 4:
The Theotokos heard a strange language when the
Archangel spoke the words of good news; she received
the greeting in faith, and thus conceived the Eternal God.
Therefore, we also cry out in joy: O God Who are incarnate
without change, grant peace to the world and great mercy to
our souls.

Prayer to the Most Holy Theotokos
Most gracious Lady, now receive from us, your unworthy
servants, these worthy gifts of praise fitting to you alone,
who are more honorable than any human being and more
beautiful that all of creation seen or unseen. Blessed is the
root of Jesse, and thrice-blessed the house of David from
which you blossomed forth. God is with you and you will not
be shaken. The Most High sanctified you, His tabernacle, and
in you the covenants and vows of God to our fathers received
a glorious fulfillment, for through you the Lord of powers
came to be with us. Blessed are you for all generations, O
holy and blessed one, more exalted than all creatures both in
heaven and on earth, more splendid than the cherubim, and
more glorious than the seraphim, the boast of virgins and
stronghold of the faithful. Most praiseworthy Theotokos, do
not cease praying for us, your unworthy servants, that we may
be delivered from the evil one and from all misfortune. O
Lady, through you we have come to know the Son of God, and
have been deemed worthy of His all-holy Body and Blood. By
your supplications, keep us free from condemnation until the
end, that we all may be saved in all things, as we magnify you
with love. We give glory to your Son, together with the Father
and the Holy Spirit, now and ever and forever. Amen.

Archangels and Angels

Stichera, Tone 1:
According to: O Martyrs worthy of all praise:
(Prechval’niji Mučenicy:  

)

O bodiless angels, you stand before God’s throne, and you
shine in gleaming splendor. You glow with radiance forever in
the company of the other lights. Pray to Christ to give our
souls peace and great mercy.
O immortal angels, you received true enduring life from
the first moment of your existence. You are truly gifted. You
hold the treasure of gazing on the Eternal Glory and the Eternal
Wisdom. You augment that radiance, and you embellish it
with lights of honor.
O angels and archangels, principalities, thrones,
dominions, six-winged seraphim, and many-eyed cherubim,
O virtues, powers, wisdoms, and godly authorities: pray to
Christ to give our souls peace and great mercy.

the angels that I may complete the road of life in virtue, so
that the evening of death may not approach me unprepared,
nor send me into the blazing fire to be tormented. Deliver me
from all of this, O Immaculate One.

Verse: Praise Him all his angels. Praise Him all his hosts.

Protect the faithful from evil spirits under the shelter of
your wings, for you dispel the darkness.
Glory:
O my guardian angel: you are the secondary light after

thrice-radiant Godhead for me.

A Composition of Joseph
Tone 8. Ode 1.
Irmos. Let us sing to our wonderful God Who freed Israel
from slavery, O people. We sing a song of triumph. We chant:
Master, we sing to You alone!
Versicle: Holy archangels and angels, pray to God for us!
Come, people! Let us sing to the uncreated Trinity Who
governs the ranks of His ministers in heaven. Let us sing:
Holy, Holy, Holy are You, God almighty.
You have formed a choir from the first fruits of Your
creation, spiritual beings which surround your throne, singing
to You: Holy, Holy, Holy are You, God almighty.
Rejoice, Gabriel, herald of the incarnation. Rejoice,
Michael, prince of angels. You join in the song: Holy, Holy.
Holy are You, God almighty.
Theotokion:
I am moved by the mystery of your incarnation, O Christ.
You were God by nature. You willed to be born a man through
the virgin, that You might save the world from the devil’s
grasp.

Service to Archangels and Angels

Ode 3.

Irmos. Instill reverence in the hearts of Your servants,
Lord. Give strength to us who truly invoke You.
You have established those mighty beings who do your
will by your power, Immortal One. They are with You always
in the highest.
Receive the ministers of Your Incarnation and Your true
Resurrection, O Christ, these leaders of the angelic hosts who
pray for us.
You have appointed angels to guard humans,
Compassionate Lord. You have made them ministers of Your
salvation, for Your saints, O Christ.
Theotokion.
O Bride of God: in a very mysterious manner you
conceived the Lord and Savior. He rescues those who invoke
you from any awful fate.

Sessional Hymn. Tone 8:
According to: Command:
(Povel’innoje:  
)
Prince of heavenly hosts! Leader of those who wait at the
sublime throne of Divinity’s glory on high: O Archangel Michael,
in the company of all holy angels, seek absolution from the
Lord for the whole world by your unceasing prayers. Seek the
remission of sins, mercy and grace for us on judgment day.
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion.
Through my many evil deeds of lawlessness I have fallen
into a pit of despair. I am confused. I am filled with anxiety. O
Lady Theotokos, save me! Help me! You are purification for
sinners. You are the regeneration of the fallen.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Stavrotheotokion.
You saw him hanging on the tree, surrounded by evil
men. He became man from you, virgin Lady, and took flesh
from your flesh. Your heart pained and you shed a mother’s
tears: O! O! O, my Child! How strange and mysterious is that
divine plan by which You regenerated creation. I sing of Your
compassion for humanity.

Ode 4.
Irmos. Like a rider on horses, Lord, You have been
carried by Your apostles. You have guided them like horses
with reins. Your sojourn has worked salvation for all who
believe and sing: Glory to Your power, O Lord!
Like a rider on horses, Lover of Mankind, You have sat
upon the throne of angels. You have guided them like horses
with reins. Your sojourn has worked salvation for all who
faithfully sing: Glory to Your power, O Lord!
O Immortal One, You filled the angels with Your virtues,
and the ends of the earth are full of Your divine and glorious
praise, O One Who had no beginning. With the angels we sing
to You: Glory to Your power, O Lord!
You came to save Your people, O compassionate Lord.
You summoned Your ministers to this work, O Christ. Your
advent is joy for those who believe and sing to You: Glory to
Your power, O Lord!
Theotokion.
You have appeared as a mother and a virgin, most pure
one, for you gave birth to Christ, Who is both God and man,
426

Service to Archangels and Angels

Who the angels praise for through your prayers you have
changed your people’s sorrow to joy.

Ode 5.
Irmos. You brought the whole world out of the darkness
of ignorance, O Lord, by imparting the knowledge of God.
Enlighten me with the dawn of Your love for mankind.
The angelic hosts praise You, O Christ, because You are
the summit of every desire, and they are carried to the very
heights by this desire.
You have formed Your angels in your own image, O
Christ. You have made them a chorus for Your majesty. They
are intellectual by nature and incorruptible in Your grace, O
Incomprehensible One.
By keeping them close to You, O Lord, You have preserved
Your ministers from evil passions. You do good to those who
serve You, for You are the very source of goodness.
Theotokion.
O all-immaculate Lady, revive my soul deadened by
passions. Guide me to the path of eternal and blessed life, for
you gave birth to the Sustainer of life.

Ode 6.
Irmos. You rescued Jonah in the whale. Rescue me from
the turbulence as You rescued him. Save me who am fettered
with the devil’s wiles.
Out of nothing You created the immortal armies of heaven
by the word of Your command. You made them radiant.
427

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

You have become the ministers of God’s praise, angelic
spirits. You cover your Creator with glory. You are His divine
tabernacle. You are citizens of heaven.
Theotokion.
You are praiseworthy who gave birth to the Light that
shines on all. O Pure One, banish the darkness of my sins

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Leaders of God’s armies and ministers of divine glory,
commanders of angels and guides of mortals, plead on our

Ikos:
O Lover of Mankind, O Immortal One, You said in Your
scriptures that the multitude of angels in heaven would rejoice

dare to implore Your compassion, O only-sinless One Who
sees our hearts. Be generous to us and send down Your mercy
upon us unworthy ones. O Master, grant forgiveness to us, for
the leaders of the bodiless powers are praying to You for all
of us.

Ode 7.
Irmos. The Hebrew youths trampled bravely upon the
flames in the furnace, and they changed the fire into dew,
singing: Blessed are You, O Lord God, forever!

428

Service to Archangels and Angels

You have revealed, O Compassionate One, the immaterial

and they cry out to You unceasingly: Blessed are You, O Lord

The multitudes of angels stand ministering without ceasing
before Him but dare not gaze upon the divine countenance as
they cry out: Blessed are You, O Lord God, forever!
Through the Hypostatic Word You created the ranks of the
angels, O God. You sanctified them by the Divine Spirit. You

Trinitarian Hymn.
Meditating on the three Hypostases, we praise the
uncircumscribed essence of the Father, Son, and Holy Spirit,

Ode 8.
Irmos. To the Lord Who was glorified on the holy
mountain, to the Lord Who revealed the virgin birth to Moses

Let us imitate the life of the angels and lift our minds to
the heights, and let us join spiritually with them, and praise
the Lord and exalt Him, forever!
The angels of the heavenly choir, exceedingly joyful, who
stand before the throne of glory, beholding God at all times,
sing and glorify Him, forever!

429

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

You have made into a flame of immaterial fire those who
ceaselessly sing Your praises in the highest; You have made
spirits Your angel messengers. Let us prostrate before the
Trinity and glorify, forever!
Theotokion.
You Who dwelt in the womb of a virgin, and through her,
in a mysterious way, raising up the old Adam: to You, the
Lord, we sing praise and glorify, forever!

Ode 9.
Irmos. You have gone above nature in conceiving the
Creator and Lord. You became a door of salvation for the
world. We praise you forever for this, O Theotokos.
We extol You ceaselessly, O Christ, Who have ineffably
united the things of earth and heaven, and have fashioned one
Church of angels and humans.
Angels and archangels, and thrones, and dominions,
and principalities, virtues, and powers, and cherubim and
seraphim, pray with the Theotokos for the world.
Trinitarian Hymn.
We glorify You, O Trinity, for You have created all things

Theotokion.

The Stichera to the Guardian Angels [at the Praises,]
Tone 2:
According to: O house of Ephrata:
)
(Dome Evfratov:
O angel of God who stand with boldness before the Holy
Trinity, do not cease praying for me, your servant.
Because God has given you the might to guard my soul,
keep it always under the shelter of your wings.
I thank Jesus, Who gave you to me, the great guardian of
my soul, and the weapon against my enemies, the pious angel.
Make me worthy of the kingdom of God Most High, that
I might join you there and sing the thrice-holy hymn.
Glory:
O my guardian angel: you are the secondary light after
God. Do not stop pleading for me. Gaze on the splendor of the
thrice-radiant Godhead for me.
Now and ever:
Queen of angels and humans, O Theotokos, do not cease
pleading with your Son on behalf of me, your servant, O
Virgin.

Prayer to the Holy Angels
To you, as protectors and guardians of my life, I, a pitiful
being, prostrate to pray: grant me through your prayers to go
through the daily sojourn pleasing to God and inexperienced
431

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

in wicked deeds and thoughts. Open my ears to hear that I
may listen and comprehend the deeds and words of God that
are beneficial for the soul; that I may see with the spiritual
eyes, for I am possessed by sinful darkness. Pray for me,
since I have sinned at all times, that I might not be struck
by the sword of the Lord’s fury: “my offenses tower higher
than my head, and they are like a heavy burden weighing on
me” [Psalm 38]. Yet, You, my Lord, Lord, “turn to me and
have mercy on me” [Psalm 118], and “bring my soul forth
from the prison” of sins [Psalm 141], before I depart from
here and come before Your fearsome judgment. Accept Your
holy angels who pray for me, who stand around Your altar
with fear, and through their prayers and especially through
the prayers of Your most pure Mother, deliver me from Your
fearsome, terrible judgment. For You are the Lamb of God
Who take away the sins of the whole world, crucified on
the cross for our salvation; listen to my prayer and send the
guardian angel to my soul and body, that, being led by him,
I may be delivered from every visible and invisible enemy
and may receive Your mercy with all those who pleased You
since time began. For You are our God, and I come to You and
I hope in You, although I have sinned more than any human
being, I do not depart from You, nor lift up my hand to another
god. I pray You, O Lord Jesus Christ, and bless and worship
You, for You are one in the Trinity, with the Father and the
Holy Spirit, now and ever, and forever. Amen.

On Monday evening at Vespers, at O Lord, I have cried:

Stichera, Tone 1:
According to: O martyrs worthy of all praise:
(Prechval’niji Mučenicy:  

)

Wondrous prophet, baptizer of Christ, and Forerunner, I
pray that you deign to draw rivers of flowing tears from my
dried and wasted heart by your prayers so that being saved
through the many pains you have suffered, I may extol you
who are so exalted.
I put my hope in you, blessed prophet, and my life’s
desires. You baptized Christ Jesus, and He saves the world
from sin’s depths. O John, beg Him to wash my heart clean. I
pray to you to beg Christ to save me.
You are a preacher of vision: you spoke of world-wide
penance. O godly Forerunner, grant that my blind and grieving
soul may take up the call of penance. Grant that my soul may
do the will of the Lord always, and for this I will praise you
with love and fidelity.

Verse: Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel, for he has

Come quickly! Deliver me from temptation, I beg you O

Kontakion, Tone 3:
According to: Today the Virgin:
(D’iva dnes’:  
)
Today she who was once barren gives birth to Christ’s
Forerunner. He himself is the fulfillment of all prophecy; for
in the Jordan, he imposed his hand upon the Word of God
Whom the prophets had foretold and was shown to be His
prophet, herald, and Forerunner.

Ikos:
Let us now praise the Forerunner of the Lord. Elizabeth
gave birth to him from a barren womb, but not without seed. For
Christ alone passed through the impassable gate without seed.
Elizabeth, the barren one, gave birth to John, but not without a
father. The pure Virgin, however, by the overshadowing of the
Father and the Spirit of God, gave birth to Jesus. And John,
who was born from a barren one, manifested himself to be a
prophet, a herald, and also the Forerunner of the One born
without seed.

Irmos. In the beginning You created the earth with a word
and established the heavens. Blessed are You, O Lord God of

442

Service to Saint John the Forerunner

Most glorious Lady and pure Virgin, with the Forerunner,
pray your Son and King to save from all necessities those who
bless you faithfully.

Prayer to Saint John the Forerunner
O Baptizer of Christ, preacher of penitence, do not disdain
me who repents, but as you are united with the heavenly
armies, pray to our Master for me: unworthy, sorrowful,
weak, and sad, for I have fallen into many distresses. I am
an abyss of wicked deeds, for I am burdened by powerful
thoughts in my mind; I am the source of sinful deeds which are
almost endless. My poor thoughts are nailed to earthly things.
What am I to do?   I do not know to whom to flee that my
soul may be saved; only to you, O holy John, whose name is
gracious, for I know that, before the Lord, after the Theotokos,
you are greater than any other one born of woman. You were
granted to touch the head of Christ the King, the Lamb of
God Who takes away the sins of the world. Pray to Him for
my sinful soul, so that at least from now, in the eleventh
hour, I may bring a measure of grace and receive the reward
with the ones who came last to labor in the vineyard. Yes, O
Baptizer of Christ, honorable Forerunner, the last prophet, the
first martyr in grace, leader to all who fast and those who are
desert-dwellers, teacher of purity and close friend of Christ, I
run to you, do not dismiss me from your protection, but raise
me up who am falling because of the multitude of sins, renew
my soul with penitence by the Sacrament of Penance which
is like another baptism, since you are the leader preaching
repentance. Baptism washes the Ancestral Sin, and by means
of repentance all are cleansed of the evil deed. Purify me who
am covered by sins to enter where nothing wicked can enter,
into the Kingdom of Heaven. Amen.

The memory of the righteous: and the Theotokion.
And the Dismissal:
May Christ our true God have mercy on us and save
us through the prayers of His most pure Mother, and of the
honorable and glorious prophet, Forerunner, and Baptist John;
of our venerable and God-bearing fathers, and of all the saints,
for Christ is good and loves mankind.

Canon
to the Most Holy Theotokos Hodegetria
A Composition of the Hieromonk Ignatius.
Tone 4. Ode 1.
Irmos. I will open my mouth. It will be filled by the
Spirit, and I will offer words of praise to the Queen Mother. I
will celebrate solemnly in radiance. In rejoicing, I will sing of
these wonders.
In my rejoicing, I now offer you praise, pure Lady, with
joy. I sing to you with tranquil voice, O Hodegetria—rejoice!
Fill me, who sing to you, with understanding.
Birth-giver of Christ, our eternal joy, O rejoice, all-praised
hope of the orthodox. O Virgin Hodegetria, fill me with that
joy which the world desires.
Glory:
All people sing with joy, and angels always cry out
together in heaven and on earth, O Hodegetria: Rejoice, O
Virgin! Your birth-giving has filled everyone with joy.
Now and ever:
O Joy, Hodegetria, grant joy to those who sing to you with
fear and awe. You are the Mother of that Joy which delivers us
445

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

from all sorrow and who have mercy on all those who hasten
to you.

Ode 3.

Irmos. O Theotokos, O living and overflowing fountain,
strengthen those who assembled in a spiritual choir to sing
hymns of praise to you, and, in the feast of your conception of
the Divine One, grant to them the crowns of glory.
O Rejoice, unshakeable, immaculate, and inspired Palace
for Christ, the King in the highest. Rejoice, Hodegetria.
Rejoice, to you through whom our city has been preserved
intact.
O Virgin Hodegetria, you contained in your immaculate
womb Him Whom creation cannot contain. Therefore,
rendering what we owe to you, we sing: Rejoice, we extol you!
Glory:
O joy of the world whom the multitudes praise! Pure
Lady, ever do we sing to you with joy. We have been deemed
worthy of lasting joy by the maternal prayers you offer the
One to Whom you gave birth, O Hodegetria.
Now and ever:
We petition you, O pure one: the golden container,
the candelabrum, the staff, and the altar, O Hodegetria.
Pronouncing these titles and with the invocation: Rejoice, we
ever call upon you.

Sessional Hymn, Tone 2:
A warm prayer-house and an insurmountable wall, a
source of mercy, a refuge for the world, we sincerely call to
You: Our Lady, Theotokos, hasten and save us from disaster,
the only imminent intercessor.

Another Kontakion, in the same tone:
Steadfast Protrectress of Christians, unshakable

Ikos:

and grant to our souls your mercy which is inexhaustible; for

and evil. Therefore, as one who has the graces of mercy,
hasten to intercede and hear our supplication, interceding
always, Theotokos, in behalf of those who honor you.

Lady, but receive the prayers of your servant, because sorrow

Canon to the Most Holy Theotokos Hodegetria

After this,

The Prayer to the Most Holy Lady Theotokos:
O Theotokos my most holy Lady, I your worthless servant,
I beg you: by your holy and all-powerful prayers rid my heart of
all despair, of all sluggishness and slowness in understanding,
of all negligence, of all evil and crafty thoughts. By your mighty
prayers cleanse my clouded mind and bruised heart of all this.
Put out the flames of all my passions. Free me from memories
of evils long gone by. Rescue me from every tendency to do
wrong. Behold my need, my Lady; behold my sorrow! In your
goodness help me, for blessed are you by all peoples, and your
all-honored name is glorified forever. Amen.

to the Holy Apostles
On Wednesday evening, at O Lord, I have cried:
Stichera, Tone 4:
According to: As valiant among the martyrs
(Jako dobl’a:  
)
O most praiseworthy disciples, as eyewitnesses and
testifiers of the Incarnate Word, you are blessed, for as brilliant
lightning you appear upon the world. As spiritual mountains
you carve delights for us. As the ever-flowing, parted rivers
of paradise you give to the Church of the Gentiles the divine
waters to drink.
As the rays that are resplendent with the radiance of the
Spirit, you were sent into the whole world. You have worked
an abundance of miracles. You were the ministers of the
mysteries of Christ, and the God-written tablets of the divine
grace inscribed with the God-instructed law, O praiseworthy
priest-servants.
The rod of the fisherman has brought into order the
wanderings of philosophers and the long-windedness of
orators, for having clearly expounded the Gospel in the Godwise teachings, the doctrine of grace, and of the gracious
Mysteries, as well as the communion of the Eternal Food, the
delight of angels and the ever-abiding glory.

Service to the Holy Apostles

O ray of light that illuminates the ends of the earth and is truly
the golden light, perfectly beautiful and unblemished that has
shone forth the Never-ending Light to the faithful.

CANON TO THE HOLY APOSTLES
A Composition of Kyr Theophane.
Tone 4. Ode 1.
Irmos. With dry feet Israel marched across the dark abyss
of the sea. Moses’ hands, uplifted like a cross, crushed the
power of Amalech in the desert.
456

Service to the Holy Apostles

Versicle: Holy apostles, pray to God for us.
O heavenly trumpeters of the Comforter, You always
proclaim Him with a divine trumpet. Sing a hymn for us, for
it will bring salvation, O blessed apostles of Christ.
I am lying on a bed of laziness, and in my sinful death I
have fallen ill with a terrible, sinful disease. Make me worthy
by your visitations, O glorious eyewitnesses of Christ.
Glory:
With the Word you filled the dumb tongues with speech,
O apostles. Enlighten my heart with the goodness of the
Comforter, for it is chained by dumb deeds.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
After bearing a child you were still a perfect virgin. You
bore the Word Who came to earth especially for us. Pray to
Him worthily to enlighten our souls!

Ode 3.
Irmos: The Church rejoices in You, Christ, and sings:
You are my strenghth, O Lord, my shelter, and my assurance.
O God, through the streams of Your verbal rivers—Your
disciples, O Master, give sacred joy to Your city.
In the company of the leaders of the spiritual armies,
deliver us from all sorrow, O truly glorious apostles and
citizens of heaven.
Glory:
Having established the heavens as witnesses, Christ,

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

establish me on the foundation of Your will by their prayers.

Now and ever: Theotokion:
