grant us Your mercies.

Ode 4.

Irmos. The Church saw You, the Sun of Justice, raised
on the cross. May her children stand in order and sing as they
ought: glory to Your power, O Lord.
You drove Your warrior steeds on the sea, O Lover of
Mankind, and they churned the waters of heresy and teach
Your pure dogma to all.
You have enlightened the minds of the Church, O starsglorious apostles, through your piety. Deliver me from the
night of sin and ignorance.
Glory:
You were made to be sharp arrows, O apostles. Cut
down the flying darts of my wickedness. Strengthen my
understanding.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
O Christ, through the prayers of the one who bore You,
and of the prayers of the holy apostles, heal my soul with
soothing deeds. It has been sickened by poison from the biting
enemy.

Ode 5.

Irmos. You came into the world as a light, my Lord—a
Holy Light which dispels murky ignorance from those who
faithfully praise You.
458

Service to the Holy Apostles

O glorious apostles, you are the living branches and the

You will guide those who foolishly live in the darkness

Glory:
Deliver us from sin in our souls, and from the coming

Now and ever: Theotokion:
Save me, O God, since You love mankind. Save me

Ode 6.
Irmos. I will offer a sacrifice of praise To You, O Lord.

The sheep of the Good Shepherd, chosen by God Himself,
have scattered over the face of the earth. They have tamed the
ferocity of wolves by faith. It has been turned to the meekness
of sheep.
O apostles, you are the fruitful trees of the Divine Paradise.
Bring the miserable barrenness of my soul to charitable deeds.
Glory:

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

I was wounded by the weapon of passion and died. You

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Lord, you have received your steadfast and inspired
preachers, the foremost of Your apostles, into the enjoyment

Ode 7.

Irmos. Abraham’s children were cast into a Persian
furnace. Not from fear of the burning flames but from piety
did they sing: Blessed are You, O Lord, in the temple of Your

By the power of all-holy preaching, forthright apostles of
Christ, you defeated the winter of deceit and enlightened the
thoughts of the believers with an understanding of God.
You exude delightfully fragrant myrrh. O divine disciples,
fill those who come to you with spiritual and fragrant myrrh.
Destroy the stench of evil passion.
Glory:

Service to the Holy Apostles

Ode 8.
Irmos. When Daniel lifted up his hands, he shut the lion’s
mouths. These young bastions of holiness put on virtue and
quenched the power of fire. They sang: All you works of the
Lord, bless the Lord!
O fiery mouth of Christ which closed malignant mouths,
you have spoken saving doctrine. Deliver us from the mouth
of the wolf as we sing: All you works of the Lord, bless the
Lord and praise Him forever!
O harmonious Trumpets of Christ, peal over my dead
soul, O apostles. Raise me from the grave of despair and from
sin’s discouragement as I sing: All you works of the Lord,
bless the Lord, and praise Him forever!
Glory:
O Christ, through the prayers of Your disciples, do not
judge me for breaking Your laws through a lewd mind; me,
O Master, the prodigal, who descended to the depths and
succumbed to the temptations of the devil.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Lady of all creatures, O Mary, free me by your prayers,
for I am possessed by the devil. I am always sinning. Placate
Christ so that I may sing in a pure life: All you works of the
Lord, bless the Lord, and praise Him forever!

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Ode 9.
Irmos. That stone which came untouched from an
unquarried mountain has become the cornerstone which came
from you, O Virgin. Christ took flesh and unites Himself to
creation. We rejoice in this, and we praise you, O Theotokos.
O chosen stones which have been set upon the Cornerstone,
shape the hearts of the faithful by that rock of faith which has
crushed the enemy to powder, O apostles.
You received the power to bind and loose from Christ.
Loosen the ties of my wickedness, and bind me to God’s love.
Make me an heir of the kingdom of heaven, O apostles.
Glory:
O heavenly clouds from the Master, rain on me, and make
my heart fertile. It is drying out from all kinds of evil works,
O apostles blessed by God.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
With the glorious martyrs, the heavenly apostles and the
holy angels, O Theotokos most pure, implore your Son and
God to save our souls from danger.

Prayer.
Master, Lord, Yours is the day, and Yours is the night;
all creatures serve You, and everything that lives gives glory
to You. I, a wretched one, have spent all my life prodigally.
I am possessed by fear when I remember my first days to the
present in which I committed all wicked and dissolute evil,
and that is the reason I do not have access to Your confidence
462

Service to the Holy Apostles

since my offenses are great and my sins are without limit, and
enemies are always oppressing me. But, my Lord, Lord, Who
opened the mouth of those without speech, open my mouth
that I may say in prayer what is pleasing to You. My soul is
like parched land without water, and it cannot yield its fruits.
But grant me fruit from the seed of Your Holy Spirit and water
me with the dew of Your grace that I might bring forth for
You the fruits of repentance. O Lord Jesus Christ, You Who
desire that all men be saved, listen to my prayer through the
prayers of Your holy apostles since they pray for us, and I
ask for forgiveness with confidence because of them, for You
ever listen to their prayers. Through their prayers, save me,
a sinner, heal the infirmities of my heart, cure the wounds
of my soul, burn my inner being with the fire of fear of You
that it may consume the thorns of my sins, and console my
soul with love. Because I desire You, True Light and Giver
of Light, from You alone I ask for mercy: save me! Feed my
hunger and give drink to my thirsty soul from the source of
Your boundless mercy. Cover me with the grace of Your love
for mankind from all evil so that I, protected by You, may be
freed from the snares of the wicked one for the rest of my
days, so that my enemies cannot boast over me, Your servant
who trusts in You. Save me according to Your mercy, that I
may give You my promise: until my last breath I repent over
my sins and glorify Your Most Holy Name, with the Father,
and the Holy Spirit, now and ever, and forever. Amen.
Then, if a Moleben: It is truly proper: Trisagion. And,
after Our Father: the Troparion of the apostles. Glory: now
and ever: Theotokion. And the Dismissal.

Service
to Holy Bishop Nicholas
On Wednesday evening, at Lord, I have called:
Stichera, Tone 2.
According to: What crowns of praise:
(Kiimi pochval’nymi:  

)

What crowns of praise shall we confer upon the saintly
Bishop? Once present in the flesh in Myra, he is present in
spirit to all who love him purely. He is the leader and defender
of everyone, a comforter in distress and a haven of all in
danger, a pillar of piety and conqueror for believers. For his
sake, Christ overcame enemies and shows us great mercy.
With what songs of praise shall we extol the saintly
Bishop? He is the foe of wickedness. He is an outstanding
leader, a great defender and teacher of the Church. He
confounds all who show dishonor. He is the refuter of Arius
and his companions. Because of him, Christ put down their
ragings and showed great mercy.
With what hymns of prophecy shall we extol the saintly
Bishop? Living in the present, he saw far into the future. He
spoke truly about distant things as though they were near.
464

Service to Holy Bishop Nicholas

He oversees the whole world and delivers the afflicted. He
appeared in a dream to the God-wise king. He delivered
prisoners who were unjustly accused of murder. Today he
grants us the mercy of Christ.
Glory: Tone 6:
We have gathered together to celebrate and to praise
with song the model of bishops and a glory to the fathers, a
fountain of miracles and a great helper of believers. Let us
sing to the saintly Nicholas: Rejoice, O Protector of Myra
who was revered as its leader and strongest pillar. Rejoice, O
Radiant Star Whose light of miracles shines throughout the
world. Rejoice, O Divine Joy to those in sorrow. Rejoice, O
Defender of those who are oppressed; for even now, all-holy
Nicholas, you still pray to God for us who celebrate your feast
with faith and who honor you with zeal and joy.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Who would not extol you, most holy Virgin? Who would
not praise your giving birth without pain? For the onlybegotten Son, Who shines forth from the Father timelessly,
has himself come forth from you, O pure one. He took flesh
from you in a manner beyond understanding; retaining divine
nature, but assuming human nature for our sake; not divided
into two persons but existing in two natures distinct and
unconfused. O honored and most blessed one, beseech him to
have mercy on our souls.
At the Aposticha, Tone 5:
According to: Rejoice:
(Radujsja:
)
Rejoice, O priestly leader, spotless vessel of virtue, model
of divine priesthood, great shepherd of your flock, bearer of
465

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

the torch of victory. You hear the prayers of those who call
upon you; you grant the petitions of the poor; you deliver
all the faithful who honor your all-glorious memory. Pray to
Christ, most blessed one, that He may shower abundant mercy
on the world.
Verse: Precious in the eyes of the Lord is the death of His
faithful. [Psalm 115:6]
Rejoice, O saintly Hierarch, pure temple of the Trinity;
pillar of the Church, protector of the faithful, helper of all in
trouble. You are a star whose rays of prayer dispel the darkest
trouble. O holy father Nicholas, you are a quiet harbor for the
storm-tossed, for all adrift in the sea of life. Pray to Christ to
save our souls with his great mercy.
Verse: Your priests will be clothed with holiness; Your
faithful shall ring out their joy. [Psalm 131:9]
Rejoice, O man filled with divine zeal. You appeared in a
dream, and you saved from death the ones unjustly sentenced.
You are a fountain in Myra, O Nicholas, overflowing with
precious myrrh. You inspire us to keep from sin. You are a
sword that cuts down the weeds of error; you proved Arius to
be a false teacher. Pray to Christ to save our souls in His great
mercy.
Glory: Tone 6:
O man of God, O faithful servant of the Lord, you are a
chosen vessel filled with desire for God. You are a pillar and a
foundation of the Church; you are an heir of the kingdom. [O
holy Father Nicholas,] pray to the Lord for us.

O Theotokos, you are the True Vine who gave birth to the

mercy for our souls.

Tone 4. Ode 1.
Irmos. I will open my mouth. It will be filled by the

Versicle: Holy Father Nicholas, pray to God for us.
Rejoice, Nicholas, good shepherd of Christ’s flock. You
were a teacher and father dear to Myra’s people. Grant me to

All generations of the earth gathered to sing “Rejoice,” O
Bishop, for you bring joy abundantly to the universe.
Glory:
Since you delivered three generals from unjust execution,
we sing to you: Rejoice, Nicholas, defender of those who run
to your protection.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Rejoice, Virgin Theotokos. You received joy from the
angel, so save those who extol you.

Ode 3.
Irmos. O Theotokos, O living and overflowing fountain,

No one who seeks the shelter of your trust goes away
empty-handed, father. By greeting you, one receives help, O
Nicholas. Grant me your help as well, O all-blessed one.

Service to Holy Bishop Nicholas

O venerable father, the angels marvel at your ardent care.

Glory:
You are a helmet and an armor of invulnerability against

Now and ever: Theotokion:
You conceived your own Creator, O Theotokos, and you

Ode 4.
Irmos. He Who sits in glory on the throne of the Godhead,

O Christ!
At the throne you are equal to any apostle. Rejoice,
Nicholas, for you have shamed the heresy of Arius. You

You delivered a child from the hands of the Saracen Emir,
and you gave joy to his parents. Therefore, together with
them, we sing to you: Rejoice!
Glory:
O Wonderworker, you saved three generals from unjust

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

execution. You appeared in a dream to the pious king, and

Rejoice, most blessed Theotokos, for you are the throne

Ode 5.
Irmos. The universe was in awe at your divine glory, for

Son, you who grants peace to those who sing to you.
O chosen Apostle of God, you stand on an equal footing

O Nicholas, extend a helping hand to me. Pray to the

Glory:
Despite my many sins, O Nicholas, I never abandoned
hope for your protection. I always rejoice in you. Deliver me
from all trouble and sorrow, for you can do whatever you will.
Now and ever: Theotokion:

Service to Holy Bishop Nicholas

Ode 6.

Irmos. By divine inspiration, the God-wise celebrate
this all-honorable and God-given feast of the Mother of God.
Come, clap your hands, and let us praise God Whom she bore.
You have been revealed as a second Peter and a friend of
Christ, O father. Rejoice, for you are a pillar of the Church and
a wondrous trumpet. You work miracles and resound with the
Holy Spirit. Therefore, O Nicholas, we always sing to you:
Rejoice!
In a dream the pious king Constantine and the eparch
Ablabius heard your warning about the men they intended
to execute unjustly. He immediately commanded them to be
released, and he cried out to you, Nicholas: Rejoice!
Glory:
You became the pilot of that floundering ship at sea, O
father. Put a good thought in my mind and heart when I am
tossed on the waves of the devil’s thoughts, so that I may
always praise you: Rejoice, Nicholas, worthy of praise.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Rejoice, most pure Virgin. Rejoice, fortress of the world.
Rejoice to you who gave birth to a Son Who is the God of all.
Now beseech Him O all-immaculate Theotokos, to save our souls.

Ode 7.

Irmos. Wise in God, they served no creature in place of
God. They overcame the flaming menace with confidence.
They rejoiced and sang: Blessed are You and praiseworthy, O
Lord and God of our fathers!
O holy Nicholas, O bishop of Christ, rejoice! You are
unspeakable joy to all. Give me a helping hand that I too may
say: Rejoice, all-blessed one.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

When the generals heard that you had them freed, they
took candles to you, singing with a loud voice: Rejoice,

Glory:
At one time you heard those chained in prison. Hear me

Now and ever: Theotokion:
O Lady Mary, Mother of the Savior, deliver me, I am

Ode 8.

Irmos. The Offspring of the maternity of the Theotokos
saved the three young men in the furnace. Then, it was a

exalt Him forever.
You are enthroned with the apostles. You serve the Trinity
with the angels. Rejoice most-praiseworthy Nicholas! Grant

Rejoice, O Nicholas, helmsman of those caught in the

I cannot bear them any longer. I call out: Rejoice, my helper
and my steadfast intercessor.
Glory:
How much sadness fills me because of those flying arrows
of the devil. I cannot bear the wounds! There is no doctor
to bandage me. But apply the oil of your prayers and the
bandage of your intercession, O Nicholas, and let me call to
you: Rejoice, O venerable father.

Service to Holy Bishop Nicholas

Rejoice, unburnt bush which Moses saw, and Sinai

Ode 9.
Irmos. Let everyone on earth dance for joy in spirit. Let
the bodiless powers solemnly celebrate in honor of the sacred
feast. O Mother of God, let them cry out: Rejoice, ever-blessed
Theotokos and pure Ever-Virgin.
Sinful desires and the piercing arrows of the tempter
possess me. Hoping for your protection, O Father, I run to
you. Dispel the deceitfulness of the evil one from me, so that
I may sing to you: Rejoice, O Nicholas.
You made a fool of Arius. You extinguished the blaze of
heresy. You heard the generals chained in prison and accepted
their rejoicing. They praise you, and we sing to you: Rejoice,
Nicholas, all-blessed one.
Glory:
You heard the prayers of Agricus, and rescued his son
Basil from the Emir. You restored him from the Saracens to
his parents safe in one moment. As for me, who pray to you,
free my sick soul from the fire of Gehenna, for it is covered
with sin and sorely grieved, O Nicholas.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
You are the Queen who gave birth to the King of the
universe. You bore Him Who bears creation. Save me, most
holy Lady, who extol you.

Hymn of Light
According to: O Women hear:
(Ženy uslyšite:  

)

Let us all praise Nicholas, the great shepherd, bishop,
and leader of Myra, for he saved many who were unjustly
condemned to death. He also appeared to the emperor and
Ablabius in a dream, putting an end to the unjust decree.
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
O Virgin, you gave birth to Christ, Wisdom personified,
the ever-existing Word, and Healer of all. Heal the wounds of
my soul and remove from my heart all lustful thoughts.

Prayer to Saint Nicholas.

O all-holy Nicholas, pre-eminent servant of the Lord, our
warm-hearted Protector, and Helper swift to assist those in
troubles everywhere, help me who am a sinner and dejected
in this present life. Implore the Lord God to grant me release
from all my sins, for from my youth and in all my life I
have sinned by deed, in word and thought, and with all my
emotions. At the departure of my soul, help me, a pitiful
being: beg the Lord God Who is the Creator of every living
being to free me from defrauding like the publican and from
everlasting torment, so that I may praise always the Father,
Son, and Holy Spirit, and your merciful intercession, now and
ever and forever. Amen.

Prayer to our Lord Jesus Christ
O Lord Jesus Christ, Son of the living God, Creator of
heaven and earth, Savior of the world: Behold, I, the unworthy
one, and the one more sinful than everyone else, I bend the
knees of my heart before the glory of Your majesty. I praise
and magnify Your limitless suffering and give thanks to You,
the King and God of all, since it pleased You to willingly
come down from Your heavenly throne, and become incarnate
486

Service to the Precious and Life-Creating Cross of Christ

of the Most Holy Virgin Mary for the salvation of the human
race. Being bodiless, You united divinity to flesh. Being rich,
You voluntarily became poor in order to enrich Man in Your
kingdom. As man, You brought on Yourself the toils and every
misfortune of the human state in order to assist in every sorrow
and need. You Who fasted forty days showed everyone the
way to moderation. Multiple times You were tested by the evil
one; You free everyone from every temptation.
I know, all-powerful Master, that You did not need all of
this, yet You suffered for the sake of the salvation of the human
race. You were betrayed for thirty pieces of silver to redeem
mankind from the oppressive weight of hostile slavery. Being
maltreated by ruthless people as the Innocent Lamb, You
liberated the human race from the destruction of the spiritual
cruel man. Being presented before the judgment seat of Annas
and Caiaphas, You freed everyone from the eternal fire. Being
bound, mocked, spat upon, defamed by false witnesses, and
condemned to an infamous death, You freed mankind from
every assault, suffering, and eternal death. Being given over
to Pilate although You did not commit any evil, and sent to
Herod, and again mocked, You freed mankind from the state
of evil and from hostile mockeries.
I do not know what can I return to You, O Master and
Lover of Mankind, for all that You have suffered for me, a
sinner. My soul and body, and all good, are from You, and
what is mine is Yours, and I am Yours. I hope only in Your
unmeasurable compassion, merciful Lord; I praise Your
mercy without limits by which You laid down for me in my
condemned state, in order for me to be justified.
Bound to the pillar, O Savior, and beaten without mercy,
O Merciful One, I pray: absolve me from my sins. Crowned
487

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

with thorns, uproot the sinful thorns of my soul. Beaten upon
the head with the rod, destroy the head of the serpent that
is wounding me with the sting of sin. Dressed in the red
vestment and handed over to the torturers, illumine, O Most
Holy King, my spiritual vestment, so that I may enter into
Your all-beautiful chamber. Being exchanged for robbers and
having brought the cross upon Your shoulders, cast away by
Your cross the robber enemy who is seeking to destroy my
soul. I know that You, long-suffering Jesus, were extremely
tortured: from the top of Your holy head to Your feet, there
was no place undamaged on You.
And what shall I say about Your ineffable love for mankind,
O Christ the Savior? With the grief of my heart, I bow down
to Your most pure sufferings and, by kissing them with all my
love, I cry out: Have mercy on me, a sinner. Having willed to
be nailed to the cross, nail my heart to Your commandments.
Exalted on the cross on the height of Golgotha, raise my
thoughts to heaven, that I may always ponder that which is
on high. Having drunk the gall and vinegar, sweeten my heart
so grieved by sin with Your love; and, being thirsty, give me
to drink with the spring of Your sweetness. Having opened
Your hands to accept everyone, accept me, a sinner. Having
Your feet nailed, always be with sinners; be with me, a sinner,
keeping my feet from every wicked path. Having an open
heart, show me, a sinner, Your grace. Having bowed Your
most holy head on the cross, listen to my unworthy prayers.
O most marvelous and immeasurable depth of mercy,
Christ God, Who prayed to God the Father for Your enemies
who crucified You, grant to me, a sinner, the grace to love my
enemies and pray for them. Having opened paradise to the
thief who repented, look, my Light, upon me, a sinner; give
488

Service to the Precious and Life-Creating Cross of Christ

me repentance, and open to me the doors of Your mercy and
remember me, the unworthy one, in Your kingdom.
At the end, having delivered Your most Holy Spirit into
the hands of God the Father, accept, O Creator, my spirit at
the time of my death. Being taken down from the cross and
placed as dead in the tomb, O Savior, living in the inaccessible
world, take away from me the heavy sinful burden; and do
not disdain, O Lover of Mankind, to dwell in the tomb of
my unworthy heart in order to put to death my rational flesh.
So that I do not live by myself, Your creature, but with You,
my Lord and God. I hope in Your mercy, O Merciful One,
to see You, my Creator and Savior, Who is crowned with
glory and honor in the world of Your inaccessible glory for
accepting death on a cross, where You reign before the ages
with Your Father Who is without beginning, and Your most
Holy, gracious, and Life-giving, Spirit, one in essence, now
and ever and forever. Amen.
It is truly proper: Trisagion. And after Our Father:
Troparion: Save your people, O Lord: Glory: now and ever:
Stavrotheotokion.
And the Dismissal.

On Friday evening, at: Lord, I have cried: the stichera,
Tone 8:
Today all the faithful commemorate the forefathers. Sing
with fervor a hymn of praise to Christ the Savior Who exalted
them among all nations. He is the Lord Who does wondrous
deeds, because He is powerful and mighty. From them He
brought forth a royal scepter, the immaculate maiden of God
and virgin Mary. From her, Christ our God came forth to give
life and eternal salvation for all.
The prophets and apostles of Christ and the martyrs have
taught us to hymn the Trinity, One in essence. They have
enlightened mistaken peoples, and have given to the children
of humans a communion with the angels.
You hierarchs for the Lord, who have spread the holy and
divine Word, crush all heterodox and heretical words. You
have become the first laborers for the faithful; for this we
venerate you.
O God bearing fathers, you are like the orders of the
bodiless angels. In a physical body you mirror their life. For
this you have gone to live with them.

heal the ulcerations of all the faithful.
Glory:
O Lord, You enlightened Your hierarchs and priestmartyrs, and all the saints. Through their prayers be gracious
with me. You know my immeasurable sins.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Most pure Virgin, you are the praise of the martyrs and
the venerable men and women, and the righteous, and all
the saints. Deliver me, I pray you, from all hostile evil of the
betrayer.

Ode 6.

Irmos. Grant to me a robe of light, O most Merciful Christ
our God. You clothe yourself with light as with a garment.
You appear like the star-bright dawn upon the earth, most
glorious armor-bearers of Christ and righteous hierarchs. You
have enlightened the faithful with the light of your virtue.
You were killed by many wounds. You inherited eternal
life. Therefore, O you holy martyrs pray to Christ to save all
the faithful.
495

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Glory:
O Christ, You are the glory of the most-wise hierarchs,
the venerable men and women, and all the saints. Through
their prayers, be compassionate with Your people. For You
acquired them by Your blood and love for mankind.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
You rejoice in God, O Lady, and we the faithful sing to
you. You gave birth to the ever-hymned God. Pray to Him to
preserve your city and its people in peace, O most pure one.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
To You, O Lord, Gardener of all creation, the world
offers the God-bearing martyrs as the first-fruits of nature.
Through their prayers and through the Theotokos, preserve
Your Church, Your dwelling place, in perfect peace, O most
merciful One.

Ikos:
Those who have borne witness over all the earth have
now become citizens of heaven; having imitated the Passion
of Christ, they deliver us from our passions. They are reunited
today in the world beyond, and they show how the Church of
the First-born bears the image of the heavenly assembly. To
Christ, they cry out: You are my God. Through the one who
gave you birth, O Lord, preserve me, O Most Merciful One.

Ode 7.
Irmos. The pious God-fearing young men did not bow
down to the golden idol in Babylon, but they were showered
with dew in the midst of the furnace flames, and singing a
hymn, they said: Blessed are You, O God of our fathers, and
praised and exalted forever.
496

Service to All Saints

You delight in the heavenly banquet, O orders of saints.
You praise the One Who rests among the holy ones with a
great voice, and rejoicing, you sing: Blessed are You, O God
of our fathers.
Brightly-radiant hierarchs, and the righteous ones, and the
prophets, worthy-wonderworking priest-martyrs, and those
who have shown forth light in fasting, ever pray for us that we
receive mercy from the One to Whom we sing: Blessed are
You, O God of our fathers.
Glory:
We rejoice and praise the assembly of all Your saints, O
Lord, who have been gathered from all over the world, and
out of every nation. We praise them, with their virtues and
deeds, and we sing to You: Blessed are You, O God of our
fathers.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
O most pure one, with the martyrs, with the venerable
fathers, with the prophets and all the saints, implore the One
Who rests among the saints to sanctify all of us who glorify
you forever.

Ode 8.
Irmos. The young men, speaking in behalf of God in the
furnace, ignored the flaming fire. They sang: All you works of
the Lord, bless the Lord!
O holy fathers, prophets, apostles, martyrs, and all you
saints, you have completed the spiritual warfare. You have
arrived to the holy dwelling with the angels. With them ask
absolution and great mercy for us all.
497

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

O venerable men and women, you have mortified the
flesh by many sufferings. You have been made worthy of the
coming life. You have pleased God. We pray you to pray that
we, too, may obtain the same life.
Glory:
Your priests, O Christ, are clothed reverently with
righteousness, and all the saints of all ages now rejoice
together. [cf. Psalm 131:9]. Now they see the divine goodness
more clearly, O Lover of Mankind; make us worthy to see it
through the intercession of all Your saints.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
O pure Theotokos, join with all the prophets, and martyrs,
and the venerable ones and priest-martyrs, and with all the
saints to pray to the all-merciful Savior to be merciful to us.

Ode 9.
Irmos. We who have been saved through you profess
that you are truly the Theotokos, O pure Virgin, and with the
choirs of the bodiless ones we extol you.
With holy hymns we bless the shepherds in their priestly
work, the choir of holy prophets, the countless number of
ascetics, the assembly of martyrs, fasters, virgins, and all the
saints. Implore the Master of all to save our souls.
You are priests of His mysteries and ministers of the
Master. You have joined the ministers of heaven. We beg you
to pray with us for us.
Glory:
We extol the venerable men and women and righteous
ones, with the virgins and the holy women who led exemplary
lives, in the company of the priest-martyrs, and all the
prophets. O Christ, deliver our souls from hell.
498

Service to All Saints

Now and ever: Theotokion:
You gave birth in the flesh to the generous and loving
God. With all the saints ever pray Him to save us from danger,
O pure Virgin and Mother, for we bless you always.
At the Stichera of the Praises, Tone 4:
O Lord, all creation celebrates the memory of your saints.
The heavens with the angels rejoice and the earth with its
people are glad. Through their prayers, have mercy on us.
O glorious apostles, who enlightened the universe, we
pray to you: always pray to Christ our Lord and God to save
our souls.
We pray to you, O praiseworthy prophets who stand
before the throne of God, we praise your precious memory.
Pray fervently that God give us enlightenment, wisdom, and
faith.
Glory:
You are the glory, O Christ, of the ancient patriarchs,
the famed prophets, the all-praised apostles, the victorious
martyrs, the wise hierarchs, and all the priest-teachers, the
diligent choir of venerables, all the ranks of the righteous,
and all the saints. Through their prayers, give mercy to Your
people which You possess with your blood for You are the
Lover of Mankind.
Now and ever:
We sing to you, blessed, pure Virgin Theotokos. Through
you the Never-setting Sun shines on those in darkenss and
in the shadow of death’s justice. With all the saints you are
especially the mediatrix of our salvation.
499

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Prayer.
Holy God Who dwells among the saints, You are
acclaimed in heaven by the thrice-holy voice of angels,
praised on earth by Your holy men and women. Through Your
Holy Spirit, You gave grace to each according to the measure
of the gift of Christ, and with that grace You established Your
holy Church, where some are apostles, some prophets, some
evangelizers, some pastors and teachers with their word of
preaching; to You, the same God, [we praise] Who accomplish
all things in all, many became saints, from every generation
to generation who were pleasing to You through their varied
good deeds, and have left us the memory of their heroic good
deeds in which they were offered to You. They are ready to
respond joyfully to help us who are in distress. Remembering
all these saints, and praising their God-pleasing lives, I praise
You Who both inspired their will, and worked to bring about
Your will to accomplish the deeds, and other good deeds, that
I believe were possible because You granted them. Grant that
I, a sinner, may follow their teaching, life, will, faith, longsuffering, and love, and through their prayerful intercession,
Your grace which accomplishes all things in all, to inherit
with them the glory of heaven, and to praise Your most holy
Name, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, forever. Amen.
After this: It is truly proper: Trisagion. After Our Father:
Troparion: God of our fathers: and the Theotokion: The
mystery hidden from all ages: see page 491.
And the dismissal.

Service of the Resurrection
OF THE SIXTH TONE.
AT GREAT VESPERS.
At O Lord, I have cried: we interpolate ten stichera, and
we sing the appointed stichera of the Resurrection, Tone 6:
Verse: Bring my soul out of this prison and then I shall
praise Your Name.
O Christ, You are victorious over Hades. You ascended the
cross to raise up with Yourself those who sat in the darkness
of death. You alone are free among the dead; from Your own
light, You well up with life, All-powerful Savior, have mercy
on us.
Verse: Around me the just will assemble because of Your
goodness to me.
Today Christ has trampled death! He arose as He foretold,
and bestowed rejoicing upon the world. So let us all sing this,
our hymn: O Wellspring of Life, O Unapproachable Light,
all-powerful Savior, have mercy on us.
501

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Verse: Out of the depths I cry to You, O Lord; Lord, hear
my voice!
Where can we sinners flee from You, O Lord, Who are
present in all creation; to the heavens? – that is where You
dwell; to Hades? – there You trampled death; to the depths of
the sea? – even there is Your hand! We flee to You and, falling
before You, we beg: O Lord, risen from the dead, have mercy
on us.
Additional Anatolian [Eastern] stichera, in the same tone.
Verse: Let Your ears be attentive to the voice of my
pleading.
We exalt in Your cross, O Christ, and we sing the glory
of Your Resurrection. For You are our God, and we have no
other Lord but You.
Verse: If You, O Lord, should mark our guilt, Lord, who
would survive? But with You is found forgiveness: for this we
revere You.
Glory to Your might, O Lord, for You have conquered
the power of death. You have renewed us through Your cross,
granting us life and incorruption.
Verse: My soul is waiting for the Lord. I count on His
word. My soul is longing for the Lord more than watchman
for daybreak.
We forever bless the Lord and praise His resurrection, for
by suffering crucifixion, He has destroyed Death by His death.

502

Service of the Resurrection

Verse: Let the watchman count on daybreak and Israel on
the Lord.
By Your death and burial, O Lord, You broke asunder the
bonds of Hades; and by Your resurrection from the dead, You
enlightened the whole world. We therefore exclaim to You:
Glory to You, O Lord.
Then, the stichera of the saint from the Menaion. Glory:
of the saint if they are available; if they are not, Glory: now
and ever: Theotokion.
Here are other stichera of the Theotokos, composed by
Paul of Amora, in Tone 3:
Verse: Because with the Lord there is mercy and fullness
of redemption, Israel indeed He will redeem from all its
iniquity.
Seeing my physical weakness, spiritual suffering and
heartache, Immaculate Virgin, make me worthy of God’s
deliverance. I beg you save me by your fervent prayers.
Verse: Praise the Lord, all you nations, acclaim Him all
you peoples!
Make me worthy of mercy at the judgment seat of your
Son and God, O Virgin, when He comes.
Verse: Strong is the love of the Lord for us; He is faithful
forever.
Wash away the multitude of all my sins, O Lady, I beg
you. Chop down the rough surges of my passions by the
sword of your prayers. I will sing of your virginal conception
with faith and love.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
Who would not extol you, most holy Virgin? Who would
not praise your giving birth without pain? For the onlybegotten Son, Who shines forth from the Father timelessly,
has Himself come forth from you, O pure one. He took flesh
from you in a manner beyond understanding; retaining divine
nature, but assuming human nature for our sake; not divided
into two persons but existing in two natures distinct and
unconfused. O honored and most blessed one, beseech Him to
have mercy on our souls.
The Entrance: O Joyful Light: The Prokeimenon of the
Day: The Lord reigns: and the rest as usual.
At the Aposticha stichera, Tone 6:
O Christ our Savior, the angels in heaven sing the praises
of Your resurrection; make us on earth also worthy to extol
and glorify You with a pure heart.
In Alphabetic order:
Verse: The Lord reigns, He is clothed in majesty.
Almighty God, You destroyed the brazen gates and bars
of Hades, and raised up fallen mankind.Therefore, with one
accord we cry out: O Lord risen from the dead, glory to You.
Verse: For He has made the world firm, not to be moved.
Christ willed to renew us from our corruption of old by
being nailed to a cross and placed in a tomb. When the women
came to anoint his body, they tearfully cried out: O what
504

Service of the Resurrection

sorrow afflicts us! O Savior of all, how could You consent
to rest in a grave? If You truly willed this, why then did You
allow Your body to be stolen? How were You removed? What
place now conceals Your life-bearing body? O Lord, appear
to us as You promised, and put an end to our tears. As they
were lamenting, an angel appeared and cried out to them: Do
not weep, but tell the apostles that the Lord is risen, granting
sanctification and great mercy to the world.
Verse: Holiness befits Your house, O Lord, for the length
of days.
O Christ, You were crucified of Your own free will and by
Your burial, You imprisoned death. As God, You rose in glory
on the third day granting life and great mercy to the world.
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
Christ the Lord, our Creator and Redeemer, came forth
from your womb, O Virgin most pure. He clothed himself in
our human flesh to set us free from the original curse of Adam.
Therefore, O Mary, we praise you without ceasing as the true
Virgin Theotokos, and we sing with the angels: Rejoice, O
Lady: advocate, protector and salvation of souls.
Then, Now You may dismiss: Trisagion, and after Our
Father: we say the Troparion of the Resurrection, Tone 6:
Angelic powers appeared at Your tomb, and the guards
became like dead men. Mary stood at the tomb seeking Your
most pure body. You despoiled Hades without a challenge.
You, the Giver of Life, met the Virgin. O Lord, risen from the
dead, glory to You.
505

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
Christ, Who called you “Mother” and “Blessed One,”
accepted the Passion of His own free will. In His desire to find
the fallen Adam, He caused light to shine forth from His cross
in order to search him out. Then He said to the angels: Rejoice
with me, for I have found the lost piece of silver. Glory to
You, O God, Who accomplished all things in such wisdom.

AT MATINS.
After the Six Psalms: The Lord is God: in Tone 6, and we
say the Troparion: Angelic powers appeared at your tomb:
twice. Glory: now and ever: Christ, Who called you “Mother”
and “Blessed One”: and the usual stichologia of the Psalter.
After the 1st Stichologion, the Sessional Hymn of the
Resurrection, Tone 6:
When the tomb was shown to be open and Hades was
lamenting, Mary cried out to the apostles who were hiding
and said: Come out, laborers of the vineyard, and proclaim the
news of the Resurrection; for the Lord is risen, granting the
world great mercy.
Verse: Arise, O Lord, lift up Your hand. O God, do not
forget the poor.
Mary Magdalene stood by Your tomb and wept, O Lord.
When she thought You were the gardener, she said: Where
have You hidden the eternal Life? Where have You placed
Him Who sits on the throne of the cherubim? When she saw
those guarding Him fearful and appearing as dead, she cried
506

Service of the Resurrection

to them: Give me my Lord or else cry out with me and say:
You have come forth from the tomb, and raised the dead, O

Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
O Theotokos, Gideon prefigured your conception, and
David interpreted your birthgiving. As dew descended upon
the fleece so the Word descended into your womb. O holy
Earth, who without seed gave birth to Christ our God, the
salvation of the world, you are full of grace.
After the 2nd Stichologion, the Sessional Hymn of the
Resurrection, Tone 6:
Truly our Life was placed in the grave, and seals were
applied to the stone. The soldiers guarded Christ as they would
a sleeping king. But, striking His enemies with blindness, the
Lord rose.
Verse: I will praise You, Lord, with all my heart; I will
recount all Your wonders.
Jonah prefigured Your tomb, O immortal Lord, and Simeon
interpreted Your divine Resurrection; for You descended into
the grave as One Who is dead. You, the Master, shattered
the gates of Hades, and free of corruption, You rose for the
salvation of the world. O Christ our God, You give light to
those in darkness.
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
O Virgin and Theotokos, pray to your Son, Christ our
God, Who was willingly nailed upon the cross and rose from
the dead, that He might save our souls.

Antiphon 1:
To the heavens have I lifted up my eyes, O Word of God.
Have mercy on me that I may live in You.
O Word, have mercy on us for we are filled with contempt;
and make us good and chosen vessels.
Glory:
The Holy Spirit is the cause of salvation for all; for when
He breathes on them, He raises them from the cares of this
world. He endows them with wings from on high to carry
them to heaven.
Now and ever: and the same.

Antiphon 2:
Had the Lord not been with us, it would not be possible
for any one of us to stand firm in wrestling with the Enemy;
for only thereby do the victors attain the exaltation of victory.

Service of the Resurrection

Woe is me! How shall I escape the Enemy while I am yet

Glory:
Through the Holy Spirit all are made divine; and in Him

Now and ever: and the same.

Antiphon 3:
They who trust in the Lord are feared by their enemies,

Glory:

Verse: Praise God in his holy place; praise Him in his

Gospel of the Resurrection of Matins
according to Luke, Pericope 114.
At that time: Jesus rose from the dead, and standing in
the midst of the disciples, said to them, “Peace be with you.”
But they were startled and terrified and thought that they were
seeing a ghost. Then he said to them, “Why are you troubled?
And why do questions arise in your hearts? Look at my hands
and my feet, that it is I myself. Touch me and see, because a
ghost does not have flesh and bones as you can see I have.” And
as he said this, he showed them his hands and his feet. While
they were still incredulous for joy and were amazed, he asked
them, “Have you anything here to eat?” They gave him a piece
of baked fish; he took it and ate it in front of them. He said to
them, “These are my words that I spoke to you while I was
still with you, that everything written about me in the law of
Moses and in the prophets and psalms must be fulfilled.” Then
he opened their minds to understand the scriptures. And he
said to them, “Thus it is written that the Messiah would suffer
and rise from the dead on the third day and that repentance,
for the forgiveness of sins, would be preached in his name to
all the nations, beginning from Jerusalem. You are witnesses
of these things. And [behold] I am sending the promise of
my Father upon you; but stay in the city until you are clothed
with power from on high.” Then he led them [out] as far as
Bethany, raised his hands, and blessed them. As he blessed
them he parted from them and was taken up to heaven. They
did him homage and then returned to Jerusalem with great joy,
and they were continually in the temple praising God. Amen.
Then:

510

Service of the Resurrection

Having beheld the resurrection of Christ let us worship the
holy Lord Jesus Who alone is sinless. We bow to Your cross,
O Christ, and we glorify and praise Your holy Resurrection.
You are our God, and besides You we recognize no other,
and we call upon Your Name. Come, all you faithful, and let
us bow to the holy Resurrection of Christ since, through the
cross, joy has come to all the world. Ever praising the Lord,
let us extol His Resurrection since He, having endured the
crucifixion, has destroyed Death by His death.
After the 50th Psalm, Glory:
Through the prayers of the holy apostles, O Merciful One,
cleanse our many sins.
Now and ever:
Through the prayers of the Theotokos, O Merciful One,
cleanse our many sins.
Then, Tone 6:
[Psalm 50:1]
Have mercy on me, God, in Your kindness. In Your
compassion blot out my offense.
Then:
Jesus is risen from the tomb, as He foretold, and granted
us eternal life and great mercy.

Open to me the doors of repentance, O Giver of Life. For

CANON OF THE RESURRECTION.
Tone 6. Ode 1.
Irmos. When the Israelites crossed the abyss as if on dry
land, and saw Pharoah their persecutor drowning in the sea,
they cried out: Let us sing a hymn of victory to our God.
Versicle: Glory to Your holy Resurrection, O Lord.
512

Service of the Resurrection

When You stretched out Your hands on the cross, O God
of goodness, You fulfilled the good will of Your Father. With
one voice we now sing a hymn of victory to You.
At Your order, O Master of life, death approached You as
a servant who is filled with fear; and through death You have
granted us resurrection and eternal life.
Glory:
He stands before Pilate’s judgment seat as He wished.
The Judge is judged; can the trial be lawful? God is slapped
across the face by iniquity’s hand. Creatures of earth and
heaven tremble.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Your Creator desired to become incarnate in your virginal
womb. Incomprehensibly you conceived Him, and you have
become the Lady of creation.

Ode 3.
Irmos. None is as holy as You, O Lord my God; You have
exalted the strength of Your faithful, O Good One, and You
have established us on the unshakeable rock of the confession
of Your Name.
When creation saw God crucified in the flesh, it trembled
with fear; but it was held together by the hand of the One Who
let Himself be crucified for us.
The power of Death has been crushed by death and now
lives without strength; for it could not bear the divine invasion
of Life, and resurrection is granted to the whole world.
513

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Glory:
Glory to Your Resurrection, Savior! You saved us from
death’s decay and from hell. You are almighty! We sing our
song: No one is holy but You, Lord, and You love us!
Now and ever: Theotokion:
You have surpassed the powers of every creature, pure
Lady, by the miracle of your holy conception. You conceived
God in your womb supernaturally, while remaining a virgin,
you gave Him birth.

Ode 4.
Irmos. Christ is my strength, my Lord and my God!
This is the hymn that the holy Church proclaims, and with a
purified heart she sings praises unto the Lord.
The wood of the true life flourished, O Christ, when Your
cross was planted in the ground. Sprinkled with blood and
water from Your pure side, it made life spring up for us.
Never again shall the serpent deceive me by offering me
the chance to become like God, for Christ, my divine Creator,
has opened the path of life for me once again.
Glory:
You died for us, Savior. They laid You in a tomb, but it
could not hold You! You rose as God to save our souls.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Truly unfathomable and incomprehensible are the
514

Service of the Resurrection

mysteries of Your sacred conception, O perfect Virgin. They
awe the creatures of heaven and earth.

Ode 5.
Irmos. O God most good, illumine with Your divine
brightness the souls of those who love You and who keep
watch before You. I beseech You, O Word of God: grant that
they may know You, the true God, Who calls us out of the
darkness of sin.
The cherubim have drawn back from me, O Lord, and
the flaming sword no longer guards Eden; for they have seen
You, O Word of God and true God, open the way to paradise
for the good thief.
I no longer fear returning to the earth, O Christ my Lord;
for in Your great compassion, when I was still abandoned,
You brought me forth from the earth to the height of eternal
life by Your Resurrection.
Glory:
The authority of death was destroyed in Your death,
blessed Lord. You flowed forth a fountain of life for us. You
gave us immortality. We honor Your burial and resurrection
through which You enlightened the world as God.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Gracious Lady of the world, save those who sincerely
confess that you are the Theotokos. We have you as an
invincible armor, O Theotokos.

515

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Ode 6.
Irmos. When I see the ocean of this life tossed about by
the tempest of temptations, I hasten to Your harbor of peace
and cry out to You, O God of goodness: Rescue my life from
the pit of corruption.
When You were nailed to the cross, O Lord, You wiped
out the ancient curse; and when the lance pierced Your side,
You tore up the debt against Adam and set the whole world
free.
Deceived by the Serpent, Adam was hurled into the pit of
Hades; but You, O God of compassion, have gone in search of
him, and carrying him upon Your shoulders, You have raised
him with You.
Glory:
You were caught in the tomb but not held, Savior. If You
willingly tasted death, still You rose as immortal God. At the
same time You raised the prisoners of death, and turned the
grief of the women to joy.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Most pure Lady you gave birth to the Lord as food
for man. Calm down the evil surges and movement of my
passions. Give peace and quiet to my heart.

Kontakion, Tone 6:
Christ our God, the Life-giver, with His life-giving hand
raised the dead from the valley of death, granting resurrection
to us all. He is the Savior of All, the Resurrection, the Life,
and the God of all.
516

Service of the Resurrection

Ikos:
O Source of Life, we the faithful, praise and bow before
Your cross and Your tomb; for You have chained Hades, O
immortal Lord, and as the almighty God, You have raised
the dead with You. You shattered the gates of Hades and
destroyed the dominion of Death. We mortals now praise You
with love, for You have risen and demolished the power of the
deadly enemy. You have raised all those who believe in You,
and You delivered the world from the arrows of the Serpent.
O all-powerful One, You have freed us from the deceits of the
Enemy. Therefore, in faith we praise Your Resurrection, by
which You saved us, O God of the universe.

Ode 7.
Irmos. In the furnace the angel poured out dew upon
the noble youths but at the order of God the fire burned the
Chaldeans; and the tyrant was forced to sing: Blessed are You,
O Lord, the God of our fathers.
Lamenting over Your passion, in full daylight the sun
was covered with darkness, and light was darkened over all
creation as it cried out: Blessed are You, O Lord, God of our
fathers.
At Your descent, O Christ, the lower kingdoms were
filled with light, and our first father was seen filled with joy;
dancing and rejoicing, he cried out: Blessed are You, O Lord,
God of our fathers.
Glory:
In regard to the mystic type, He Who once delivered
517

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Israel from Pharoah allows Himself to be crucified by Israel.
He undoes the bonds of sin. We sing to Him: Blessed are You,
God the Savior.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
Light bursts upon the whole world from you, Virgin
Mother. You gave birth to God, the creator of everything. Ask
Him to give abundant mercy to his faithful people, O pure
Lady.

Ode 8.
Irmos. You made dew spring forth amid the flames for
Your holy ones, and through water You set fire to the sacrifice
of Your just one, for You accomplish all things through Your
will alone. O Christ, we exalt You through all ages.
The people who formerly killed the prophets have now
been seized with envy and have crucified the Word of God,
Whom we exalt through the ages.
Without leaving the vaults of heaven, You descended
into Hades, O Christ, and raised with You humanity who had
been lying in the corruption of the grave, and who exalts You
through all ages.
Glory:
All who hear are astounded! The One from on high has
come to earth by His own will. He vanquished hell’s might by
His cross and burial. He raised everyone up to sing: Children,
bless Him! Priests, sing to Him! People, praise Him, forever!

518

Service of the Resurrection

Now and ever: Theotokion:
Out of light from the Light-giver you conceived the Word.
How mysteriously you gave birth to Him! You were glorified,
obedient Maiden, for the Spirit of God abode in you. Now we
join in chorus to praise you forever.
Then we sing More honorable than the cherubim:

Ode 9.
Irmos. It is impossible for man to see God upon Whom
even the orders of angels dare not gaze; but through you, O
most pure, the Incarnate Word revealed Himself to mankind.
Therefore exalting Him together with the heavenly hosts, we
call you blessed.
You remained a stranger to passions, O Word of God,
even though You lived our human condition in the flesh; but
You delivered humanity from its passions, having overcome
our passions by Your own passion, O our Savior. For You
alone are beyond all suffering and are almighty.
Descending into the abyss of death, You preserved Your
body from the corruption of the tomb; and Your soul was not
left in Hades, O Giver of life, but You were raised up as from
sleep, O Lord, raising us with You.
Glory:
All of us praise God the Father, the co-eternal Son, and we
venerate the unfathomable and glorious power of the All-Holy
Spirit. You are the One, Almighty, and Undivided Trinity.
519

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Now and ever: Theotokion:
By your unutterably mysterious and inexpressible
conception, most pure Theotokos, resurrection has been
granted to the world. Life was robed in flesh from you. It
shone for all! It crushed the threat of death!
After this The Exapostilarion from Matins,
Tone 6:
After Your resurrection from the grave, O Savior, You
revealed Your human nature as You stood in the midst of Your
disciples; You were with them and taught them the baptism of
repentance. Then You ascended to Your Father and promised
to send them the Paraclete. Therefore, O Lover of Mankind
and God most high, glory to Your holy resurrection!
Glory: now and ever: Theotokion:
The Author of all creation and the God of all took a carnal
body from your pure womb, O holy Virgin. He renewed our
nature which had been corrupt, preserving your virginity after
birthgiving as you were before. Therefore, we all praise you
in faith and exclaim: Rejoice, O Queen of the whole world.
At The Praises the Stichera of the Resurrection, Tone 6:
Verse: To carry out the sentence pre-ordained: this honor
is for all His faithful.
Your cross, O Lord, is life and resurrection to Your people
and we place our hope in it. We praise You, our God, risen
from the dead. Have mercy on us!
Verse: Praise God in His holy place, praise Him in His
mighty heavens.
520

Service of the Resurrection

Your grave, O Master, has opened Paradise to the human
race. Freed from corruption, we praise You, our God, risen
from the dead. Have mercy on us.
Verse: Praise Him for his powerful deeds, praise His
surpassing goodness.
Let us praise Christ, risen from the dead, together with the
Father and the Spirit, and let us cry out to Him: You are our
life and resurrection; have mercy on us.
Verse: O praise Him with sound of trumpet; praise Him
with lute and harp.
You rose from the grave on the third day, O Christ,
according to the Scriptures. You raised up our first father
along with You; the human race, therefore, glorifies You and
sings the praises of Your resurrection.
Other Anatolian [Eastern] stichera, in the same tone.
Verse: Praise Him with timbrel and dance, praise Him
with strings and pipes.
Great and awesome is the mystery of Your holy
Resurrection, O Lord; for You came forth from the tomb like
a Bridegroom from His chamber, destroying Death in order
to free Adam. Therefore, the angels rejoice in heaven, and on
earth we glorify Your compassion for us, O Lover of Mankind.
Verse: O praise Him with resounding cymbals, praise
Him with clashing of cymbals. Let everything that lives and
that breathes give praise to the Lord.
O Pharisees and transgressors of the Law, where are the
seals and the silver which you gave to the soldiers? In truth the
Treasure has not been stolen but has risen, for He is almighty.
521

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Blush with shame, therefore, O deniers of Christ. The Lord of
glory suffered, was buried and rose from the dead. He is the
Lord Whom we worship.
Verse: Arise, O Lord, lift up Your hand! O God, do not
forget the poor!
How were you robbed of the buried One when the tomb
was sealed, after having placed guards and seals on it?
Behold, the King came out even though the doors were closed.
Therefore, either show us His body or worship Him with us as
God and sing: Glory to Your cross and Resurrection, O Lord!
Verse: I will praise You, Lord, with all my heart; I will
recount Your wonders.
The myrrh-bearing women came to Your life-giving
grave, O Lord, weeping and carrying ointments. They sought
Your most pure body to anoint it. Then they saw an angel
wrapped with light and sitting on a stone. He spoke to them,
saying: Why are you shedding tears for the One from Whose
side life overflowed to the world? Why do you seek in the
grave One Who is deathless? Hasten instead to His disciples
to proclaim with joy His glorious Resurrection. O Savior, You
give joy to the whole world by Your Resurrection; enlighten
us also and grant us forgiveness and great mercy.
Glory: The Gospel sticheron, Tone 6:
Since You are the true peace of God for us, O Christ, You
gave Your peace to Your disciples after Your Resurrection.
They were frightened when they thought that they were
beholding a spirit. But You removed the anxiety of their hearts
when You showed them Your hands and feet, yet they were
still in doubt. But when You took food with them, reminding
522

Service of the Resurrection

them of Your preaching, You opened their minds to understand
the Scriptures. You made the eternal covenant with them; You
blessed them and rose, ascending into heaven. Therefore, with
them, we worship You; O Lord, glory to You!
Now and ever: Theotokion:
You are most blessed, O Virgin Theotokos. Through the
One Who was incarnate of you, Hades is made captive, Adam
is restored; the curse is destroyed; Eve is freed; Death put to
death, and we have been made alive. Therefore, we cry out in
praise: Blessed are You, O Christ, our God, Who so willed.
Glory to You.
The Great Doxology. After that the Troparion of the
Resurrection, and on the first, third, fifth, and seventh tones,
we say this:
Today salvation has come to the world. Let us sing to Him
Who is risen from the tomb, the Source of our life, Who has
crushed Death by death, and bestowed on us victory and great
mercy.
On the 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 8th tones, we say this:
Rising from the tomb and breaking the bonds of Hades,
O Lord, You abolished the sentence of Death, delivering all
from the snares of the enemy. Then You revealed Yourself to
Your apostles and sent them forth to preach, and through them
You have granted Your peace to the whole world, You Who
alone are most merciful.
