524

Troparia, Theotokia
and Kontakia
during the Year

525

526

Troparia and Kontakia of the Resurrection
of the Eight Tones, with their Theotokia and Hypakoj,
Prokeimena and Kontakia

TONE ONE
Troparion
The stone was sealed by the Jews, soldiers guarded Your
most pure body, but You, O Savior, arose on the third day
granting life to the world. Therefore, the heavenly powers
acclaimed You, O Giver of Life: Glory to Your resurrection,
O Christ! Glory to Your Kingdom! Glory to Your salvation!
You alone love mankind.
Theotokion
O holy Tabernacle, Gabriel cried out to you: Rejoice,
O Virgin, full of grace: the Lord of All became incarnate of
you, as the righteous David had foretold. In bearing your
Creator, you have shown yourself to surpass the vastness of
the heavens. We therefore cry out: Glory to Him Who dwelt in
you! Glory to Him Who came forth from you. Glory to Him
Who has set us free through your life-giving birth.
Hypakoj
The repentance of the good thief opened paradise to him,
527

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

and the tears of the myrrh-bearing women proclaimed the
joyful news: O Christ as God You are risen, granting great
mercy to the world.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 12:
I Myself will arise, says the Lord. I will grant them the
salvation for which they thirst.
Verse: The words of the Lord are words without alloy.
Kontakion
According to: When You will come:
(Jehda prijdesi:
)
As God, You arose in glory from the grave and raised the
world with You. Human nature praises You as God and Death
has vanished. Adam sings in exaltation, O Lord; Eve, freed
from bondage, cries joyfully: O Christ, it is You Who give
resurrection to all.

TONE TWO
Troparion
When You descended to death, O Immortal Life, You
destroyed Hades by the brilliance of Your divinity; and when
You raised the dead from the depths of the earth, all the
heavenly powers cried out: O Giver of Life, Christ our God,
glory to You.
Theotokion
O Theotokos, the mysteries surrounding you are
exceedingly glorious, and beyond the power of understanding.
For you retained the seal of purity, and your virginity remained
528

Troparia and Kontakia of the Resurrection

inviolate; yet you are acknowledged, without doubt, to be the
Mother who gave birth to the true God. We beg you, therefore,
to entreat Him to save our souls.
Hypakoj
The women went to the tomb after Your passion to anoint
Your body, O Christ our God. They saw the angels and were
astonished; for they heard them crying with a loud voice: The
Lord is risen and grants great mercy to the world.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 7:
Lord, rise up in Your anger, rise against the fury of
my foes. My God, awake! You will give judgment. Let the
company of nations gather round You.
Verse: Lord God, I take refuge in You. From my pursuers
save me and rescue me.
Kontakion
You arose from the grave, Almighty Savior. Seeing
the miracle, Hades was struck with fear; the dead arose. At
this sight, all creation rejoices with You; Adam joins with
exultation; and the world, O my Savior, sings Your praises
forever.

TONE THREE
Troparion
Let the heavens rejoice, let the earth be glad; for the Lord
has shown the might of His arm. By His death the Lord has
trampled Death; He has become the first-born of the dead; He
has delivered us from the depths of Hades and has granted
great mercy to the world.
529

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Theotokion
We sing your praises, O Virgin; for as the Theotokos, you
always intercede for the salvation of the human race. It is from
you that our God and your Son took flesh. Then, by suffering
the Passion on the cross, He delivered us from corruption as
the Lover of Mankind.
Hypakoj
The brilliant angel startled the myrrh-bearing women and
said: Why do you seek the Living One in the grave? He is
truly risen and has emptied the tombs. Know, therefore, that
the Changeless One changed corruption to incorruption. Say
to Him: How dreadful are Your works, O Lord, for by Your
death You have saved the human race.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 95:
Proclaim to the nations: God is King. The world He made
firm, not to be moved.
Verse: O sing a new song to the Lord; sing to the Lord,
all the earth.
Kontakion
According to: Today the Virgin:
(D’iva dnes’:  
)
Today, You arose from the grave, O merciful Lord; You
led us out of the gates of Death. Today, Adam exalts and Eve
rejoices. With them, the prophets and patriarchs ever praise
the might of Your divine power.

530

Troparia and Kontakia of the Resurrection

TONE FOUR
Troparion
The joyful message of the resurrection was heard by
the women disciples from the angel, and being freed from
the ancestral curse, they boasted to the apostles: Death is
despoiled; Christ our God is risen, giving great mercy to the
world.
Theotokion
The mystery hidden from all ages and unknown to the
angels has been made known to those on earth through you, O
Theotokos. God has taken flesh in a union without confusion,
and willingly accepted the cross for us; whereby He raised the
first formed Adam and saved our souls from death.
Hypakoj
The myrrh-bearing women hastened to the apostles and
related to them the account of Your Resurrection, O Christ,
saying: You rose because You are God, and You grant great
mercy to the world.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 43:
Stand up and come to our help! Redeem us because of
Your love!
Verse: We heard with our own ears, O God; our fathers
have told us the story of the things You did in days long ago.
Kontakion
According to: You have revealed Yourself:
(Javilsja jesi dnes’:   
)
O my Savior and Redeemer, as God, You raised from the
grave all those who were in chains and destroyed the gates of
Hades; and, as Lord, You arose on the third day.
531

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

TONE FIVE
Troparion
O faithful, let us praise and adore the Word eternal with the
Father and the Spirit, and born of the Virgin for our salvation.
For He chose to ascend the cross in the flesh and to suffer
death, and to raise the dead by His glorious resurrection.
Theotokion
Rejoice, Virgin, impassible Gateway of the Lord! Rejoice,
protective Wall of those who take refuge in you! Rejoice,
peaceful Haven untroubled by storms! Rejoice, O Virgin who
has not known wedlock, and yet has given birth in the flesh to
your Creator and God! O Theotokos, never cease to intercede
for all those who praise and worship your Son.
Hypakoj
The minds of the myrrh-bearing women were dazzled
by the angelic vision, and their souls were illumined by the
divine Resurrection. Therefore, they spoke to the apostles,
saying: Declare to the nations the Resurrection of the Lord
Who works His wonders with us and bestows on us great
mercy.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 9:
Arise, then, Lord! My God, lift up Your hand! The Lord
is King forever!
Verse: I will praise You, Lord, with all my heart; I will
recall all Your wonders.

532

Troparia and Kontakia of the Resurrection

Kontakion
According to: Let us the faithful:
(Sobeznačal’noje Slovo:  

)

O Savior, You descended into Hades. You crushed its
gates as the Almighty. You raised the dead and destroyed the
sting of Death as the Creator. You delivered Adam from the
curse, O Lover of Mankind; therefore, all cry out to You, O
Lord, save us.

TONE SIX
Troparion
Angelic powers appeared at Your tomb, and the guards
became like dead men. Mary stood at the tomb seeking Your
most pure body. You despoiled Hades without a challenge.
You, the Giver of Life, met the Virgin. O Lord, risen from the
dead, glory to You.
Theotokion
Christ, Who called you “Mother” and “Blessed One,”
accepted the Passion of His own free will. In His desire to find
the fallen Adam, He caused light to shine forth from His cross
in order to search him out. Then He said to the angels: Rejoice
with me, for I have found the lost piece of silver. Glory to
You, O God, Who accomplished all things in such wisdom.
Hypakoj
By Your voluntary and life-giving death, O Christ,
You crushed the gates of Hades and opened the paradise of
old, because You are God! Having risen from the dead You
redeemed our life from corruption.
533

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 79:
O Lord, rouse up Your might! O Lord, come to our help!
Verse: O Shepherd of Israel, hear us; You Who lead
Joseph like a flock.
Kontakion
Christ our God, the Life-giver, with His life-giving hand
raised the dead from the valley of death, granting resurrection
to all of us. He is the Savior of All, the Resurrection, the Life,
and the God of All.

TONE SEVEN
Troparion
You have destroyed Death by Your cross; You opened
paradise to the thief. The sorrow of the myrrh-bearers You
turned to joy. You commanded Your apostles to proclaim;
Christ our God, You have risen, granting great mercy to the
world.
Theotokion
O Theotokos, we sing your praises, for you were a virgin
before conceiving, and remained a virgin after giving birth.
And since you have given birth to our Salvation, Jesus Christ,
you have become a treasury of assistance for all who seek
resurrection and eternal life. Therefore, lift us up from the
depths of our transgressions, for we place our hope in you.

534

Troparia and Kontakia of the Resurrection

Hypakoj
You have taken our image and likeness and endured
crucifixion in the flesh; save me by Your resurrection, O Christ
our God, for You are the Lover of Mankind.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 9:
Arise, then, Lord my God, lift up Your hand. O God, do
not forget the poor!
Verse: I will praise You, Lord, with all my heart; I will
recount all Your wonders.
Kontakion
No longer can the might of Death rule over us; Christ
descended, destroying and crushing its power. Hades remains
enchained. The prophets rejoice together. The Savior has
appeared, saying to those in darkness: Come forth, faithful, to
the Resurrection.

TONE EIGHT
Troparion
You descended from on high, O merciful One. You
accepted burial for three days to free us from our passions. O
Lord, our Resurrection and our Life, glory to You.
Theotokion
O gracious Lord, for the sake of mankind You were born
of a virgin; through Your death on the cross You conquered
Death; and through Your resurrection You revealed Yourself
as God. O Merciful Lord, do not disdain those whom You
have created with Your own hands, but show forth Your love
535

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

for mankind. Accept the intercession which the Mother who
bore You makes in our behalf: O Savior, save Your despairing
people.
Hypakoj
The myrrh-bearing women came to the tomb of the Giver
of Life, seeking among the dead the Lord, Who is deathless.
When they received the Good News from the angels, they
preached to the apostles that the Lord is risen, granting great
mercy to the world.
At the Matins Prokeimenon, Psalm 145:
The Lord will reign forever; Zion’s God from age to age.
Verse: My soul, give praise to the Lord! I will praise my
God all my days.
Kontakion
According to: To You, O Lord, the Gardener:
(Jako načatki:  
)
Rising from the grave, You raised the dead. You lifted
up Adam, and Eve rejoices in Your resurrection. The whole
world celebrates Your resurrection from the dead, O Most
Merciful One.

536

Troparia and Kontakia of the
Days of the Week
SUNDAY EVENING [MONDAY]
[Dedicated to the Holy Angels]
Troparion, Tone 4:
Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us by your prayers and to
shelter us beneath the wings of your sublime glory. Watch
over us who bow to you and cry out fervently: Deliver us from
danger, for you are the commanders of the powers on high.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Leaders of God’s armies and ministers of divine glory,
commanders of angels and guides of mortals, plead on our
behalf for what we need and for great mercy; since you are the
leaders of the heavenly hosts.

537

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

MONDAY EVENING [TUESDAY]
[Dedicated to the Holy Prophet, Forerunner,
and Baptist John]
Troparion, Tone 2:
The memory of the righteous is celebrated with praise,
but for you, O Forerunner, the Lord’s testimony is enough.
You were shown to be more honorable than the prophets since
you were deemed worthy to baptize in the waters the Lord you
had proclaimed. Therefore, you fought for the truth, and with
joy proclaimed the good news to those in Hades, that God has
appeared in the flesh to take away the sins of the world and to
grant us great mercy.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Today she who once was barren gives birth to Christ’s
Forerunner. He himself is the fulfillment of all prophecy; for
in the Jordan, he imposed his hand upon the Word of God
Whom the prophets had foretold and was shown to be his
prophet, herald, and Forerunner.

TUESDAY EVENING [WEDNESDAY]
[Dedicated to the Precious, Holy, and Life-Creating Cross
and to the Most Holy Theotokos]
Troparion of the cross, Tone 1:
Save Your people, O Lord, and bless your inheritance.
Grant victory to your Church over evil and protect Your
people by Your cross.
538

Troparia and Kontakia of the Days of the Week

Kontakion of the cross, Tone 4
Christ our God, Who were willingly raised upon the cross,
grant Your mercies to the new people who bear Your Name.
By Your power grant joy to the Church. Give her victory over
evil with Your invincible trophy, the weapon of peace, as an
ally.

WEDNESDAY EVENING [THURSDAY]
[Dedicated to the Holy Apostles
and to Our Holy Father Nicholas of Myra]
Troparion of the Apostles, Tone 3:
O holy apostles, intercede with the merciful God that He
may grant our souls forgiveness of sins.
Another, Troparion to St. Nicholas, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you to your flock as a rule of faith,
an image of gentleness, and a teacher of moderation. You
acquired greatness through humility and wealth through
poverty. O father and archbishop Nicholas, intercede with
Christ our God to save our souls.
Kontakion of the Apostles, Tone 2:
Lord, You have received Your steadfast and inspired
preachers, the foremost of Your apostles, into the enjoyment
of Your good gifts and repose. You preferred their sufferings
and death above any sacrifice. For You alone know the secrets
of the heart.

539

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Another Kontakion to St. Nicholas, Tone 3:
You were renowned as a priest in Myra, O holy Nicholas;
for you fulfilled the Gospel of Christ, O venerable father. You
risked your life for your people and saved the innocent from
death. Thereby you have been initiated into the mysteries of
the grace of God.

THURSDAY EVENING [FRIDAY]

[Dedicated to the Precious, Holy, and Life-Creating Cross]
Troparion of the cross, Tone 1:
Save Your people, O Lord, and bless Your inheritance.
Grant victory to your Church over evil and protect Your
people by Your cross.
Kontakion of the cross, Tone 4:
Christ our God, Who were willingly raised upon the cross,
grant Your mercies to the new people who bear Your Name.
By Your power grant joy to the Church. Give her victory over
evil with Your invincible trophy, the weapon of peace, as an
ally.

FRIDAY EVENING [SATURDAY]

[Dedicated to All Saints and to the Faithful Departed]
Troparion of the Saints, Tone 2:
Apostles, martyrs, and prophets, bishops, venerable and
righteous saints, you have finished the course and have kept
the faith. Since you can approach the Savior with confidence,
we ask you to beseech His goodness on our behalf, for the
salvation of our souls.
540

Troparia and Kontakia of the Days of the Week

A Second Troparion, for the Departed, Tone 2:
O Lord, in Your goodness, remember Your servants and
forgive whatever sins they committed in their life; for no one
is sinless but You alone. You have the power to grant rest to
the departed.

SATURDAY, We say:
Glory:
With the saints, O Christ, give rest to Your servants, where
there is no pain, sorrow, nor mourning, but life everlasting.
Now and ever: Tone 8
To You, O Lord, Gardener of all Creation, the world
offers the God-bearing martyrs as the first fruits of nature.
Through their prayers and through the Theotokos, preserve
Your Church, Your dwelling-place, in perfect peace, O most
merciful One.

541

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

542

Theotokia and Stavrotheotokia
of the Eight Tones

said on Sunday evening Vespers
and on Tuesday and Thursday evening Vespers
according to the Tone of the Troparia
of the Saints
Sunday evening Vespers: Theotokion, Tone 1:
The universe recognizes in you, O Woman full of grace,
the marvel of marvels and it rejoices. You have borne without
human seed the One Whom even the highest ranks of angels
cannot look upon, and you have given birth in a manner
beyond understanding. Intercede with Him for the salvation
of our souls.
Tuesday and Thursday evening Vespers:
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 1:
O Pure One, we have obtained your protection. Through
your intercession, we have been kept from harm and
surrounded at all times with the grace of your Son’s cross.
Therefore, we exalt you with great devotion.

543

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Theotokion, Tone 2:
Most Merciful Theotokos, fount of mercy; deem us worthy
of compassion. Look upon a sinful people and as always show
your power; for placing our trust in you, we cry out to you
“Rejoice,” as once did Gabriel, the commander of angels.
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 2:
O Virgin and all-glorious Theotokos, we sing to you
a hymn of praise, for Hades has been destroyed by your
Son’s cross; Death has been put to death, and we, the dead,
have been made to rise and become worthy of life. We have
obtained paradise, the original bliss. Therefore, we glorify you
by giving thanks to Christ our God, for He alone is almighty
and all-merciful.
Theotokion, Tone 3:
Gabriel was rapt in amazement as he beheld your virginity
and the splendor of your purity, O Theotokos, and he cried out
to you: By what name shall I call you? I am bewildered, I am
lost! I shall greet you as I was commanded to do: Rejoice, O
Woman full of grace!
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 3:
O Theotokos, we have obtained your Son’s cross as a
staff of power with which to strike down the boastings of the
Enemy. Therefore we exalt you without ceasing.
Theotokion, Tone 4:
To the one who was reared in the Temple, close to the
Holy of Holies, and who was full of faith, wisdom, and perfect
virginity, Gabriel, the captain and leader, offered esteem and
544

Theotokia and Stavrotheotokia of the Eight Tones

greetings from heaven when he said: Rejoice, O Blessed One!
Rejoice, O Glorified One! The Lord is with you!
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 4:
O Virgin, All-Immaculate Mother of Christ God, a sword
pierced your holy soul when you saw your Son and God
willingly crucified. Therefore, O Blessed One, never cease to
pray to Him that he may grant us forgiveness of our sins.
Theotokion, Tone 5:
With the angels of heaven and with people on earth, O
Theotokos, we cry out to you exultingly: Rejoice, O gate that
is wider than heaven! Rejoice, only salvation of the human
race! Rejoice, O honorable one, full of grace, who gave birth
to the incarnate God!
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 5:
Since you are all-pleasing to God, may the error of idol
worship be destroyed, and may the power of demons be
trodden underfoot by the might of your Son’s cross. Therefore,
we, the faithful, always sing to you in humility; we bless you
and we exalt you, professing that you are truly the Theotokos.
Theotokion, Tone 6:
The announcement of Gabriel to the Virgin was the
beginning of salvation, for she heard the salutation and did
not flee from the greeting, nor did she doubt as did Sarah in
the tent. She proclaimed, instead: Behold the handmaid of the
Lord. Be it done to me according to your word.

545

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Stavrotheotokion, Tone 6:
O Virgin Theotokos, pray to your Son, Christ our God,
Who delivered the world from error, when He accepted
willingly to be crucified, that He may have mercy on our souls.
Theotokion, Tone 7:
Undefiled Virgin Theotokos, pray to your Son with the
powers of heaven that before death, He may grant forgiveness
of sins to those who faithfully glorify Him.
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 7:
O Virgin Theotokos, intercede with Christ our God Who
was crucified for us and destroyed the power of Death, that He
may save our souls.
Theotokion, Tone 8:
Rejoice, O Woman who at the angel’s greeting, contained
the joy of the world! Rejoice, for you gave birth to your
Creator and Lord! Rejoice, for you were made worthy to
become the Theotokos!
Stavrotheotokion, Tone 8:
Seeing the Lamb and Shepherd and Savior of the world
on the cross, she who bore Him said weeping: The world
rejoices, for it receives redemption; but my inner being burns
as I see Your crucifixion which You endured for all, O my Son
and my God.

546

Troparia and Kontakia of the
Classes of Saints
Troparion to the Theotokos, Tone 4:
Let us humble sinners now flee with fervor to the
Theotokos. Let us prostrate in repentance and cry out from
the depths of our souls: O Lady, help us and have mercy on us.
Hurry to assist us for we are perishing because of our many
sins. Do not turn us away empty handed. For you alone we
have as our protectress.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
We have no other help and no other hope but you, most
pure Virgin. You are our help; in you we hope and we praise
you. We are your servants; do not let us be put to shame.
Troparion to the Bodiless Ones, Tone 4:
Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us by your prayers and to
shelter us beneath the wings of your sublime glory. Watch
over us who bow to you and cry out fervently: Deliver us from
danger. For you are the commanders of the powers on high.

547

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Leaders of God’s armies and ministers of divine glory,
commanders of angels and guides of mortals, plead on our
behalf for what we need and for great mercy; since you are the
leaders of the heavenly hosts.
Troparion to a Prophet, Tone 2:
As we celebrate the memory of your prophet (Name), O
Lord, we implore You to save our souls through his prayers.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Your pure heart was enlightened by the Spirit and became
a vessel of radiant prophecy. Because you saw as present the
events yet to come we honor you, O blessed and glorious
prophet (Name).
Troparion to an Apostle, Tone 3:
O holy Apostle (Name), intercede with the merciful God
that He may grant our souls forgiveness of sins.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
O Apostle (Name), the Church has gained you for all time
as a brilliant star, enlightening it with the multitude of your
miracles. Therefore, we cry out to Christ: O most merciful
Lord, save those who in faith honor the memory of Your
Apostle.
Troparion to two or more Apostles, Tone 3:
O holy apostles, intercede with the merciful God that He
may grant our souls forgiveness of sins.
548

Troparia and Kontakia of the Classes of Saints

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Wise apostles of the Lord, you became branches of the
vine of Christ, bearing clusters of virtues and pouring out the
wine of salvation for us. Partaking of it, we are filled with
joy. As we celebrate your glorious memory, pray that we be
granted great mercy and forgiveness of sins.
Troparion to a Hierarch, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you to your flock as a rule of faith,
an image of gentleness, and a teacher of moderation. You
acquired greatness through humility and wealth through
poverty. O father and bishop (Name), intercede with Christ
our God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Divine thunder, spiritual trumpet, sower of faith, and
destroyer of heresies, servant of the Trinity, O great bishop
(Name), you stand forever with the angels. Pray without
ceasing for all of us.
Troparion to two or more Hierarchs, Tone 4:
God of our fathers, You always deal with us in Your
kindness. Take not Your mercy away from us; but through
their prayers guide our life in peace.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
The Church glorifies you in song as teachers of virtue
and the splendor of hierarchs. By your prayers, grant growth
in virtue and deliverance from the snares of evil for you are
invincible.
549

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Troparion to a Venerable Man, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image was strictly preserved;
taking up your cross, you followed Christ. You taught us by
example how to spurn the flesh, for it passes away, and how to
care for the soul, which is immortal. Therefore, O venerable
(Name), your soul rejoices with the angels.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You armed yourself in a godly way with purity of soul, and
you wielded unceasing prayer as a mighty spear, piercing the
armies of demons. Our father (Name), pray without ceasing
for all of us.
Troparion to several Venerable Men, Tone 4:
God of our fathers, You always deal with us in Your
kindness. Take not Your mercy away from us; but through
their prayers guide our life in peace.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Passing through the stormy waves, you remained dry. You
drowned the bodiless enemies in the mighty streams of your
tears. O venerable fathers, filled with God’s wisdom, you have
received the gift of miracles. Pray without ceasing for all of
us.
Troparion to a Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr (Name), O Lord our God, in his struggle
received an incorruptible crown from You. With Your
strength, he brought down the tyrants and broke the cowardly
valor of demons. Through his prayers, O Christ our God, save
our souls.

Troparia and Kontakia of the Classes of Saints

Kontakion, Tone 2:
O victorious martyr (Name), you arose as a bright star not
misleading the world but announcing Christ the Sun by your
rays. You have extinguished all error. Give us light as you
pray without ceasing for all of us.
Troparion to two or more Martyrs, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God, in their struggles received

brought down the tyrants and broke the cowardly valor of

or this Troparion, Tone 1:
O Lover of Mankind, accept the sufferings which Your
saints endured for You. As we pray, heal all our pains.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You appeared as bright lamps, O godly martyrs. You
enlightened all creation with the brilliance of your miracles.
As you free us from sickness and drive away forever the
depths of darkness, pray without ceasing to Christ our God
for all of us.
Troparion to a Priest-martyr, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life and succeeded to
their throne, divinely inspired bishop. You found access to
contemplation in the active life. Therefore, you rightly taught
the word of truth and struggled for the faith to the shedding of
your blood. O Priest-martyr (Name), pray to Christ our God
to save our souls.

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Kontakion, Tone 4:
You lived piously as a bishop, and followed the path to
martyrdom. Filled with divine wisdom, you put out the fire of
sacrifice to idols. You were a defender of your flock. Therefore,
to honor you we mystically sing: Our father (Name), by your
prayers, deliver us always from tribulation.
Troparion to several Priest-martyrs, Tone 4:

all ascetics.

Kontakion, Tone 2:

trampled serpents.

Kontakion, Tone 2:
In your love for the Lord you disdained the desire for rest,
O venerable woman. You enlightened your soul by fasting and
with power you conquered beasts; but by your prayers destroy
the pride of our enemies.
Troparion to several Venerable Women, Tone 2:
With sincere desire you wedded yourselves to Christ and
rejected worldly marriage, O glorious women. You matured in
the struggle for virtues and rose to the summit of incorruption.
Beautiful in soul and richly blessed, you were the standard and
pillars of monastic women. Therefore, pray without ceasing
for us who celebrate your memory with love.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You disciplined your bodies by fasting and, with unceasing
prayers, implored the Giver of Life that you might receive
perfect forgiveness for your sins. Having received divine
pardon and the kingdom of heaven, now pray to Christ our
God for all of us.

you enlightened all by your teachings; intercede with Christ
our God to save our souls.

said from the Sunday of the Publican and the Pharisee,

SUNDAY OF THE PUBLICAN AND PHARISEE
Troparion of the Resurrection Tone.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Let us offer the Lord sighs like the publican. As sinners,
let us fall before Him, our Master; for He wills the salvation
of everyone. He grants forgiveness to all who repent for, while
remaining God, co-eternal with the Father, He took flesh for
our sake.
Or, this Kontakion, Tone 4:
Let us shun the boastful words of the Pharisee. Let us
learn the grandeur of the humble speech of the publican. It
summons us to repentance. O Savior of the world, have mercy
on Your servants.
SUNDAY OF THE PRODIGAL SON
Troparion of the Resurrection Tone
Kontakion, Tone 3:
When I foolishly spurned Your fatherly glory, I squandered
the riches You had given me on evil deeds. So now I cry out to
559

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

You with the voice of the prodigal son: I have sinned against
You, O merciful Father; accept my repentance and treat me as
one of Your hired servants.
MEAT-FARE SATURDAY
Troparion, Tone 8:
In the depth of Your wisdom, O only Creator, You govern
all with love and supply the needs of each. Now give rest to
the souls of Your servants, for they have placed their hope in
You, our Creator, Maker, and our God.
Glory: Kontakion, Tone 8:
With the saints, O Christ, give rest to Your servants, where
there is no pain, sorrow, nor mourning, but life everlasting.
Now and ever: Theotokion, in the same tone:
We have in You a defense and a refuge, and an advocate
acceptable to God, to Whom you gave birth, O Virgin
Theotokos, the salvation of the faithful.
SUNDAY OF MEAT-FARE
Troparion of the Resurrection Tone
Kontakion, Tone 1:
When You come to the earth in glory, O God, and the
universe trembles, and a river of fire flows before Your
judgment seat, and the books are opened, and everything
hidden is revealed, deliver me then from the unquenchable
fire, and make me worthy to stand at Your right hand, O most
righteous Judge.

on which we commemorate

Troparion, Tone 2:
Great are the accomplishments of faith. The holy martyr
Theodore rejoiced in the fountain of flames just as if resting
in calm water. Consumed in the fire, he was offered up like
a sacrifice of sweet-breads to the Holy Trinity. Through his
prayers, O Christ God, save our souls.

it in word and deed.

My soul, my soul, arise! Why are you sleeping? The end

when He came down is entirely contained in you without
change. Seeing Him in your womb taking the form of a slave,
I am amazed as I exclaim: Rejoice, O Unwedded Bride.

became a bride of the kingdom.

SIXTH SATURDAY
The Holy and Righteous Lazarus.
Troparion, Tone 1:
Christ our God, before Your passion You confirmed our
common resurrection when You raised Lazarus from the dead.
Therefore, like the children, we carry the symbols of victory
and cry out to You, the Victor over Death: Hosanna in the
highest! Blessed is He Who comes in the Name of the Lord.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O Christ, the Joy of All, the Truth, the Light, the Life,
and the Resurrection of the World, has appeared to those on
earth because of his goodness. He became the pattern of our
resurrection, granting divine forgiveness to all.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who for our salvation came to
Bethany to raise the righteous Lazarus:

PALM SUNDAY

Troparia and Kontakia of the

Flowering
Troparion,Triodion
Tone 1:

Christ our God, before Your passion You confirmed our
common resurrection when You raised Lazarus from the dead.
Therefore, like the children, we carry the symbols of victory
and cry out to You, the Victor over Death: Hosanna in the
highest! Blessed is He Who comes in the Name of the Lord.
And this Troparion, Tone 4:
Through baptism we were buried with You, O Christ our
God, and we have become worthy of immortal life by Your
resurrection. Therefore, we raise our voices in praise to You:
Hosanna in the highest! Blessed is He Who comes in the
Name of the Lord.
After the Third Ode
The Hypakoj, Tone 6:
Having first praised You with their palms, the ungrateful
people then crucified You; but we honor You with our
unchanging faith as our Benefactor, O Lord, and we
unceasingly cry out to You: Blessed is He Who comes to draw
Adam forth from the tomb.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
In heaven You are seated on a throne; but on earth upon a
colt, O Christ our God. You accepted the praise of angels and
the song of the children crying out to You: Blessed is He Who
comes to restore Adam.

On the lips of children and of babes, You have found

the praise of the Hebrew children, have mercy on us and save
us:
At Vespers on Sunday evening, and until Holy
and Great Thursday:
May the Lord, Who came to his voluntary passion for our
salvation, Christ our true God:
HOLY AND GREAT MONDAY
At Matins upon Alleluia,
Troparion, Tone 8:
Behold the Bridegroom is coming in the middle of the
night. Blessed is the servant He shall find awake. But the one
He shall find neglectful will not be worthy of Him. Beware,
therefore, O my soul! Do not fall into a deep slumber, lest
you be delivered to death and the door of the Kingdom be
closed to you. Watch instead and cry out: Holy, Holy, Holy
are You, O God. Through the intercession of the Theotokos,
have mercy on us.
570

Troparia and Kontakia of the Flowering Triodion

Kontakion, Tone 8:
While Jacob wept over the loss of his son, Joseph,
wearing a king’s attire, nobly rode in a chariot. He refused
to be enslaved by the pleasures of Egypt. Therefore, God,
Who knows the secrets of the human heart and distributes
incorruptible crowns, covered him with glory.
Hymn of Light:
I see Your bridal chamber completely engulfed with light,
O my Savior, and I do not have a wedding garment to enter
and enjoy Your brightness; fill the garment of my soul with
light and save me, O Lord. Three times.

HOLY AND GREAT TUESDAY
Troparion:
Behold the Bridegroom is coming in the middle of the
night:
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O wretched soul, think of your last hours. Be dismayed
at the rebuking of the fig tree. Act and double the talent given
you with a loving purpose. Be watchful and cry out: Grant
that we not be left outside the bridal chamber of Christ.
Hymn of Light:
I see Your bridal chamber:

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

HOLY AND GREAT WEDNESDAY
Troparion, Tone 8:
Behold the Bridegroom is coming in the middle of the
night:
Kontakion, Tone 4:
O gracious God, I sinned more than the Adulteress and
yet never offered refreshing teardrops. In silent prayer, I now
prostrate myself, kissing with love Your immaculate feet in
order to receive from You, O Master, the forgiveness of my
sins. I cry out to You: O Savior, deliver me from the murk of
my evil deeds.
Hymn of Light:
I see Your bridal chamber:
HOLY AND GREAT THURSDAY
At Matins, upon Alleluia,
Troparion, Tone 8:
While the illustrious disciples were enlightened as their
feet were washed at the supper, the ungodly Judas darkened
by a sick love of silver, betrayed You, the Just Judge, to
lawless judges. See how a money-hungry man hanged himself
because of it, and flee the greedy soul who would do such
things to the teacher. O Lord, so good to everyone, glory to
You. Three times.

Troparia and Kontakia of the Flowering Triodion

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Judas, the deceitful servant, when he stretched his hand
secretly and took bread, did therefore take the price of Him
Who made humanity with His own hands, thus remaining
reprobate.
Hymn of Light:
I see Your bridal chamber:
At the end of Matins, the Dismissal:
May the Lord, Who came to His voluntary passion for
our salvation, Christ our true God:
At the end of Vespers and Liturgy, the Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who, because of His surpassing
goodness, showed us the most excellent way of humility
when He washed His disciples’ feet, and humbled Himself
even unto the cross and burial:
HOLY AND GREAT FRIDAY
Troparion:
While the illustrious disciples:
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O come, and let us all praise Him crucified for our sake,
just as did Mary when she beheld Him on the cross and said:
Even though You have suffered crucifixion, You are still my

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Exapostilarion:
The wise thief You made worthy of paradise in a single
moment, O Lord. By the wood of Your cross, illumine me as
well and save me.
Troparion at the Dismissal, Tone 4:
You have redeemed us from the curse of the law with Your
precious blood; nailed to the cross and pierced with the lance,
You have become a fountain of immortality for us; glory to
You, our Savior.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who for the salvation of the
world suffered being spat upon, then suffered scourges,
wounds, crucifixion and death, have mercy on us and save us:
Glory: Troparion of the First Hour, Tone 1:
When You ascended Your cross, O Christ, You crushed
the tyranny and power of the Enemy; it is neither an angel
nor a human, but God Himself Who saves us: O Lord, glory
to You.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
What shall we call you, O Full of Grace? A Heaven; for
you gave rise to the Sun of Justice? A Paradise; for you have
brought forth the Flower of incorruption? A Virgin; for you
have remained undefiled? A pure Mother, holding in her holy
arms the Son Who is the God of all? Intercede with Him for
the salvation of our souls.

Troparia and Kontakia of the Flowering Triodion

Kontakion, Tone 8:
O come, and let us all praise Him crucified for our sake,
just as did Mary when she beheld Him on the cross and said:
Even though You have suffered crucifixion, You are still my
Son and still my God.
Glory: Troparion of the Third Hour, Tone 6:
O Lord, the children of Israel have condemned You to
death, You the Life of the world. Those who crossed the Red
Sea because of the staff of Moses, have nailed You to the wood
of the cross; those who tasted the honey from the rock, have
given You gall as food. Yet You suffered willingly to deliver
us from slavery to the Enemy. O Christ our God, glory to You.
Now and ever: Theotokion:
O Theotokos, you are the True Vine who gave birth to the
Fruit of Life: wherefore, we implore you, O Lady, to intercede
together with the apostles and all the saints that we may obtain
mercy for our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
[O come, let us all praise Him] crucified for our sake:
Glory: Troparion of the Sixth Hour, Tone 2:
O Christ God, You brought about salvation in the middle
of the earth. You stretched out Your all-pure hands on the cross
in order to gather together all the nations, who cry aloud: O
Lord, glory to You!

575

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Now and ever: Theotokion:
Since we have no one in whom to confide because of our
many sins, O Virgin Theotokos, intercede for us with the One
Who was born of you, for a mother’s prayer is a powerful
means for obtaining the Master’s favor. You are most worthy
of veneration, so do not turn away from the pleading of us
sinners; for the One Who willed to suffer in the flesh for our
sake is full of mercy. And His power is sufficient to save us.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
[O come let us all praise Him] crucified for our sake:

Glory: Troparion of the Ninth Hour, Tone 8:
Seeing the Author of life hanging on the cross, the Good
Thief cried out with His act of faith. If the One crucified with
us were not God in the flesh, the sun would not have hidden
its rays, nor would the earth have trembled with fear. And
You patiently bear all this; remember me, O Lord, in Your
kingdom.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O come, and let us all praise Him crucified for our sake,
just as did Mary when she beheld Him on the cross and said:
Even though You have suffered crucifixion, You are still my
Son and still my God.
Dismissal of the Hours:
May Christ our true God, Who for us and for our salvation,
suffered the passion, the life-giving cross, and voluntary burial
in the flesh, have mercy on us and save us:

Troparia and Kontakia of the Flowering Triodion

GREAT AND HOLY SATURDAY
Troparion, Tone 2:
The noble Joseph took down Your most pure body from
the cross. He wrapped it in a clean shroud and with fragrant
spices laid it in burial in a new tomb.
Glory:
When You descended to death, O Immortal Life, You
destroyed Hades by the brilliance of Your divinity; and when
You raised the dead from the depths of the earth, all the
heavenly powers cried out: O Giver of Life, Christ our God,
glory to You.
Now and ever:
The angel standing by the tomb cried out to the myrrhbearing women: Myrrh is fitting for the dead, but Christ has
shown Himself not subject to corruption.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
He Who closed the depths of the sea is beheld wrapped
in linen and embalmed with myrrh; the Deathless One is
placed in the tomb like One Who is dead. The women came
to embalm Him, weeping bitterly and crying: Behold the
Sabbath transcendent in blessings in which Christ has slept
and will rise on the third day.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who suffered the passion, the
life-giving cross, and voluntary burial in the flesh for our sake
and for all mankind, have mercy on us and save us:
577

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

578

ORDER OF THE HOLY
AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA
The principal celebrant with the priests go forth from the
church singing the sticheron, Tone 6:
Your resurrection, O Christ our Savior, the angels in
heaven praise with hymns; make us, on earth, also worthy
with a pure heart to extol and give glory to You.
The priest in a loud voice exclaims:
Glory to the holy, consubstantial, life-creating and
undivided Trinity, always, now and ever and forever.
And we, responding Amen, the principal celebrant with
the other clergy sing aloud the appointed troparion, in Tone
5 [special tone]:
Christ is risen from the dead! By death He trampled
Death, and to those in the tombs He granted life.
And we also sing it in the same way, with sweet melody.
This troparion is sung three times by the principal
celebrant, and three times by us.
579

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then, the principal celebrant says the verses:
First: Let God arise and let His enemies be scattered, and let
those who hate Him flee from before His face!
And at each verse we sing the troparion:
Christ is risen: the entire troparion once.
Second: As smoke vanishes, so let them vanish, as wax melts
before a fire.
Christ is risen:
Third: So let the wicked perish at the presence of God, but let
the righteous ones rejoice.
Christ is risen:
Fourth: This is the day that the Lord has made; let us be glad
and rejoice in it.
Christ is risen: once.
Glory: Christ is risen: once.
Now and ever: Christ is risen: once.
Then the principal celebrant sings in a higher tone:
Christ is risen from the dead! By death He trampled Death:
580

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

And he opens the doors. The principal celebrant enters
with the precious cross, with two lamps borne before him, and
with the brethren, singing:
and to those in the tombs He granted life.
The three principal bells are struck, and all the bells are
rung.
The principal celebrant with the priests enter the altar,
and the deacon says the Great Litany:
In peace, let us pray to the Lord. [see p. 104-105]
Exclamation: For to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, is
due all glory, honor, and worship, now and ever and forever.
Choir: Amen.
And the principal celebrant begins the canon.

CANON
A Composition of John of Damascus.
Tone 1. Ode 1.
Irmos. It is the day of Resurrection. O People, let us be
enlightened by it. The Passover is the Lord’s own Passover,
since Christ our God has brought us from death to life and
from earth to heaven. We, therefore, sing the hymn of victory.
Versicle: Christ is risen from the dead!

581

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Let us cleanse our senses that we may see the risen Christ
in the glory of His resurrection and clearly hear Him greeting
us: “Rejoice”—as we sing the hymn of victory.
Let the heavens properly rejoice, and let the earth be glad,
and let the whole visible and invisible world celebrate; for
Christ, our everlasting joy is risen.
Then, the Little Ektenia, and the exclamation:
For You are the supreme ruler, and Yours are the kingdom,
and the power, and the glory, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit,
now and ever and forever.

Ode 3.
Irmos. Come, let us partake of a new drink, not
miraculously produced from the barren rock, but from the
fountain of immortality, springing up from the tomb of Christ.
In Him is our firm strength.
Today all things are filled with light—earth and heaven
and the world beneath. Then let all creation celebrate the
resurrection of Christ. In Him is the firm foundation of all
things.
I was buried yesterday with You, O Christ; but today I
rise, resurrected with You. Yesterday I crucified myself with
You, O Savior. Now glorify me with You in Your kingdom.
The Little Ektenia, and the exclamation:
For You are our God, and we give glory to You, Father,
Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever and forever.
582

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

Hypakoj, Tone 4:
The women with Mary before the dawn found the stone
rolled away from the tomb, and they heard the angel say:
“Why do you seek among the dead, as a mortal, the One Who
abides in everlasting light? Behold the linens of burial. Go
in haste and proclaim to the world that, having conquered
Death, the Lord is risen; for He is the Son of God, the Savior
of mankind.”

Ode 4.
Irmos. Let Habakkuk, speaking in behalf of God, stand
with us at the divine watch; let him show us the brilliant Angel
who proclaims: “Today, salvation comes to the world; for
Christ, being Almighty is risen.”
Christ had appeared as a man when He was born of the
Virgin. As a mortal, He was called “Lamb”. Being undefiled
and without blemish, He is our Passover; and as true God, He
is proclaimed perfect.
Christ, our blessed crown, was sacrificed of His own will
like a yearling lamb for all of us, and so became our cleansing
Pasch. From His tomb He shines on us again as the splendid
Sun of Righteousness.
David, ancestor of the Lord, danced and made music
before the Ark which was only a symbol. As God’s holy
people, let us witness the symbol fulfilled and rejoice in spirit;
for Christ, being Almighty, is risen.
The Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
583

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

For You are a good God and You love mankind, and we
give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever.

Ode 5.
Irmos. Let us rise at early dawn and bring to our Master
a hymn instead of myrrh, and we shall see Christ, the Sun of
Righteousness, Who enlightens the life of all.
When those bound by chains in the realm of Death saw
Your boundless mercy, O Christ, they hastened to the light
with joy, praising the eternal Pasch.
Bearing torches let us meet the Bridegroom, Christ, as He
comes forth from his tomb; and let us greet, with festive song,
the saving Pasch of God.
The Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
For sanctified and glorified is Your all-honorable and
majestic Name: Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever
and forever.

Ode 6.
Irmos. You have descended into the realm of Death,
O Christ, and have broken ancients bonds which held the
captive. You arose from the tomb on the third day like Jonah
from the whale.
When You arose from the tomb, O Christ, You preserved
its seals intact, just as in Your holy birth a virgin’s vow was
unbroken. You opened to us the gates of paradise.
584

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

O my Savior, being God, willingly You offered Yourself.
As a never-consumed yet living victim, You gave Yourself to
the Father. You arose from the tomb, resurrecting Adam, the
father of all.
The Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
For You are the King of peace and the Savior of our souls,
and we give glory to You, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now
and ever and forever.

Kontakion, Tone 8:
Although You descended into the grave, O Immortal One,
You destroyed Hades’ power. You arose as a victor, O Christ
God. You exclaimed to the myrrh-bearing women: Rejoice!
You gave peace to Your apostles and granted resurrection to
the fallen.

Ikos:

Early in the morning before sunrise, as if it were already
day, myrrh-bearing virgins were seeking the Sun, previously
descended into the grave; and they cried out to one another:
“Come, O friends! Let us anoint with fragrant spices the lifegiving and yet already buried body of Christ Who resurrected
the fallen Adam. Let us hasten, as did the Magi, and adore
Christ and bring our myrrh as a gift to Him Who is wrapped
not in swaddling clothes but in a shroud. Let us weep and
exclaim: ‘Arise, O Master, granting resurrection to the
fallen!’”
Then we say:
Having beheld the resurrection of Christ let us worship the
holy Lord Jesus Who alone is sinless. We bow to Your cross,
O Christ, and we glorify and praise Your holy Resurrection.
585

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

You are our God, and besides You we recognize no other,
and we call upon Your Name. Come, all you faithful, and let
us bow to the holy Resurrection of Christ since, through the
cross, joy has come to all the world. Ever blessing the Lord,
let us extol His Resurrection since He, having suffered the
crucifixion, has destroyed Death by His death. Three times.

Sticheron, Tone 6:
Jesus is risen from the tomb, as He foretold, and granted
us everlasting life and great mercy.

Ode 7.
Irmos. God, Who saved the three youths from the furnace,
has become man and suffered as any mortal; but His passion
clothed His mortality with the splendor of incorruption. He is
the only Blessed One, God of our fathers, and is worthy of all
praise.
Pious women ran in tears to You, O Christ, bringing
myrrh to You as dead; but instead, they adored You in joy as
the living God and announced Your mystical Passover to Your
disciples.
We celebrate Your victory over Death, the destruction of
the deep abyss, and the birth of a new eternal life. With joy,
we praise the Author of all things, the only-blessed One, God
of our fathers, for He is worthy of all praise.
This most splendid and saving night is sacred and allworthy of solemnity. It heralds the bright day of resurrection
on which the Eternal Light in the flesh has shown forth from
the tomb to all.
586

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

The Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
For Yours is the might; and Yours are the kingdom and the
power and the glory, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and
ever and forever.

Ode 8.
Irmos. This is that chosen and holy day, feast of feasts,
most solemn day, only king and lord of all Sabbaths on which
we ever praise Christ.
Come, on this glorious day of resurrection, and partake of
the fruit of the new vine, the divine joy of Christ’s kingdom,
ever-praising Him as God.
Lift up your eyes, O Zion, and behold. See your children
coming to you. From the east, west, north, and south, they
come to you like stars of light divine, ever blessing Christ.
[O Most Holy Trinity, our God, glory to You!]
Trinitarian Hymn. O Almighty Father, Spirit, and Word,
three Persons, yet one essence, fullness of all divinity—we
have been baptized in You, and ever bless You.
Then, the Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
For blessed is Your Name, and glorified is Your kingdom,
Father, Son, and Holy Spirit, now and ever and forever.
Verse on Ode 9.
The angel exclaimed to her, full of grace: Rejoice, O pure
Virgin; and again, I say: Rejoice! Your Son is risen from the
587

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

grave on the third day and has raised the dead. Rejoice, all
you nations!

Ode 9.
Irmos. Shine in splendor, O new Jerusalem; for the glory
of the Lord is risen upon you, O Zion, now dance and be glad;
and you, pure Theotokos, rejoice in the resurrection of your
Son.
How pleasingly divine and sweet was Your voice, O
Christ, when You promised without fail to remain with us until
the end of time. We, the faithful rejoice in this firm foundation
of hope.
O Christ, Great and Sacred Pasch, Wisdom, Power and
Word of God, grant that we be with You in Your kingdom on
the never-ending day.
The Little Ektenia, and the Exclamation:
For all the heavenly Powers praise You, and we give glory
to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit, now and
ever and forever.

Exapostilarion Samohlasen:
You, O King and Lord, have fallen asleep in the flesh as
a mortal man but on the third day You arose. You have raised
Adam from his corruption and made death powerless. You are
the Pasch of incorruption. You are the salvation of the world.
Three times.

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

Then, The Praises, Let everything that lives:
in Tone 1.
We interpolate four stichera. And we sing the stichera of
the Resurrection, Tone 1:
Verse: Praise Him for His powerful deeds, praise His
surpassing greatness. [Psalm 150:2]
We praise Your saving passion, O Christ, and we glorify
Your Resurrection.
Verse: O praise Him with sound of trumpet, praise Him
with lute and harp. [Psalm 150:3]
You endured the cross and abolished death; You arose
from the dead. Make our lives peaceful, O Lord, for You alone
are most powerful.
Verse: Praise Him with timbrel and dance, praise Him
with strings and pipes. [Psalm 150:4]
You despoiled Hades and raised up humanity at Your
Resurrection, O Christ. Make us worthy to praise and glorify
You with a pure heart.
Verse: O praise Him with resounding cymbals, praise
Him with clashing of cymbals. Let everything that lives and
that breathes give praise to the Lord. [Psalm 150:5-6]
We glorify Your divine condescension and sing hymns
to You, O Christ. You were born of the Virgin and remained
inseparable from the Father. As man, You suffered and
willingly endured the cross. Coming forth as if from a bridal
chamber, You arose from the grave to save the world. O Lord,
glory to You.
589

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then both choirs join together; they sing
the stichera of Pascha, Tone 5:
Verse: Let God arise and let His enemies be scattered, and
let those who hate Him flee from before His face. [Psalm 67:2]
Today the sacred Pasch is revealed to us, holy and new
Pasch, the mystical Passover, the venerable Passover, the
Pasch which is Christ the Redeemer, spotless Pasch, great
Pasch, the Pasch of the faithful, the Pasch which is the key
to the gates of Paradise, the Pasch which sanctifies all the
faithful.
Verse: As smoke vanishes, so let them vanish, as wax
melts before a fire. [Psalm 67:3]
O women, be the heralds of good news and tell what you
saw; tell of the vision and say to Zion: “Accept the good news
of joy from us, the news that Christ has risen.” Exalt and
celebrate and rejoice, O Jerusalem, seeing Christ the King,
coming forth from the tomb like a Bridegroom.
Verse: So let the wicked perish at the presence of God, but
let the righteous ones rejoice. [Psalm 67:3-4]
The myrrh-bearing women arrived just before the dawn at
the tomb of the Giver of Life and found an angel seated on the
stone who spoke these words to them: “Why do you seek the
living among the dead? Why do you mourn the incorruptible
among those subject to decay? Go announce the good news to
His disciples.”
Verse: This is the day the Lord has made; let us be glad
and rejoice in it. [Psalm 117:24]
Pasch so delightful, Pasch of the Lord, is the Pasch—most
honored Pasch now dawned on us. It is the Pasch! Therefore,
590

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

let us joyfully embrace one another. O Passover, save us
from sorrow; for today Christ has shown forth from the tomb
as from a bridal chamber and filled the women with joy by
saying: Announce the good news to the Apostles.
Glory: now and ever, Tone 5:
This is the Resurrection Day! Let us be enlightened by this
Feast and let us embrace one another! Let us call “Brethren”
even those who hate us, and in the Resurrection, forgive
everything and let us sing:
Christ is risen from the dead! By death He trampled

Priest: O most holy Theotokos, save us.
Choir: Shine in splendor:
After this, the principal celebrant: Glory to You, O Christ

Choir: Christ is risen from the dead! By death He trampled
Death; and to those in the tombs He granted life. Lord, have

591

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

And immediately the principal celebrant says the dismissal
with the cross:
May Christ our true God, risen from the dead, by death
trampling Death and granting life to those in the tombs, have
mercy on us and save us through the prayers of His most
pure Mother and of all the saints, for Christ is good and loves
mankind.
Then, raising the cross, he says: Christ is risen, three
times. We respond: Indeed, He is risen, three times. Then, we
sing the final Christ is risen: three times, the entire troparion.
And following this we conclude the hymn: And to us He
granted life eternal. Let us bow before His resurrection on the
third day!
And we kiss the most pure cross, held in the hand of the
principal celebrant.

THE HOURS ON HOLY PASCHA
and on all of Bright Week

The priest beginning: Blessed is our God: we say three

Having beheld the resurrection of Christ let us worship the
holy Lord Jesus Who alone is sinless. We bow to Your cross,
O Christ, and we glorify and praise Your holy Resurrection.
You are our God, and besides You we recognize no other,
and we call upon Your Name. Come, all you faithful, and let
us bow to the holy Resurrection of Christ since, through the
cross, joy has come to all the world. Ever blessing the Lord,
let us extol His Resurrection since He, having suffered the
crucifixion, has destroyed Death by His death.
Then the Hypakoj, once:
The women with Mary before the dawn found the stone
rolled away from the tomb, and they heard the angel say:
“Why do you seek among the dead, as a mortal, the One Who
abides in everlasting light? Behold the linens of burial. Go
in haste and proclaim to the world that, having conquered
Death, the Lord is risen; for He is the Son of God, the Savior
of mankind.”

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then the Kontakion, once:
Although You descended into the grave, O Immortal One,
You destroyed Hades’ power. You arose as a victor, O Christ
God. You exclaimed to the myrrh-bearing women: Rejoice!
You gave peace to Your apostles and granted resurrection to
the fallen.
And then this Troparion, once:
When Your body was in the tomb, and Your soul in Hades,
when You were in paradise with the thief, You were at the
same time, O Christ, as God upon Your throne with the Father
and the Spirit, infinite and filling all things.
Glory:
Your life-giving tomb, O Christ, has appeared to us as
truly more precious than paradise and more brilliant than any
other dwelling place. It is the source of our resurrection.
Now and ever: Theotokion
Rejoice, O sanctified dwelling place and divine tabernacle
of the Most High! It is through you, O Theotokos, that joy

Then, Lord, have mercy, 40. Glory: now and ever: More

mercy, three times. Give the blessing.

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

And the Dismissal of the First Hour.
The same model is sung for the 3rd, for the 6th, and the
9 Hour, and for Compline, likewise, also, for the Midnight
Service.
th

595

VESPERS ON THE EVENING OF THE
HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA
After the 9th Hour, and on the entire Bright Week, the
principal celebrant vests in all the priestly vestments. And
having stood before the Holy Table with the censer, he makes
the sign of the cross [with it], and says aloud:
Blessed is our God always, now and ever and forever. And
we respond: Amen. And he begins: Christ is risen from the
dead! By death He trampled Death; and to those in the tombs
He granted life. Three times. And we also respond three times.
And the principal celebrant says the introductory verses: 1st:
Let God arise: 2nd: As smoke vanishes: 3rd: So let the wicked
perish: 4th: This is the day the Lord has made: We sing on
each verse: Christ is risen: once after each. Glory: We again:
Christ is risen: Now and ever: We again: Christ is risen: And
again, the principal celebrant: Christ is risen from the dead!
By death He trampled Death: And we conclude: and to those
in the tombs He granted life. Then the Great Ektenia by the
Deacon: In peace, let us pray to the Lord.
After this: Lord, I have called: and what follows.
The Entrance with the Gospel Book. O Joyful Light:
596

ORDER OF THE HOLY AND GREAT SUNDAY OF PASCHA

Then, the Great Prokeimenon, Tone 7:
What God is as great as our God? You are the God Who
works wonders!
1: You showed Your power among the peoples. Your
strong arm redeemed Your people.
2: I said: Now I begin, and this is the will of the Most
High.
3: I remember the deeds of the Lord. I remember Your
wonders of old.
And again: What God is great:
After the prokeimenon, the deacon intones:
That we may be deemed worthy of hearing the holy Gospel,
let us pray to the Lord our God.
After this the principal celebrant reads the gospel, from
John, pericope 65: On the evening of the first day: the end:
in His Name.
After this, the ektenia: Let us all say: and Count us worthy,
O Lord…this evening: Then: Let us complete our evening
prayer:
After the exclamation we sing the stichera of the
Resurrection, Tone 2:
Your resurrection, O Christ our Savior, has enlightened
the whole universe; and through it, You call back to Yourself
all creation. Almighty God, glory to You.
Then the Paschal stichera, Tone 5: Today the sacred
Pasch: with their refrains. Glory: now and ever: It is the
Resurrection Day: Christ is risen, three times.
597

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

Then the deacon: Wisdom. We: Give the blessing.
Principal celebrant: Blessed is Christ our God, the One-WhoIs: And we: O God, strengthen: Then the principal celebrant:
O most holy Theotokos, save us. And we: Shine in splendor:
Then the principal celebrant: Glory to You, O Christ our God:
Choir: Christ is risen from the dead! By death He trampled
Death; and to those in the tombs He granted life. Lord, have
mercy. 3. Give the blessing.
And immediately he says the Dismissal
with the cross:
May Christ our true God, risen from the dead, by death
trampling Death and granting life to those in the tombs, have
mercy on us and save us through the prayers of His most
pure Mother and of all the saints, for Christ is good and loves
mankind.
Then raising the cross, he says: Christ is risen, three times.
We respond: Indeed, He is risen, three times. Then we sing the
conclusion: Christ is risen: three times, the entire troparion.
And after, we conclude the hymn: And to us He granted life
eternal. Let us bow before His resurrection on the third day!

evening, morning, and at noon.

SUNDAY OF THE HOLY APOSTLE THOMAS
Troparion, Tone 7:
Though the tomb had been sealed, O Life, from the grave

according to Your great mercy.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
With his probing right hand, Thomas searched Your lifegiving side, O Christ our God. When You entered, although
the doors were locked, he cried out to You with the other
apostles: You are my Lord and my God.

Dismissal:
Coming to His disciples although the doors were locked

THE SUNDAY OF THE MYRRH-BEARERS
Troparion of the Resurrection, Tone 2:
When You descended to death, O Immortal Life, You
destroyed Hades by the brilliance of Your divinity; and when
You raised the dead from the depths of the earth, all the
heavenly powers cried out: O Giver of Life, Christ our God,
glory to You.
And: The noble Joseph took down Your most pure body
from the cross. He wrapped it in a clean shroud and with
fragrant spices laid it in burial in a new tomb. But You, O
Lord, arose on the third day, bestowing great mercy upon the
world.
And: The angel standing by the tomb cried out to the
myrrh-bearing women: Myrrh is fitting for the dead, but Christ
has shown himself not subject to corruption. So now cry out:
The Lord is risen, bestowing great mercy upon the world.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
By Your resurrection, O Christ our God, You told the
myrrh-bearers to rejoice; and You stilled the weeping of Eve,
the first mother. You commanded Your apostles to proclaim:
The Savior is risen from the tomb.

Kontakion of Pascha:
Although You descended into the grave, O immortal One,
You destroyed Hades’ power. You arose as a victor, O Christ
God. You exclaimed to the myrrh-bearing women: Rejoice!
You gave peace to Your apostles and granted resurrection to
the fallen.
THE SUNDAY OF THE PARALYTIC
Troparion of the Resurrection, Tone 3:
Let the heavens rejoice, let the earth be glad; for the Lord
has shown the might of His arm. By His death the Lord has
trampled Death; He has become the first-born of the dead; He
has delivered us from the depths of Hades and has granted
great mercy to the world.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
O Lord, with Your divine authority, as You once raised
the paralytic, now raise my soul, paralyzed dreadfully with all
kinds of sin and disgraceful deeds, that, being saved, I may
cry out to You: Glory to Your power, O merciful Christ.
MID-PENTECOST WEDNESDAY
Troparion, Tone 8:
In the middle of the feast, quench the thirst of my soul
with streams of devotion. For You, O Savior, have exclaimed
to all: Let anyone who thirsts come to Me and drink. O Christ
our God, Fountain of Life, glory to You!

At the foot of the cross of her Son stood the virgin Mother
with the virginal disciple. She could not bear to gaze upon Him
lifted up on the cross. Overcome by grief she cried out: How
can You suffer when God cannot suffer? My Son, I glorify
Your unspeakable benevolence which surpasses every mind.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Seeing You nailed to the cross, Jesus, and witnessing
Your voluntary sufferings, O Master, the virgin Mother cried
out: Woe is me, O sweet Child! How unjustly You bear these
wounds, O Healer of human infirmities! By Your mercy You
have delivered all from corruption.

612

Menologion

613

614

On Signs
for Feasts of the Master and
of the Theotokos and of the Saints
Be it known that feasts are divided into Great, Middle,
and Small.
The Great Class of Feasts are the following:
The Feasts of Christ
The Feasts of the Theotokos
The Nativity and the Beheading of
		
Saint John the Baptist
The Feast of the Leaders of the Apostles,
		
Peter and Paul.
In the liturgical books these great feasts are denoted by a
cross in a circle:
This indicates that the feast has a vigil and the entire
service for the feast is taken according to the rule.
The Middle Class of Feasts is divided into two:
The first group is designated by a cross with a half circle.
This group has a vigil and the Canon of the Theotokos is
sung at Matins according to the rules.
The second group is designated by a cross.
This group has no vigil. At Vespers: “Blessed is the
615

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

man…”, the First Antiphon of the First Kathisma is taken, and
on the Psalm 140 “Lord, I have cried to you…”, six stichera
are taken, or, if desired, eight. There are three readings from
the Scriptures and the Apostichera. At Matins the Polyeleos is
sung. There is also a Gospel reading. There are eight odes at
the Canon. The Great Doxology is sung, and all the rest of the
service according to the rules.
The Small Class of Feasts has two groups.
The first group of the Small Class is designated by three
dots in an imperfect [open] circle printed in red.
At Vespers the usual Kathisma is chanted. On the Psalm
140 “Lord, I have cried to you…” six stichera are taken. There
are six odes of the Canon at Matins. The Great Doxology is
sung and all the rest of the service according to the rules.
The second group of the Small Class is designated by
three dots in an imperfect [open] circle printed in black.
On the Psalm 140 “Lord, I have cried to you…” at Vespers
there are only six stichera. At Matins there are six odes at the
Canon. At the Liturgy all is taken according to the rules.
When there is no sign whatsoever, there are but three
stichera at Vespers and four at the Canon at Matins.

Menologion

1

September

The Beginning of the Indiction, that is,
the New Church Year.
Our Venerable Father Simeon the Stylite
and his Mother (459).
The Synaxis of the most holy Theotokos of Miasena.
The Holy Martyr Aeithalas (380).
The Forty Holy Women martyred with their 		
Instructor Ammon the Deacon (313).
The Holy Martyr Callista and her two Brothers,
Evodius and Hermogenes (309).
Joshua the Just, Son of Nun.
Troparion of the New Year, Tone 2:

O Lord, Maker of the universe, Who alone have power
over times and seasons, bless the crown of this year with Your
bounty, preserve Your country in safety, keep Your people in
peace, and save us through the prayers of the Theotokos.
And of the Venerable Father, Tone 1:
You became a column of endurance and rivaled the
forefathers, O venerable one, becoming like Job in your
sufferings and like Joseph in your trials, like the bodiless
angels, though you lived in the flesh. O Simeon, our father,
pray to Christ God that He may save our souls.
617

Menologion - September

And of the Theotokos, Tone 1:
Rejoice, O Virgin Theotokos full of grace, refuge and
intercessor of the human race, for from you the Savior of the
world was incarnate. As you alone are Mother and Virgin,
ever-blessed and most-glorified, pray to Christ God to grant
peace to the whole universe.
Kontakion of the New Year, Tone 2:
O Christ the King Who dwells on high, Creator and
Maker of all that is visible and invisible, You Who made both
day and night, and time and years, now bless the crown of
this new year. Protect and keep in peace our government,
Your right-believing kings, this city, and Your people, O Most
Merciful One.
Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 2:
You sought that which is on high and became like an angel.
You made of your pillar a chariot of fire. Now that you are a
companion of the angels, join them in praying ceaselessly to
Christ God for all of us, O venerable father.

2

The Holy Martyr Mammas (274).
Our Venerable Father John the Faster, Patriarch of
Constantinople (595).
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr Mammas, O Lord our God: see page 550.

618

Menologion - September

Troparion of the Venerable Hierarch, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 3:
O holy Mammas, with the staff God gave to you, lead
your people as a flock to life-giving pastures; crush the fierce
and invisible enemies beneath the feet of those who sing to
you; for all those in danger have received you as their fervent
intercessor.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 3:
You proved yourself a heavenly vessel of abstinence, O
blessed John, and a lasting treasure of piety. Your life was
radiant with perfect self-control, and you enriched the poor
with alms, O venerable father; pray to Christ God to give
great mercy to us.

3

The Holy Priest-Martyr Anthimus, Bishop of
Nicomedia (303).
Our Venerable Father Theoctistus, Companion of our
Venerable Father Euthymius the Great (431).
Troparion of a Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:

You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Troparion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
Your abundant tears made the wilderness bloom, and
your sufferings made your labors fruitful a hundred-fold; you
became a shining torch over the world. O Theoctistos, our
father, pray to Christ God that He may save our souls.
619

Menologion - September

Kontakion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:
You were outstanding among bishops and traveled the
path to martyrdom. You vanquished pagan idol worship and
were the protector of your flock, O God-wise one. Therefore,
we now honor you, mystically crying out: deliver us from
dangers through your prayers, O ever-memorable Anthimus.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 4:
You joined the great Euthymius in the desert, and you
became an angel on earth with your good works. O Father, you
cleanse the hearts of the faithful by the power of wonderful
signs. We venerate you with love for this, O Theoctistos.

4

The Holy Priest-Martyr Babylas, Bishop of Great
Antioch (283).
The Holy Prophet Moses, who saw God.
Troparion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:

You shared in the apostles’ way of life and succeeded to
their throne, divinely inspired bishop. You found access to
contemplation in the active life. Therefore, you rightly taught
the word of truth and struggled for the faith to the shedding of
your blood. O priest-martyr Babylas, pray to Christ our God
to save our souls.
Troparion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
As we celebrate the memory of your prophet Moses, O
Lord, we implore you to save our souls through his prayers.
620

Menologion - September

Or this troparion in the same tone:
O prophet Moses, you reached the summit of virtues. By
this you came to see the glory of God. You received the tablets
of the grace-giving Law and became the crown of prophets
and a mystery of piety; for you carried grace deep within you.
Kontakion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 8:
O glorious Babylas, the Church glorifies you. Today
you are revered as a preacher of holiness and the fortitude
of martyrs. Since you have confidence before the Lord, beg
Christ to protect us; for we praise and glorify you, O longsuffering martyr.
Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
Because their prophecy is fulfilled among us, Moses,
Aaron, and the choir of prophets rejoice. The cross is
triumphant today because by it You saved us. Through their
prayers, O Christ God, have mercy on us.

5

The Holy Prophet Zachary [and his Wife, the
Holy and Venerable Elizabeth], Parents of the
glorious John the Forerunner.
Troparion of Zechariah, Tone 4:

Arrayed in the vestment of a priest, O wise Zechariah,
you offered in a priestly manner worthy whole-burnt offerings
according to the law of God. You became a shining light and a
witness of the mysteries, clearly bearing within you the signs
of grace, O all-wise one. You were slain by the sword in God’s
temple. O prophet of Christ, together with the Forerunner,
intercede with God that He may save our souls.
621

Menologion - September

Kontakion of Zechariah, Tone 3:
Today Zechariah the prophet and priest of the Most
High, and the father of the Forerunner, has set the table of his
memorial and mixed the drink of righteousness, nourishing
all the faithful. For them he has died as a divine mystic of the
grace of God.

6

The Commemoration of the Miracle of the Holy
Archangel Michael at Colossae in Chionia.
The Holy Martyr Eudoxius and his Companions
(c. 311).
Our Venerable Father Archippus.
Troparion of the Archangel, Tone 4:

Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us by your prayers and to
shelter us beneath the wings of your sublime glory. Watch
over us who bow to you and cry out fervently: deliver us from
danger, for you are the commanders of the powers on high.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr Eudoxius, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Archangel, Tone 2:
Leaders of God’s armies and ministers of divine glory,
commanders of angels and guides of mortals, plead on our
behalf for what we need and for great mercy; since you are the
leaders of the heavenly hosts.
622

Menologion - September

Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 8:
You gathered wealth in heaven and showered it upon the
earth. You gave bread to the hungry and received a glorious
crown. You are resplendent in your confession of Christ. You
were brave and died at the hands of the law; thus you have
earned the wages of your work. O long-suffering Eudoxius,
pray to Christ God to grant us remission of sins.

7

Pre-festive Day of the Nativity of the most
Holy Theotokos.
The Holy Martyr Sozon (304).
Troparion of the Prefestive, Tone 4:

Today is born to us from the root of Jesse and the loins
of David, Mary, the godly child. Therefore, all creation
rejoices and is renewed. Heaven and earth rejoice together.
You families of nations sing her praise. Joachim is elated and
Anna cries out in celebration: the barren woman gives birth to
the Theotokos and the Sustainer of our life.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr Sozon, O Lord our God, in his struggle,
received an incorruptible crown from You. With Your
strength, he brought down the tyrants and broke the cowardly
valor of demons. Through his prayers, O Christ our God, save
our souls.
Kontakion of the Theotokos, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin Mary, the Theotokos, is born from a
barren womb according to the divine plan. She is the inviolate
bridal chamber of the heavenly Bridegroom. The chariot of
623

Menologion - September

the Word is made ready, for this is why she was preordained to
be the gateway of God and truly the Mother of Life.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 2:
Let us gather today and sing aloud to Sozon, the genuine
and God-wise martyr, masterful sufferer for piety, mystical
seer of divine grace, generous provider of healing; for he
prays to Christ God for all of us.

8

THE NATIVITY OF OUR MOST HOLY LADY,
THE THEOTOKOS AND
EVER-VIRGIN MARY.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your birth, O Virgin Theotokos, heralded joy to the
universe; for from you arose the Sun of Justice, Christ our
God. Removing the curse, He gave the blessing, and by
destroying Death, He granted us eternal life.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
At your holy birth, O Immaculate One, Joachim and Anna
were freed from the reproach of childlessness and Adam and
Eve from the corruption of death. Your people, delivered from
the guilt of their faults, celebrate your birth and cry out: the
barren woman gives birth to the Theotokos and Sustainer of
our Life.

Menologion - September

9

The Synaxis of the Holy and Just Grandparents
of God Joachim and Anna.
The Holy Martyr Severian (320).
Troparion of the Feast
And of the Saints, Tone 2:

We celebrate the memory of Your grandparents, O Lord,
and we pray to You to save our souls.
Or this one, Tone 1:
Joachim and Anna, since you were righteous under the law
of grace, you gave birth to the God-given infant for our sakes.
Therefore, today the Church of God solemnly celebrates your
honorable memory joyfully in radiance, giving glory to God
Who has raised up a horn of salvation for us from the House
of David.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr Severian, O Lord our God, See page 550.
Kontakion of the Grandparents, Tone 3:
Today Anna rejoices because the chains of infertility are
broken. She feeds the most pure Lady and invites all to sing
to Him Who gave for all people the only Mother and Virgin
from her womb.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 1:
With a soul armed with courage, O God-wise one, you
yourself were given over to various sufferings because you
were enflamed with love of the Master, O most-wealthy one.
Therefore, you accused the unjust torturer, O Severian, and
you were given an incorruptible triumphal crown by God.
