Menologion - September

10

The Holy Martyrs Menodora, Mitrodora, and 		
Nymphodora (306).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Women Martyrs, Tone 4:

You traded violent tortures and bitter death for eternal
life. Three virgins professed the Uncreated Trinity before a
false judge at an illegal trial. You followed the footsteps of the
slaughtered Lamb when they pierced you with a sword. Pray
for those who honor your memory.
Kontakion of the Women Martyrs, Tone 4:
Fearless as you were in your struggles for the Holy Trinity
and because of your sisterly love for each other, you defeated
the enemy of your spiritual life. Therefore, in the company
of the five virgins you entered victoriously into the heavenly
mansions where you are forever joyful with the angels in the
presence of the King of all.

11

Our Venerable Mother Theodora of Alexandria (490).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:

In you, O mother, the divine image was strictly preserved;
taking up your cross, you followed Christ. You taught us by
example how to spurn the flesh, for it passes away, and how to
626

Menologion - September

care for the soul, which is immortal. Therefore, O venerable
Theodora, your soul rejoices with the angels.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 2:
Having exhausted your body with fasting, with vigilant
prayers you entreated the Creator concerning your deeds, that
you might receive complete remission. You manifestly acquired
this, O mother, having shown us the path of repentance.

12

The Holy Priest-Martyr Autonomus (c. 300).
Troparion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:

As you are a venerable bishop and a martyr for the faith,
the Church calls us to praise your holy memory and to celebrate
with faith, O splendid and glorious Autonomus, who pleased
the Trinity. Pray for us to God, the only Lover of Mankind.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O most wise one, you worthily offered the Divine
Mysteries, You became an acceptable offering, O God-blessed
one. You drank from the cup of Christ, O most glorious one;
O candlelabrum of the whole world, pray unceasingly for all
of us.
On this day is the Leave-taking of the Feast of the
Nativity of the most Holy Theotokos.

The Commemoration of the Dedication of the
		
Holy Church of the Resurrection of
		
Christ our God in Jerusalem (335).
Prefestive of the Exaltation of the Precious
		
and Life-creating Cross
The Holy Bishop-Martyr Cornelius
the Centurion.
Troparion of the Dedication, Tone 4:

Lord, Life, and Resurrection of All, You showed the
beauty of the holy dwelling place of Your glory on earth like
the splendor of the firmament on high. Make it stand firm
forever. Through the Theotokos, accept our prayers which we
unceasingly offer to You within it.
Troparion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life, See page 551.
Troparion of the Prefestive, Tone 4:
Lord, we offer to You in intercession the goodness of
Your life-creating cross which You gave to us, Your unworthy
people. Save our nation and Your Church which implores You
through the Theotokos. For You alone love mankind.
Kontakion of the Dedication, Tone 4:
You have made of the Church a resplendent heaven,
enlightening all the faithful. Therefore, we stand in the midst
of this holy dwelling place and we cry out to You: make firm
this house, O Lord.
628

Menologion - September

Or this one, Tone 2:
Grant the renewal of the spirit in our hearts and the
enlightenment of our souls to those who faithfully restore the
temple - Your home. For You have blessed its creation in honor
of Your Divine name, the Only One glorified in the saints!
Kontakion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:
O God-wise Cornelius, priest of the Mysteries, the
Church, receiving you as the holy first-fruit of the Gentiles, is
enlightened by the acts of your good deeds.
Kontakion of the Prefestive, Tone 8:
Today the saving wood shines forth from the bosom of the
earth. It is reverently lifted up in the church by the hands of
the bishop. The whole world prostrates and kisses it with awe.
Save us through Your cross, O Lord.

THE UNIVERSAL EXALTATION OF THE
PRECIOUS AND LIFE-CREATING CROSS.
Troparion, Tone 1:

Save Your people, O Lord, and bless your inheritance.
Grant victory to your Church over evil and protect Your
people by Your cross.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Christ our God, Who were willingly raised upon the cross,
grant Your mercies to the new people who bear Your Name.
By Your power grant joy to the Church. Give her victory over
evil with Your invincible trophy, the weapon of peace, as an
ally.

Menologion - September

15

The Holy Great Martyr Nicetas (372).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:

Your martyr, Nicetas, O Lord, see page 550.
Or, this Troparion, in the same tone:
You fervently took up the cross of Christ like a sword, and
you hastened to fight the enemy. You were burnt to death for
Christ, and thus you offered up your priestly soul to the Lord.
You have been rewarded with the gifts of healing from Him,
O great-martyr Nicetas; now pray to Christ God to save our
souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O Nicetas, your name means victory. You crushed the
power of deception by your resistance and received the crown
of victory through your suffering. You rejoice with the angels
in glory, praying unceasingly with them to Christ God for all
of us.

16

The Holy Great Martyr Euphemia the
All-Praiseworthy (303).
Troparion of the Feast.

630

Menologion - September

And the Troparion of the Saint, Tone 4:
Your lamb Euphemia, O Jesus, cries out in a loud voice: I
love You, my Bridegroom; I seek You with painful longing; I
am crucified with You; in your baptism, I am buried with You;
I suffer for You that I may reign with You; and I die for You
that I may live with You. Receive me as a spotless sacrifice
immolated with love for You. By her prayers, O merciful One,
save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
You honorably completed your good ascetic struggle,
all-praised Euphemia, and after your death you poured out
miraculous wonders and sanctified us. Therefore, we sing
your holy dormition, flowing into your divine church with
faith so that we may deliver ourselves from spiritual illnesses
and gain the grace of your miracles.

17

The Holy Martyr Sophia (Wisdom) and her three
Children, Faith [Vera], Hope [Nadežda],
and Charity [L’uba] (c. 137).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:

The Church solemnly celebrates and rejoices over the
newly-born children and their radiant mother. Named for
Wisdom and like her name, she gave birth to three children
equal to the three theological virtues. In the company of these
three wise virgins, she gazes on God the Word and Chaste
Groom. We join her in her happiness spiritually and sing: O
thrice-blessed martyrs, Faith, Hope, and Charity, make us firm
in faith, hope, and charity.
631

Menologion - September

Kontakion, Tone 1:
The three sacred branches of honorable Sophia, Faith
and Hope and Charity, have shown forth. Through grace they
confounded the wisdom of the Greeks. Through their suffering
and through being revealed as bearers of victory, Christ, the
Master of All, granted incorruptible crowns to them.

18

Our Venerable Father Eumenius the Wonder-worker,
Bishop of Gortyna (7th Century).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 7:

You enriched your life with fasting; you loved the poor
and gave them all you had. You were brighter than the sun
in virtue, cheering the sad and comforting the mourners. By
virtue of these riches and by your prayers, O father Eumenius,
now pray Christ to forgive our sins.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Illumined by the Divine Light, O all-blessed Eumenius,
enlighten us who sing of your honorable and glorious and
holy death with love. O father and hierarch Eumenius, pray
unceasingly for all of us.

Menologion - September

The Holy Martyrs Trophimus, Sabbatius, and
Dorymedontus (c. 227).
Troparion of the Feast.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 8:

God is praised in the Holy Trinity, and we praise the trinity
of martyrs, Trophimus, Sabbatius, and Dorymedontus. By
their faith, they conquered the enemy. Through their prayers,
O Christ God, have mercy on us.
Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 8:
The Church honors and glorifies your light-bearing
passion as a foundation of martyrs and confirmation of piety.
O ever-hymned blessed passion-bearer, divinely wise and
glorious Trophimus, and those who suffered with you, implore
cleansing for those who profess you, for you are invincible.

The Holy Martyr Eustace and his Companions
(118).
The Holy Martyrs and Confessors, the Great
Prince Michael and his Counselor Theodore,
Wonder-workers of Chernigov (1244).
Troparion of the Feast.

633

Menologion - September

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God, in their struggles received
incorruptible crowns from You. With Your strength, they
brought down the tyrants and broke the cowardly valor of
demons. Through their prayers, O Christ our God, save our
souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O holy Eustace, you were an imitator of Christ in His
passion. You drank of His cup with courage and thereby
became a sharer of His glory, receiving divine forgiveness
from on high from the God of all.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Having completed your life as martyrs, having been

God to protect your country according to His great mercy.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Perceiving an earthly kingdom as nothing and having
abandoned passing glory, you came to the labor of voluntary
ascetic effort. You preached the Trinity to the impure torturers,
O passion-bearer Michael and brave Theodore. Standing
before the King of Powers, pray to protect your country
without harm, and for us who venerate you unceasingly.

The Holy Prophet Jonah.

O holy Apostle Quadratus, intercede with the merciful

You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Troparion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
As we celebrate our prophet Jonah: see page 548.

O Lord, the world offers You the Apostle Quadratus, a

635

Menologion - September

Kontakion of Phocas, Tone 6:
As a bishop you offered the sacrifice, O father, and at the
end of your life you offered yourself. You gave witness to
Christ God before the law, strengthened by angels and ready
for death. Be ever with those who sing to you: be with us,
Phocas, and never against us.
Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 4:
You accepted God’s decree and became a marvelous
prophet. You remained in the whale for three days as an image
of the third day Resurrection. You left the whale unharmed.
You were a confessor of the faith in the great city of Nineveh.
For all of this we come to praise you, Jonah, as a type of Christ
God Who loves mankind.

The Conception of the Honorable, Glorious
Prophet, Forerunner, and Baptist John.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Joy to you, O barren one, unable to give birth; behold, you

will enlighten the whole world that suffers from blindness.
Rejoice, O Zechariah, and cry out in all confidence: the
prophet of the Most High is about to be born!
Kontakion, Tone 1:
Great Zechariah is radiant in joy with his wife, the allglorious Elizabeth, for she has conceived John the Forerunner
whom the angel announced with rejoicing, and whom we
humans honor properly as the mystical passage of grace.

Menologion - September

24

The Holy Martyr, First Among Women, and 		
Equal to the Apostles, Thecla (51).
Troparion, Tone 4:

O bride of God, Thecla, you were instructed by the words
of Paul; you were made firm in the faith by Peter. You were
revealed the first martyr called by God among women and
the first woman to suffer. You walked into the flames as into
a flowering garden; the beasts and the brutes were frightened
of you, for you were armed with the cross. O all-praiseworthy
Thecla, pray to Christ God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
You were radiant with the goodness of virginity and
you were adorned with the crown of martyrdom. You were
entrusted with the work of the apostles, O Virgin Thecla, for
you are most glorious since you transformed the flames of the
fire into dew. Through your prayers, you tamed the anger of
the youth, for you were the first woman to suffer martyrdom.

Our Venerable Mother Euphrosyne (479).
Troparion, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: See page 554.
Kontakion, Tone 2:

When you longed for life in the highest, you turned away
from the longest delight of the world. You put on the clothing
of a man, all beautiful one, and abandoned your earthly
betrothed for Christ your Bridegroom before the time.

The Passing of the Holy Apostle and Evangelist
John the Theologian.
Troparion, Tone 2:

Beloved Apostle of Christ God, hasten to deliver a

to Christ, O Theologian, that He may overcome the darkness
of pagan nations, and beg that He grant us peace and abundant

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Who can tell of your mighty deeds, O virgin saint? You
pour forth miracles, and you are a source of healings, and as

You mingled your confession in the fountain of your

Our Venerable Father Cyriacus the Anchorite (557).
Troparion, Tone 1:

You made the wilderness your dwelling, O father
Cyriacus, the bearer of God. You became an angel in the
flesh and a wonderworker. Through prayers, fast, and vigils,
you obtained from God special graces to heal the sick and to
sanctify the souls of those who come to you with trust. Glory
to the One Who gave you strength! Glory to the One Who
crowned you! Glory to the One Who through your intercession
grants healing to all!

Menologion - September

Kontakion, Tone 8:
The holy lavra always honors you as a powerful protector

Another Kontakion, Tone 2:
With the divine weapon of purity of spirit, and armed
with unceasing prayer as with a powerful spear, you
were like a sickle cutting down the demonic temptation.
Cyriacus our father, pray unceasingly for all of us.

THE PROTECTION OF THE MOST
HOLY THEOTOKOS.
The Holy Apostle Ananias, one of the Seventy.
Our Venerable Father Romanus the Melodist (496)

Troparion of the Theotokos, Tone 4:
Protected by your appearance, O Theotokos; today, we
devout people solemnly celebrate. Gazing upon your most
pure icon, we fervently say: Protect us with your holy veil,
and deliver us from all evil, imploring your Son, Christ our
God, to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin is present in the Church, and with the
choirs of saints, invisibly prays to God for us. The angels
worship with the hierarchs, the apostles rejoice with the
prophets; because the Theotokos prays for us to the eternal
God.
Troparion of the Apostle, Tone 3:
O holy Apostle Ananias, intercede with the merciful God
that He may grant our souls forgiveness of sins.
Troparion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image was strictly preserved;
taking up your cross, you followed Christ. You taught us by
example how to spurn the flesh, for it passes away, and how to
641

Menologion - October

care for the soul, which is immortal. Therefore, O venerable
Romanus, your soul rejoices with the angels.
Kontakion of the Apostle, Tone 2:
With fervent prayers O Intercessor, and asking a speedy
hearing, accept our prayers, O Ananias, and pray to Christ to
have mercy on us, O unique one reposed among the saints.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
You were adorned from childhood with the divine virtues
of the spirit, O all-wise Romanus, you were a precious
adornment of the church of Christ. For you made it lovely
with beautiful hymnody. Therefore, we pray to you: grant
your divine gift to those who desire it, that we may cry out to
you: Rejoice O all-blessed father, beauty of the Church.

The Holy Bishop-Martyr Cyprian (258).
The Holy Martyr Justina (258).

You renounced the magic arts O God-wise one, in order

The Holy Bishop-Martyr Dionysius the Areopagite.
Troparion, Tone 4:
You learned goodness and practiced temperance in

Menologion - October

all things. You robed yourself in the priesthood and girded

In a spiritual way you passed through the gates of heaven,

As an inviolable pillar, O Hierotheus, you were not afraid
of intimidating enemies, but you destroyed the stronghold of

The Holy Martyr Charitina (304).

The Holy and Glorious Apostle Thomas.
Troparion, Tone 2:

You were both a disciple of Christ and a member of

O Thomas, full of wisdom and grace, you were a disciple

Menologion - October

Menologion - October

You were shown to be a citizen of the desert: see page 565.
Kontakion of the Apostle, Tone 2:
Let us extol James with praises as a herald of God, for he
implanted wise doctrines deeply in pious souls. Now he stands
before the throne of the Master and rejoices in the company of
angels, praying for all of us unceasingly.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
You took the light burden of the Lord on your shoulders
and followed Him, O Andronicus, and hated the worldly
worries and settled in the desert, O blessed one, where you
perfectly performed the discipline of fasting, uniting with
God. That is why we sing to you: pray to Christ God to grant
us forgiveness of our sins, that we may honor your holy
memory with love.

The Holy Martyrs Eulampius and Eulampia (302).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551

Kontakion, Tone 3:
Let us honor the wise Eulampius and Eulampia, fearless
martyrs. They were brother and sister in the flesh. Through
the power of the crucified Christ, they put to shame their
persecutors’ guile, and together they became the glory and
praise of martyrs.

Menologion - October

O Christ our God, You are above all praise. You have

Menologion - October

Kontakion, Tone 6:
The Son shone forth from the Father indescribably. In two
natures he was born of a woman. Recognizing this, we do
not reject the representation of His human form; rather, we
depict it with reverence and honor it with faith. Therefore, the
Church holds fast to the true faith and kisses the image of the
incarnation of Christ.

The angelic powers of heaven were rapt in amazement

Our Venerable Mother Paraskeva of Trnovo (1201).
Troparion, Tone 4:
You followed closely in the steps of Christ, your Spouse,
loving the silent, desert life. As a young woman you took up

of the cross. By fasting and prayer, by tears and penance,
you utterly quenched the fires of passion. Now you stand
with the wise virgins in Christ’s presence in the heavenly
bridal chamber, and pray for us who honor your memory, O
Paraskeva, worthy of glory.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
Let us all sing of holy Paraskeva, holy intercessor of all who
are in trouble. For she rejected the corruptible and accepted the

As we celebrate the memory of Your prophet Hosea:

Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
With sure steps, you followed the commands of the Lord,

those who strayed from the path of justice and set them on
the road to the heavenly Jerusalem. Now you stand within that
city and implore the Lord, praying without ceasing for all of us.
Kontakion of the Venerable-Martyr, Tone 3:
Today Constantinople, Capital of the Byzantine Empire,

Menologion - October

and calls all cities and countries to participate. It rejoices in

The Holy and Glorious Great-Martyr Demetrius,

The Commemoration of the Great and Fearful

Troparion, Tone 3:

O Passion-bearer, the whole world has seen you as a

Demetrius, pray to Christ God to grant us great mercy.
Troparion of the Earthquake, Tone 8:
O Christ our God, Who look upon the earth, and it quakes:
deliver us from the dreadful threat of earthquakes, and send
down upon us Your rich mercies through the prayers of the
Theotokos and save us.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
With streams of your blood, O Demetrius, the God, Who
gives you invincible might, has dyed the Church in purple,
and keeps your city unharmed, for you are its foundation.
Kontakion of the Earthquake, Tone 6:
Deliver all of us from a powerful earthquake, O Lord, and
from unbearable wounds caused by our sins. O Lord, spare
Your [right-believing rulers and] people whom You have
purchased with Your Blood, O Master; and do not deliver our
cities to destruction by terrible earthquakes, for we do not
honor any other god besides You, O God. Answer those who
cry out to to You: “I am with you and no one can be against
you.”

[The Holy Priest-Martyr Theodore Romzha,

of Truth: Christ God. And as a zealous pastor you taught the

your life, and like the rock of faith you blocked the way of
godlessness. You accepted the priceless pearl of patience even
to the shedding of your blood. We who venerate you with
profound love now call to you: O priest-martyr Theodore,
pray for the souls of us sinners before the throne of the AllMerciful.]

father, pray to Christ God that He may save our souls.

You fought like a brave soldier against the hostile flesh,
and you battled spiritual enemies by deep fasting. You
vanquished legions of devils by humility and in the end have
shown yourself a great conqueror. You received power to
work wonders from God. O venerable Joannicus, now pray to
Him to save our souls.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.

Menologion - November

Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
You were revealed as a brilliant star enlightening the

were revealed as the mightiest physician. As you received the

may cry out: Rejoice, O father Joannicus.
Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
You were enlightened with the anointing of truth, and

praying to obtain purification through your prayers.

The Holy Martyrs Galaction and Episteme (253).

Kontakion, Tone 2:
O glorious Galaction, you and your honorable wife and

struggles. Therefore, pray unceasingly to the only God for all

Our Father among the saints, Paul the Confessor,

The Church sees you among her priests as another Paul

668

Menologion - November

Abel and Zechariah calls for you to the Lord. O venerable

The Holy Thirty-three Martyrs at Melitene (298).
Our Venerable Father Lazarus, the Wonder-worker,

Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:

Your martyrs, O Lord our God, see page 551.

Your falling tears and prayer vigils watered the pillar,

Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 8:
The radiant choir of martyrs, the light-bearing army,

memory, beseeching from You, our Savior: through their
prayers deliver us from distress that we might sing to You:

THE SYNAXIS OF THE ARCHANGEL 		
MICHAEL AND ALL THE BODILESS
POWERS OF HEAVEN.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us through your prayers and

danger, for you are the commanders of the powers on high.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Leaders of God’s armies and ministers of divine glory,
commanders of angels and guides of mortals, plead on our

Menologion - November

Troparion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image was strictly preserved;
taking up your cross, you followed Christ. You taught us by
example how to spurn the flesh, for it passes away, and how to
care for the soul, which is immortal. Therefore, O venerable

Kontakion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 2:
In your love for the Lord you disdained the desire for rest,

By your patience, you obtained your reward, O venerable

O John, most wise, by distributing all your wealth to the

The Holy Priest-martyr Josaphat, Archbishop of
Polotsk (1623).
Troparion, Tone 4:
You have become a brilliant light, O Priest-Martyr
Josaphat. You gave up your life for your sheep like the Good
Shepherd. You were slain by the lovers of schism, and you
have entered into the Holy of Holies to rest in the company
673

Menologion - November

of the angels. O long-suffering saint, we make this petition to

Kontakion, Tone 2:
You were enlightened by a spark from the crucified Christ
from the time when you were a child. You were like an angel
in monastic life, living in it with true holiness. You openly
preached unity, and with your martyr’s blood, you calmed the
hearts of those who had been tossed about with schism. Christ

pillar of unity.

Our Father among the saints, John Chrysostom,
Archbishop of Constantinople (407).
Troparion, Tone 8:

The grace shining forth from your mouth like a torch has
enlightened the universe; it has stored up in the world the
treasure of disdain for wealth. It has shown us the heights of
humility. Instruct us by your words, John Chrysostom, our
father, and intercede with the Word, Christ God, to save our
souls.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
You have received divine grace from heaven and with
your lips you teach all how to worship one God in the Trinity,
all-blessed venerable John Chrysostom. It is proper that we
praise you, for you are the teacher who reveals the divine.

Menologion - November

14

The Holy and All-praiseworthy Apostle Philip.
Troparion, Tone 3:

The whole world is adorned and Ethiopia sings for joy
at her crown. She received light from you, and is adorned by
your crown. O Philip, speaking in behalf of God, she solemnly
celebrates your memory. You taught everyone to believe in
Christ and you completed the course of the Gospel worthily.
Therefore, Ethiopia has come to lift their hands to God. Pray
to Him to grant us great mercy.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O Lord, Your disciple and friend and imitator of Your
passion, Philip, has preached You as God to the universe.
Through his prayers deliver Your Church from her lawless
enemies, and through the Theotokos protect every city, O
Most Merciful Christ.

The Holy Martyrs and Confessors Gurias, Samonas,

The Fast of the Nativity of Christ begins from here,
and goes until the day of the Nativity of Christ.
Troparion, Tone 5:
You granted us the miracles of Your holy martyrs as an
unshakable stronghold, O Christ God. Through their prayers,

the kingdom for You alone are good and love mankind.

Menologion - November

Having received grace from on high O wise ones, you

The Holy Apostle and Evangelist Matthew.
Troparion, Tone 3:

Earnestly you followed Christ the Master, Who in His
goodness appeared on earth to the human race. He called
you from the tax booth, revealing you as a chosen apostle,
the evangelist of the Gospel to all the world. Therefore, O
Matthew, speaking in behalf of God, we honor your precious
memory. Pray to the merciful God to grant remission of sins
to our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
When you renounced the yoke of the publican’s scale
and were united to the yoke of truth, you were revealed to
be a merchant of all-excellence, gathering in the riches of the
wisdom from on high. You were the herald for this cause, the
word of truth, and aroused souls from slothfulness by writing
about the day of judgment.

You became worthy of your name through your way of

Menologion - November

Kontakion, Tone 2:
You received the power to perform many miracles,

The Holy Great Martyr Catherine (310).
The Holy Great Martyr Mercury (c. 255).
Troparion of the Woman Saint, Tone 4:

You enlightened pagan philosophers with the light of

at night. You overcame the darkness and converted the queen.
You stood up to the torturer, O blessed Catherine, chosen
by God. On your wishes you were carried to the heavenly
bridal chamber of your splendid Bridegroom Christ. You
were espoused to him with a regal crown, O bride chosen by
God. In the company of the angels, pray for us who keep your
memory.

Your martyr, O Lord: see page 550.

O martyr Mercury, you were led to the struggle of your

King. You have gone confidently and were welcomed into
the ranks of the passion-bearers. Hasten to give help to the
faithful who hold fast to your memory.
Kontakion of the Woman Saint, Tone 2:
Let us who love the divine martyrs now raise up an
honorable choir honoring the all-wise Catherine. For this she
681

Menologion - November

preached Christ in the arena, and trampled down the serpents,
despising the wisdom of the long-winded orators.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 4:

warrior in battle and a sure defender in trouble. He delivers

If this day falls on Sunday, omit the service of Saint

Troparion of Clement, Tone 4:

Menologion - November

always fervently flow into the church given you by God, and

Our Venerable Father Alypius the Stylite (640).
Troparion, Tone 1:

You became a column of endurance and rivaled the

Or this, in Tone 4:
You seem a terror unscalable to the devils, crippling

passions by fasting. You are a firm support of those wavering.
O venerable father Alypius, beg Christ God for the salvation
of our souls.

The Commemoration of the Consecration of the
Church of the Holy Great Martyr George in
Kiev before the gates of Holy Wisdom Cathedral.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Today the ends of the world bless you when you were

Kontakion, Tone 2:

The Holy Martyr James the Persian (400).
Our Venerable Father Palladius (c. 600).
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:

You astonished everyone by enduring horrible torture with

performed the slaughter, you uttered prayers of thanksgiving
to the Lord. Through your suffering you received your crown,
and went up to the throne of the heavenly King, Christ God. O
James, pray to Him to save our souls.

Menologion - November

Kontakion of Irenarchus, Tone 1:
May you have an abundance of peace, O martyr, for you
laid hold of the enemy. You defeated that army of spiritual
deception by the power of divine grace. You endured the most
terrible sufferings. Now we beseech you to deliver from all
harm those who keep your memory, O Irenarchus.

1

December
The Holy Prophet Nahum.
If it is not Alleluia, Troparion, Tone 2:

As we celebrate the memory of Your prophet Nahum, O
Lord, we implore You to save our souls through his prayers.
Another Troparion, Tone 8:
By the radiance of the life-creating Trinity and the
enlightenment of the Spirit, the God-directed prophet Nahum
warned the idolatrous Ninevites of impending doom. You
reaped the reward in martyrdom. But now you rejoice in
heaven with the angelic choirs, standing in the presence of
the Triple Splendor, yet because you have the confidence of a
prophet, pray for us who always honor your memory.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Your pure heart was enlightened by the Spirit and became
a vessel of radiant prophecy. Because you saw as present the
events yet to come we honor you, O blessed and glorious
Prophet Nahum.

Menologion - December

Another Troparion, Tone 4:
O all-blessed Lamb, you were divinely enlightened by

the antagonist of enemies: for he took up the weapon, the
cross of the Lord, and overcame the temptation of heresy, and
stands as a fervent intercessor before God, so that He would
grant remission of sins to all.

691

Menologion - December

5

Our Venerable and God-bearing Father Sabbas
the Sanctified (532).

Troparion, Tone 8:
Your abundant tears made the wilderness bloom, and
your sufferings made your labors fruitful a hundred-fold; you
became a shining torch over the world. O Sabbas our father,
pray to Christ God that He may save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
You were offered up by your virtues, becoming a Gardener
of Piety, being a chaste offering to God from your youth,
O Blessed Sabbas. Therefore, you were the enrichment of
monastics, and a praiseworthy citizen of the desert. Therefore,
we cry out to you: rejoice, truly wealthy Sabbas.

6

OUR FATHER AMONG THE SAINTS
NICHOLAS THE WONDER-WORKER,
ARCHBISHOP OF MYRA IN LYCIA (343).

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you to your flock as a rule of faith,
an image of gentleness, and a teacher of moderation. You
acquired greatness through humility and wealth through
poverty. O father and archbishop Nicholas, intercede with
Christ our God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
You were renowned as a priest in Myra, O holy Nicholas;
for you fulfilled the Gospel of Christ, O venerable father. You
risked your life for your people and saved the innocent from
death. Thereby you have been initiated into the mysteries of
the grace of God.
692

Menologion - December

7

[Pre-festive Day of the Maternity.]
Our Father among the saints Ambrose,
Bishop of Milan (397).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your life has shown you to your flock as a rule of faith,
an image of gentleness, and a teacher of moderation. You
acquired greatness through humility and wealth through
poverty. O father and archbishop Ambrose, intercede with
Christ our God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Shining with divine teachings, you darkened the delusion
of Arius, O Priest of the Mysteries and Shepherd, Ambrose.
Working wonders by the power of the Spirit, you worked
wonders and healed diverse passions. O father and archbishop,
pray to Christ God for the salvation of our souls.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Today the beginning of our salvation is conceived in a
barren womb; and Anna rejoices with Joachim, Adam rejoices
to be freed, and with them, we also begin our hymn: rejoice, O
woman full of grace, the Lord is with you.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin Mary, the Theotokos, is born from a
barren womb according to the divine plan. She is the inviolate
bridal chamber of the heavenly Bridegroom. The chariot of
the Word is ready, for this is why she was preordained to be
the gateway of God and truly the Mother of Life.
693

Menologion - December

8

THE CONCEPTION OF THE HOLY ANNA
WHEN SHE CONCEIVED THE MOST
HOLY THEOTOKOS.

Troparion, Tone 4:
Today the bonds of barrenness are loosed, for God has
heard the prayers of Joachim and Anna. He promised, beyond
hope, the birth of their godly daughter. The Indescribable,
Himself, born of her as a mortal, commanded us through the
angel to sing to her: rejoice, O woman full of grace, the Lord
is with you.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Today the whole world celebrates how Anna became a
mother by the power of God. She conceived the woman whose
conception of the Word is beyond our words.

9

Our Venerable Father Patapius (7th Century).
Troparion, Tone 8:

In you, O father, the divine image was strictly preserved;
taking up your cross, you followed Christ. You taught us by
example how to spurn the flesh, for it passes away, and how to
care for the soul, which is immortal. Therefore, O venerable
Patapius, your soul rejoices with the angels.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
The people who come to your temple with reverence, O
Holy One, as a place of spiritual healing, ask to receive healing
of their infirmities and forgiveness of sins which they have
committed in their lives. For you are revealed, O venerable
Patapius, as an intercessor for all in need.
694

Menologion - December

10

The Holy Martyrs Menas, Hermogenes, and 		
Eugraphus (4th Century).
Troparion, Tone 8:

Having mortified the fiery visions and movements of the
passions by abstinence, the martyrs of Christ received grace to
dispel the ailments of the infirm, and to live even after death
to work wonders. O truly most glorious wonder, that naked
bones pour forth healing. Glory to the One God and Creator.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
Let us all honor with sweet singing Menas the wonderful,
Hermogenes the divine, and Eugraphus dedicated together,
for they honored the Lord and suffered honorably for Him,
and are worthy to be numbered with the bodiless choir in
heaven; and they are bountiful wonders.

11

Our Venerable Father Spiridon the Wonder-		
worker, Bishop of Tremithus (348).
Our Venerable Father Daniel the Stylite (489).

[In the traditional menologion, this day is the commemoration
of Saint Daniel the Stylite. Saint Spiridon the Wonder-worker
is commemorated on December 12.]
Troparion, Tone 1:
You became a column of endurance and rivaled the
forefathers, O venerable one, becoming like Job in your
sufferings and like Joseph in your trials, and like the bodiless
695

Menologion - December

angels though you lived in the flesh. O Daniel our father,
intercede with Christ God that He may save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Having ascended the pillar like a radiant star, O blessed
One, you illumined the world with your venerable deeds,
and dispelled the darkness of deception, O Father. Therefore,
we pray you: shine forth even now the never setting light of
understanding into the hearts of your servants.
Troparion of the Wonder-worker, Tone 1:
You were revealed as a champion of the First Council, and
a wonderworker, our God-bearing father Spiridon; for you
called out to the woman dead in the tomb and you transformed
the serpent into gold. And when you sang your holy prayers,
you had angels serving with you, O most holy one. Glory to
Him Who gave you strength. Glory to Him Who granted a
crown to you! Glory to Him Who through you grants healing
to all.
Kontakion of the Wonder-worker, Tone 2:
O all-holy father, enraptured by the love of Christ, you
soared on the wings of the Spirit to pure contemplation which
inspired your apostolic life, and you became an altar of
sacrifice, beseeching the Lord that He may enlighten all of us.

Troparion of the Resurrection.
Troparion of the Forefathers, Tone 8:
By faith, You, O Christ, justified the forefathers. Through

Menologion - December

The saints rejoice in Glory because a glorious offspring has

The Theotokos of Guadalupe (1531).

[When you appeared in the New World, O Theotokos, you
fixed your image on Juan Diego’s rose-laden tilma. All the

revealed the Son to us. O Mother of the Americas, imprint His

The Holy Martyrs Eustratius, Auxentius, Eugene,
Mardarius, and Orestes.
The Holy Martyr Lucy, the Virgin.

Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion of Eustratius, Tone 2:
You revealed the candlestick shining in darkness to those
sitting in unbelief, O Passion-bearer. For with faith like a
spear you fearlessly besieged the wandering enemies for you
are an eloquent orator.

14

The Holy Martyrs Thrysus, Leucas, Philemon, 		
Appolonius, and Callinicus (2nd Century).
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:

Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You showed the violence of the enemy in public after you
spat upon the barbarian torturer. You upheld the holiness of
the faith, finding your strength in the help of Christ. Now pray
for us, all you martyrs.
698

Menologion - December

15

The Holy Priest-martyr Eleutherius (120).
Our Venerable Father Paul of Latra (950).
Troparion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:

You shared in the apostles’ way of life and succeeded to
their throne, divinely inspired bishop. You found access to
contemplation in the active life. Therefore, you rightly taught
the word of truth and struggled for the faith to the shedding
of your blood. O Priest-Martyr Eleutherius, pray to Christ our
God to save our souls.
Troparion of the Venerable Man, in the same Tone:
You were numbered among the monks and a companion
of angels, and so we raise this song to you, O glorious Paul.
Pray that we may find mercy for our souls.
Kontakion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 2:
As an inspiration to priests, venerable father, and as one
who reenacted the Passion, we come with petitions and praise
to you. O Priest-Martyr Eleutherius: deliver us from trouble
of any kind. As we approach with love to keep your memory,
pray without ceasing for all of us.
Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 8:
You acted maturely from your childhood and spurned the
goods of the world. You became a temple of the Trinity in
your quest for the divine life. You enlighten those who come
to you. And so we sing: rejoice, generous father Paul.
Our Father among the saints Stephen the
Confessor, Archbishop of Surozh (c. 775).

Menologion - December

16

The Holy Prophet Haggai.
Troparion, Tone 2:
As we celebrate the memory: see page 548.
Or this, Tone 1:

Your eyes were opened to pure spiritual reality that is
all from God which you prophesied and understood, O allpraised prophet, guide of peaceful repentance. Therefore we
celebrate your holy memory, and we pray you, to intercede
especially with your prayers to God, O Haggai.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Your mind was enlightened with the fire of the Spirit; you
proclaimed the mysteries of God, O prophet. You revealed
what was to come, pointing to the mysteries of what was to
happen. Pray Christ God to have mercy on us.

17

The Holy Prophet Daniel and the Three Holy 		
Children, Hananiah, Azariah, and Mishael.
Troparion, Tone 2:

Great are the accomplishments of faith: the three holy
youths rejoiced in the streams of fire as if in refreshing waters;
and Daniel the prophet shepherded lions like sheep. Through
their prayers, O Christ our God, save our souls.

700

Menologion - December

Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 3:
Your pure heart was enlightened by the Holy Spirit so that
it could become an instrument of prophecy; you perceived
distant events as if they were present. When you were thrown
into the pit, you stopped the lions’ mouths. Therefore, we
honor you, O blessed and glorious prophet Daniel.
Kontakion of the Children, Tone 6:
You did not worship a man-made image, O thrice-blessed

The Holy Martyr Sebastian and his Companions (287).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 8:

O Sebastian, by the shedding of your blood you were
clothed in martyrdom, being arrayed in a robe of precious
purple. Therefore, you took up your abode with Christ in the
kingdom without end on high, and you received the crown of
glory with those who suffered with you. O wise Sebastian, as
you sing with them, always remember us.

20

Pre-festive Day of the Nativity in the flesh
of our Lord God and Savior Jesus Christ.
The Holy Priest-martyr Ignatius the God-bearer
(107).
Troparion of the Prefestive, Tone 4:

Bethlehem, make ready, Eden has been opened for all.
Ephrathah, prepare yourself, for the Tree of Life has blossomed
from the Virgin in the cave. Her womb has become a spiritual
paradise in which divinity was planted. If we partake of it, we
shall live and not die like Adam. Christ is born to raise up the
likeness that had fallen.
Troparion of Ignatius, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life and succeeded to
their throne, divinely inspired bishop. You found access to
contemplation in the active life. Therefore, you rightly taught
the word of truth and struggled for the faith to the shedding of
your blood. O Priest-martyr Ignatius, pray to Christ our God
to save our souls.
703

Menologion - December

Or this, in the same tone:
You followed the apostles’ way of life and succeeded
to their throne, you ascended to the vision of contemplation
through your deeds, O God-bearer, facing savage beasts, fire,
and sword for the sake of the Word of truth, and made the
course of truth straight even at the price of your own blood.
O priest-martyr Ignatius, pray to Christ God for the salvation
of our souls.
Kontakion of the Prefestive, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin is coming to the cave to give birth to the
eternal Word in a manner beyond expression. Let the world
dance when it hears the news; with the angels and shepherds
glorify the eternal God Who chose to appear as a newborn
child.
Kontakion of Ignatius, in the same tone:
The light-bearing day of your radiant ascetic fight
proclaims beforehand to all the One Who was born in a cave.
For thirsting lovingly to delight in Him, you hastened to be
devoured by wild beasts. For this you were called God-bearer,
O all-wise Ignatius.

21

The Holy Martyr Juliana [of Nicomedia] (304).
Troparion of the Prefestive.
And of the Woman Martyr, Tone 4:

Your lamb Juliana, O Jesus, cries out in a loud voice: I
love You, my Bridegroom; I seek You with painful longing; I
704

Menologion - December

am crucified with You; in Your baptism, I am buried with You;
I suffer for You that I may reign with You; and I die for You
that I may live with You. Receive me as a spotless sacrifice
immolated with love for You. By her prayers, O merciful One,
save our souls.
Kontakion of the Woman Martyr, Tone 3:
O virgin, made most pure with the goodness of virginity,
and now, having been crowned with the martyr’s crown, you
grant healing and salvation to those in need who approach
your shrine for Christ pours forth divine grace and eternal life.
Kontakion of the Prefestive, Tone 2:
As we see the One Who holds the world in his hands now
wrapped in swaddling clothes in Bethlehem, let us offer our
hymns in anticipation to the one who gave him birth; for with
a mother’s joy she cradles the Son of God.

22

The Holy Great Martyr Anastasia (304).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb, O Lord: see page 553.
Or this, in the same tone:

How truthfully named are you for the Resurrection, O
martyr of Christ. By enduring suffering you gained victory
over the enemy for the sake of Christ your Bridegroom. Pray
to Him to save our souls.

705

Menologion - December

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Those in temptations and afflictions hasten to your church,

23

The Holy Ten Martyrs of Crete (250).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Or this, Tone 3:

We honor Crete of many wonders from which these
precious flowers have shone forth, pearls of Christ and
offspring of martyrs. Although these blessed only numbered
ten, they overcame the idolatrous nation. Therefore, these
brave souls were given crowns.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
The noble struggle of the martyrs shines forth like the
morning star and sheds brilliant light for us on the One Who
was born in a cave, to whom the Virgin has given birth without
human seed.

Menologion - December

24

The Holy Great Martyr Eugenia (262).
Troparion of the Prefestive, Tone 4:

At that time, Mary registered in Bethlehem with the elder
Joseph who was of the house of David. She had conceived
without seed and was with child, and her time to give birth had
come. They found no room in the inn, but the cave became a
pleasant palace for the Queen. Christ is born to raise up the
likeness that had fallen.
Troparion of Eugenia, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: see page 554.
Kontakion of the Prefestive, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin is coming to the cave to give birth to the
eternal Word in a manner beyond expression. Let the world
dance when it hears the news; with the angels and shepherds
glorify the eternal God Who chose to appear as a newborn
child.
Kontakion of Eugenia, Tone 4:
You left the passing glory of the world to follow Christ,
and you kept immaculate the brilliance of your soul: O Godwise martyr, all-praised Eugenia.

707

Menologion - December

25

THE NATIVITY IN THE FLESH OF OUR
LORD GOD AND SAVIOR JESUS CHRIST.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your birth, O Christ our God, has shed upon the world
the light of knowledge; for through it, those who worshiped
the stars have learned from a star to worship You, the Sun of
Justice, and to know You, the Dawn from on High. Glory to
You, O Lord!
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Today the Virgin gives birth to the Transcendent One; and
the earth offers a cave to the Unapproachable. The angels sing
his glory with the shepherds; the wise men journey with the
star. The eternal God is born for us as an infant child.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who for our salvation was born
in a cave in Bethlehem of Judea and lay in a manger, have
mercy on us and save us through the prayers of His most pure
Mother; and of our venerable and God-bearing fathers, and
through the prayers of all the saints; for Christ is good and
loves mankind.

27

THE HOLY APOSTLE, FIRST MARTYR,
AND ARCHDEACON STEPHEN.
Our Venerable Father and Confessor Theodore
the Branded, Brother of Theophane the
Composer of Canons (845).
Troparion of the Apostle, Tone 4:

First martyr and Apostle of Christ, you fought the good
fight. You convicted the tyrants of their wickedness. When you
were killed by stoning at the hands of sinners, you received
a crown from God’s right hand while you cried out: Lord, do
not hold this sin against them.
Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 2:
Guide to Orthodoxy: see page 555.
Kontakion of the Apostle, Tone 3:
Yesterday, in human flesh the Master came to us; today,
from the flesh, His servant departs. Yesterday, the King was
born in the flesh; today, His servant is killed by stoning. Thus,
the holy Stephen, the first martyr, is brought to perfection.
Kontakion of the Venerable Man, in the same tone:
Your mouth spoke bravely, and you shamed the haughty
torturer by your great wisdom through suffering tortures: you
were grievously wounded on your face for the sake of the allhonorable icon of Christ which you taught us always to honor
and venerate. O Theodore, obtain great mercy for us.
710

Menologion - December

28

The Holy Twenty-thousand Martyrs burned at
Nicomedia (302).
Troparion, Tone 2:

O passion-bearers of the Lord, blessed is the earth that
received your blood, and holy is the place that received
your bodies. You have vanquished the enemy in battle and
proclaimed Christ with courage. We pray to you to intercede
with Him, the Good One, that He may save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O saints made steadfast in soul by faith, twenty thousand
accepted suffering by fire, calling out to Him Who was born
of the Virgin: accept our all-consumed burnt offering as You
accepted gifts of gold, myrrh and frankincense from the
Persian kings, O God existing from all eternity.

29

The Holy Innocents killed for Christ by Herod in
Bethlehem of Judea.
Our Venerable Father Marcellus, Hegumen of the
Akimetes [Sleepless Ones, that is, those
who keep prayer vigil day and night by turns]
Monastery(486).
Troparion, Tone 1:

O Lover of Mankind, accept the sufferings which Your
saints endured for You. As we pray, heal all our pains.

711

Menologion - December

Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Infants, Tone 6:
When the King was born in Bethlehem, wise men from
Persia came bringing gifts. They were led by the brilliant
star. But Herod became exceedingly agitated, and had the
infants harvested like lamenting wheat, for he sees his power
suddenly coming to an end.
Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 2:
You rose in the East shining like a radiant star, O allblessed Marcellus, and you edified with good deeds. You
were a teacher to many monks, O venerable one. Therefore,
you were a light to the imperial city. For this we sing to you:
rejoice, O all-blessed father.

30

The Holy Martyr Anysia.
The Venerable Zoticus, Priest and Protector of 		
Orphans (4th Century).
Troparion of the feast.
Troparion of the Woman Martyr, Tone 4:
Your lamb, O Jesus: see page 553.
Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image: see page 552.
712

Menologion - December

Kontakion of the Woman Martyr, Tone 3:
Today this martyr destroys the seduction of the devil by
faithful devotion and demolishes the enemy by the martyrdom
of suffering for the faith, and the angels  bestow upon her the
gift of a crown. For her sake, save us, O Savior of the world

Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 2:
You loved the poor for the love of Christ, and you gave
them aid and comfort. Now you have inherited heaven’s
wealth, O most-wealthy Zoticus. This is why we all venerate
you and solemnly celebrate your memory.

31

Our Venerable Mother Melany of Rome (438).
Troparion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:

You loved the purity of virginity and convinced your
husband with gracious words. You spent your fortunes for
the monks and nuns, and you built monasteries for them, O
Melany, blessed by God. Therefore you have gone to dwell in
a heavenly monastery. Remember us, O all-glorious Melany.
Kontakion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 4:
You fulfilled the divine mandate and gave your gold to the
multitude of the poor. Joining your husband, you took up your
cross and followed Christ, crucified in the flesh, our only God.
On this day the leave-taking of the Nativity of Christ
is celebrated.

Menologion - December

714

1

January
THE CIRCUMCISION ACCORDING TO
THE FLESH OF OUR LORD, GOD, AND
SAVIOR JESUS CHRIST.
COMMEMORATION OF OUR FATHER
AMONG THE SAINTS BASIL THE
GREAT, ARCHBISHOP OF CAESAREA
IN CAPPADOCIA (379).
Troparion of the Feast, Tone 1:

O Jesus, although You are seated on a fiery throne with
the eternal Father and Your divine Spirit, You were pleased
to be born of a virgin maiden, your Mother who has never
known man. Therefore, as man You were also circumcised
when You were eight days old. Glory to Your most noble
decision! Glory to Your salvation! Glory to Your humility!
You alone love mankind.
Troparion of the Saint, Tone 1:
Your voice resounds to the whole world which has
received your word of instruction in divine dogmas. You
explained the nature of creation and gave rules to order human
conduct. O royal priest, O venerable father Basil, beg Christ
our God to grant us His great mercy.
Kontakion of the Saint, Tone 4:
You have appeared as the unshakeable foundation of
the Church, leading all mortals to safe pasture in the Lord,
715

Menologion - January

and confirming them by your teachings, O venerable Basil,
revealer of heavenly mysteries.
Kontakion of the Feast, Tone 3:
The Lord of all endures circumcision and being good, He
cuts away the sins of mortals. Today He grants salvation to
the world, and the bishop Basil, the Creator’s morning star,
rejoices; he has been initiated into the mysteries of Christ.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who was circumcised according
to the Law on the eighth day for our salvation, have mercy on
us and save us:

2

Pre-festive Day of the Feast of Light [Theophany].
Our Holy Father Sylvester, Pope of Rome (335).
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:

Zebulun, make ready; Naphtali, prepare yourself. O River
Jordan, stand and leap for joy to receive the Master coming to
be baptized. O Adam, rejoice with the first mother, Eve, and
do not hide yourselves as once you did in Paradise. For, seeing
you naked, Christ has appeared to put on the first robe. He has
appeared to renew all creation.
Troparion of the Saint, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.

716

Menologion - January

Kontakion of the Saint, Tone 4:
O God-bearer of the King and God, having been a
companion of fasting ascetics, you were revealed as a priest
among priests: O father Sylvester, the glory of pastors, being
happy in the heavens where the angelic hosts now rejoice
together, save in love those who keep your memory.
Kontakion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:
Today the Lord appears in the Jordan’s streams and cries
out to John: do not be afraid to baptize me, for I have come to
save Adam, the first created.

3

The Holy Prophet Malachi.
The Holy Martyr Gordius (304).
Troparion of the Prophet, Tone 2:

O God-wise Malachi, you announced the fearsome day
of the coming of Christ, and you prophesied of the fulfilment
of the Law, saying: truly the Lord is coming, Whom we have
joyfully sought in the temple, and now we pray to Him to save
our souls.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 4:
O Prophet, by bestowing rich prophesies, you clearly
predicted the coming of Christ, Who enlightened the world by
His radiance, and the salvation of the world.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 8:
As a soldier unyielding against suffering, and bearing
717

Menologion - January

the invincible crown among the martyrs, O Gordius, you are
worthy of all praise, rising in the east like a great star shining
with truth, and a martyr bestowing grace upon Christians.

4

The Synaxis of the Holy Seventy Apostles.
Our Venerable Father Theoctistus, Hegumen at
Cuomo Monastery in Sicily (800).
Troparion of the Apostles, Tone 3:
O holy apostles: see page 548.
Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Apostles, Tone 2:

O faithful, let us praise the choir of the Seventy Disciples
of Christ, and let us sing praise to them in hymns. For they all
taught us to consider the Trinity undivided, and are the divine
shining lights of our Faith.
Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 1:
You gained your merit by feeding the sheep of the Lord
by your words of exhortation in an unfeeling land, O Godbearing Theoctistus. You filled it with zeal and presented it to
the Savior. Now that you have passed over to Him, you have
received a reward worthy of your troubles. Glory to Him Who
gave you strength. Glory to Him Who crowned you. Glory to
Him Who heals all through your labors.

718

Menologion - January

5

The Holy Martyrs Theopemptus and Theonas (c. 350).
Our Venerable Mother Syncletica (4th Century).
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:

After Elijah had been taken up, the River Jordan was
parted in two by Elisha’s mantle; and a dry path was opened
in the waters as an image of true baptism by which we pass
beyond this fleeting life. Christ appeared at the Jordan to
sanctify the waters.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Troparion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: see page 554.
Kontakion of the Pre-festive, Tone 2:
O most compassionate Christ, Who take away the many
sins of all, because of Your immeasurable mercy, You have
come to be baptized in the waters of the Jordan as a man,
clothing in a robe of glory the misery of my ancient nakedness.
Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 1:
Theopemptus with the mighty Theonas have been
revealed as a means of holiness to those on earth. How well
they endured the suffering imposed by the torturer. They
rejoice in the Lord and sing: we adore Him Who buried the
sins of all in the flowing waters of the Jordan.

719

Menologion - January

Kontakion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 5:
You endured the pain of your suffering by fasting. You
are delighted to find a finer dwelling in heaven and have been
filled with more splendid light because you followed Christ so
courageously along the difficult path. You turned away from
the goods of earth and became like an angel. Now you share
in their glory.

6

THE HOLY THEOPHANY OF OUR LORD,
GOD, AND SAVIOR JESUS CHRIST.
Troparion, Tone 1:

At your baptism in the Jordan, O Lord, worship of the
Trinity was revealed; for the Father’s voice bore witness to
You, calling You His beloved Son, and the Spirit in the form
of a dove confirmed the truth of these words. O Christ God,
You appeared and enlightened the world. Glory to You!
Kontakion, Tone 4:
You have revealed yourself to the world today; and Your
light, O Lord, has set its seal on us. We recognize You and
exclaim to You: You have come and revealed Yourself, O
Unapproachable Light.
Dismissal:
May Christ our true God, Who for our salvation deigned
to be baptized by John in the Jordan, have mercy on us and
save us:
720

Menologion - January

7

The Synaxis of the Holy, Glorious Prophet,
Forerunner, and Baptist John.
Troparion of the Forerunner, Tone 2:

The memory of the righteous is celebrated with praise,
but for you, O Forerunner, the Lord’s testimony is enough.
You were shown to be more honorable than the prophets since
you were deemed worthy to baptize in the waters the Lord you
had proclaimed. Therefore, you fought for the truth, and with
joy proclaimed the good news to those in Hades, that God has
appeared in the flesh to take away the sins of the world and to
grant us great mercy.
Or this, in the same tone:
O prophet, Forerunner, and dweller in the desert, you
heard the divine voice of the Father, you were deemed worthy
to baptize the Son and Lord, and you were a witness of the
Holy Spirit. Having proclaimed the baptism of repentence,
now ask for us the forgiveness of sins, that through your
prayers we may receive the great mercy of Christ our God.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
The River Jordan trembled, and was driven back filled
with fear at your coming in the flesh, while John drew back
in awe as he fulfilled the ministry of the Spirit. The ranks of
angels stood amazed when they beheld You baptized in the
stream, and we, who were in darkness, are filled with light,
praising You, God-made-manifest, Who enlighten all!

Menologion - January

Our Venerable Father George the Chozebite (614)
and [Our Venerable Father] Emilian the

Our Venerable Mother Domnica (474).
Troparion of the feast.
Troparion of the Venerable Men, Tone 4:

Come, O people, and piously honor the memory of
George. Sing praises for his wonderful fasting and praise
Emilian for his profession. Let us cry out: O Christ, save our
souls for the sake of Your venerable men.
Troparion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: see page 554.
Kontakion of George, Tone 4:
You were revealed as the brightest star, O George,
enlightening with divine rays those who faithfully call to you:
Pray for us to the Master, Christ, Who has revealed Himself in
the streams, and Who enlightens those born on earth.
Kontakion of the Venerable Woman, Tone 4:
O Domnica, you crucified the flesh with your sufferings,
and your love for Christ was total and constant. For this you
have been crowned and admitted to the choirs of the angels.
Pray for all those who venerate you, O venerable mother.

When the Savior bowed His head in the Jordan, the heads

Our Father among the Saints Gregory of Nyssa (c. 395).

God of our fathers: see page 549.

Watching with the eye of your soul, O Bishop, revealing

unharmed, O all-wise Gregory.

Menologion - January

That divine hierarch of the Church and precious mystic

Kontakion of the Venerable Man, Tone 1:
You were anointed with the divine priesthood, and you
showed this by virtue and obedience to Christ. Having finished

Our Venerable Father Theodosius, Founder of

Troparion, Tone 8:

Your abundant tears: see page 667.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Planted in the courts of your Lord, you beautifully
blossomed by your venerable virtues and you multiplied
your children in the wilderness, giving them drink from the

Therefore let us cry: rejoice, O father Theodosius.

The Holy Martyr Tatiana (c. 227).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb, O Jesus: see page 553.
Or this, Tone 2:

You followed the most pure Lamb and Shepherd, O

beasts, but you armed yourself with the Sign of the cross
and you vanquished them to the end. You have entered the

Kontakion, Tone 4:
O passion-bearer, adorned with your blood you shone
forth radiantly in your suffering, and like a beautiful dove

13

The Holy Martyrs Hermylaus and Stratonicus (c. 309).

On this day the holy fathers in Sinai and Raithu killed
by Bedouin is sung together with this commemoration so
that the leave-taking of the feast of holy Theophany is on
the 14th day.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.

Our Venerable Fathers massacred [by the Arabs] in

Troparion, Tone 4:

Having escaped from worldly fame, and having died

Menologion - January

Kontakion of John, Tone 2:
Having loved evangelical poverty freely accepted, you
turned down your parents’ wealth, O most wise John. Taking

The Veneration of the Precious Chains of the

Troparion, Tone 4:

Without leaving Rome you come to us by your precious

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Let us praise the great Peter, the highest and first among
the apostles, truly the disciple of the Divine One. Therefore,
let us kiss his chains with faith, that he may grant forgiveness
of our sins.

Christ the Rock gloriously praises the rock of faith, the
First-throne of the disciples, O Peter. He commands all to

Menologion - January

celebrate the feast of your wondrous and honorable chains,

17

Our Venerable and God-bearing Father
Anthony the Great (356).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Father Anthony, you zealously imitated Elijah in
righteousness, and you followed the straight paths of the
Baptist. You were a desert-dweller and established the world
through your prayers. Therefore, pray to Christ God for the
salvation of our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Having rejected the cares of this life, you quietly ended
this way of life, imitating the Baptist in every model of
venerable asceticism. Together with him we honor you, O
Anthony, the Beginner of the ascetical fathers.

Our Fathers among the Saints and Archbishops
of Alexandria, Athanasius (373) and

Troparion, Tone 3:

Having shone with deeds of the true faith, having
extinguished all heretical slander, you were victorious trophybearers. Having enriched all with God-fearing piety, you
greatly beautified the Church, and you properly found Christ
God, granting us great mercy.

Menologion - January

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Most magnified hierarchs of piety, and noble defenders

Having ended a blessed way of life with the choir of

Our Venerable and God-bearing Father 		
Euthymius the Great (473).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Joy to you, O barren wilderness; rejoice, sterile desert
that has never known the travail of birth, for your spouse has
multiplied your children. He has planted them in devotion
and piety, and made them grow in detachment for the sake of
perfect virtue. Through his prayers, O Christ God, give peace
to our lives.

Our Venerable Father Maximus the Confessor (c. 620).

Today the Church is filled with hymns, and the whole

Kontakion of Maximus, Tone 8:
Zealot of the Trinity, great Maximus, who clearly taught

crying out: rejoice, O preacher of the Faith.

Menologion - January

Kontakion of Neophyte, Tone 4:
You are a new shoot in the garden of Christ’s passionbearers. You offer the fruits of heavenly understanding which
nourish those who venerate you in faith. O glorious, wise,

Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 2:
Having assembled together, let us praise the devoted
and God-bearing martyrs shining as stars of light: Eugene,
Candidus, Valerian, and Aquila with them. They spurned the

The Holy Apostle Timothy.
The Holy Venerable Martyr Anastasius the Persian (628).
Troparion of the Apostle, Tone 4:

Having learned goodness and being temperate in all

Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
Let us, the faithful, sing praises to Timothy, divine
disciple, and companion of Paul, and with him honor the wise
Anastasius, who shone like a star from Persia, driving away
our spiritual passions and carnal infirmities.

The Holy Martyr Clement, Bishop of Ancyra (c. 296).
The Holy Martyr Agathangel (c. 296).

You were an honorable branch of the vine of Christ, O

Our Father among the Saints Gregory the
Theologian, [Archbishop of Constantinople]
(389).
Troparion, Tone 1:

Your theology like a shepherd’s flute has overcome the
trumpet blasts of orators. As you have searched the depths

Gregory, now pray to Christ our God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
O glorious one, you destroyed rhetorical traps with your

of orthodoxy woven from on high, and wearing them she cries

Menologion - January

27

The Translation of the precious Relics of our
Father among the Saints John Chrysostom
(438).
Troparion, Tone 8:

The divine Church sings praises and the whole world
radiantly celebrates the transfer of your honorable relics,
O venerable hierarch John Chrysostom. You lived in Godfearing piety among hierarchs and freely willed to be a martyr.
Therefore, we sing to you: O tortured martyr who shared the
throne of hierarchs, pray to Christ God to save our souls.
Or this, in the same tone:
The grace shining forth from your mouth like a torch has
enlightened the universe; it has stored up in the world the
treasure of disdain for wealth. It has shown us the heights of
humility. Instruct us by your words, John Chrysostom, our
father, and intercede with the Word, Christ God, to save our
souls.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
The honorable Church is mystically joyful in the return of
your honorable relics, and hiding them as gold of much value!
Through your prayers, O John Chrysostom, abundantly grant
healing grace to those singing to you.

31

The Holy Wonder-workers and Unmercenaries
[Physicians] Cyrus and John (311).
Troparion, Tone 5:

The grace of the Trinity settled in your pure hearts, O
most blessed Cyrus and John. You have become marvelous
exorcists of impure spirits. You were doctors over hidden and

God Who loves mankind, through your unceasing prayers
heal our spiritual diseases.
Or this, in the same tone:
The miracles of Your holy martyrs give us unconquerable

snares of the nations by the strength of the scepter of the
kingdom, for You alone are good and the Lover of Mankind.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Having received the gift of wonders from divine grace, O
holy ones, work wonders unceasingly, cut out all our passions
through your unseen skill, O God-wise Cyrus with glorious
John, for you are divine physicians.

February

1

Pre-festive Day of the Meeting of our Lord, God
and Savior, Jesus Christ.
The Holy Martyr Tryphon (250).
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 1:

The angelic choir of heaven looks earthward, peering
down from the heavenly heights to behold the firstborn of all
creation carried into the Temple as an infant in the arms of the
mother who has not known man. Together with us they are
overwhelmed with awe and sing a hymn in preparation for
the feast.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Pre-festive, Tone 6:
The invisible Word of the Father has become visible in
the flesh. He was born of the Virgin ineffably and was placed
in the arms of the elderly priest. Let us all worship Him, our
true God.

739

Menologion - February

Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 8:
You have destroyed polytheism to the ends of the earth
with firm Trinitarian resolve, O all glorious; you were honored
by Christ. And having conquered the torturers through Christ
the Savior, you received the crown of martyrdom and the gift
of divine healing, for you are invincible.

2

THE MEETING OF OUR LORD GOD AND
SAVIOR JESUS CHRIST [WITH SIMEON
AND ANNA].

A Feast, and fish is permitted, during the holy Forty

Rejoice, Theotokos,
Virgin full of grace; for
from you has shown forth
the Sun of Justice, Christ
our God, enlightening
those who are in darkness.
Rejoice also, you just
elder; you received in
your arms the liberator of
our souls, who grants us
resurrection.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
Christ our God,
through Your birth You
sanctified the virgin’s
740

Menologion - February

womb and blessed the hands of Simeon as was proper. Now
You have come and saved us. Give peace to nations at war and
strengthen our government. You, alone, love mankind.

May Christ our true God, Who for our salvation deigned
to be held in the arms of the righteous Simeon, have mercy on
us and save us:

3

The Synaxis of the Holy and Just Simeon, Who
received God, and the Prophetess Anna.
Troparion of the feast.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Today the elder Simeon is filled with happiness, receiving
in his arms the eternal God as an infant. And he begs to be
released from the bonds of the flesh, for he says: my eyes have
seen the salvation of the world.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Today the elder is removed from the bonds of his prayerful
way of life in the flesh taking in his hands Christ, the Creator
and Lord.
Or this, in the same tone:
Today the elder Simeon, receiving the Creator and Lord
of all into his arms, prayed to be released from the bonds of
this corruptible life. He was released and departed to eternal
life.

Menologion - February

4

Our Venerable Father Isidore of Pelusium (c. 450).

If it is not the 40 Day Fast, the service of the feast and
the saint [is observed].
Troparion of the Venerable Man, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image: see page 550.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
The Church, finding you another morning star, O most
glorious one, enlightening her by the lightning of your words,
cries out to you: Rejoice, O all-blessed, God-wise Isidore.

The Holy Martyr Agatha (250).

Rejoice, praise of Catania.

Our Venerable Father Bucolus, Bishop of Smyrna
(2nd Century).
The Holy Martyr Silvanus, Bishop of Emesa,
and his Companions (313).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.

Menologion - February

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Shining with the light of the priesthood, you enlightened
the people, O bishop. You destroyed the darkness of idolatry,
and you dispersed the clouds of the passions by your cures.
You have gone before the unsetting Light. Now we ask you to
pray for us who honor you, O all-blessed Bucolus.

7

Our Venerable Father Parthenius, Bishop of 		
Lampsacus (318).
Our Venerable Father Luke.
Troparion, Tone 4:
God of our fathers: see page 549.
Kontakion, Tone 3:

You received the divine grace of miracles, O God-wise
priest, God-bearer, and wonderworker, Parthenius. You
cleansed all the faithful of passions and drove away evil
spirits, O father. Therefore, we sing to you as a great revealer
of the mysteries of the grace of God.
Kontakion of Luke, Tone 8:
God, Who chose you before birth for His service and led
by Him by destiny, always sanctifies you from the womb and
reveals you as His slave, directing your path, Luke, as a lover
of mankind. Now, rejoicing, you stand before Him.

743

Menologion - February

8

The Holy Great Martyr Theodore the Recruit (318).
The Holy Prophet Zechariah the Sickle.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Recruited by the truth, O passion-bearer Theodore, you
proved yourself a capable warrior for the King of heaven.
You equipped yourself wisely with the armor of faith and
conquered legions of demons. Because you revealed yourself
as a victorious athlete, therefore in faith we ever bless you.
Troparion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
As we celebrate the memory: see page 548.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You put on the whole armor of faith with courage and
took the word of God as a spear in your hand. You conquered
the enemy, Theodore, great among martyrs. Together with
them, never cease to pray to Christ God for all of us.
Kontakion of the prophet, Tone 2:
You saw the chariots being directed by the hand of the
God of all, and you looked down upon the bodiless servants,
O Zechariah. As you rejoice among them now as an evermemorable prophet, pray for those who celebrate your memory
with faith, O all-sanctified one, that we may be directed upon
the road of divine understanding.

9

The Holy Martyr Nicephorus (260).
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord: see page 550.
744

Menologion - February

Kontakion, Tone 1:
Having been united in love, O Nicephorus, you clearly
destroyed the spite of hatred, and beheaded by the sword, you
became a divine martyr of the incarnate Savior; pray for us,
who sing your glorious memory.
Or this, Tone 3:
O glorious one, you were inspired by the love of the
Lord, and taking His precious cross upon your shoulders,
you shamed the goats of the devil. You endured even to death
and have been revealed a true conqueror, a defender, and an
initiate in the mystery of grace.
On this day is the leave-taking of the feast of the Meeting.

The Holy Martyr Charalampus (203).
[In Benedictine communities: Our Venerable Mother

Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion, Tone 8:

Made perfect by the grace of the priesthood, O glorious
one, you adorned the Church with splendor through your
divine suffering. You rejoiced as you bravely accepted torture
for the sake of Christ, O Charalampus, and honored lamp of
the universe, enlightening the ends of the world, for you are
invincible.

The Holy Martyr Blaise, Bishop of Sebaste (316).

Kontakion, Tone 2:

Holy plant, God-bearing martyr Blaise, unfading blossom

Our Father among the Saints Meletius, Archbishop

The apostate Macedonius fled in fear from your spiritual

Our Venerable Father Martinian (c. 398).

O blessed one, you appeased the flames of passion with

746

Menologion - February

the assault of the wild beasts. You cried out: glorified are You,

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Let us worthily praise in hymns the ever-memorable

sufferer and desert dweller and settler, for he trampled on the

Our Venerable Father Auxentius (5th Century).
Troparion, Tone 1:
You made the wilderness your dwelling: see page 639.
Kontakion, Tone 2:

You found your joy in asceticism, O God-wise one, and

The Passing of our Venerable Father Constantine
the Philosopher, in the monastic life called
Cyril, Teacher of the Slavs (869).
Troparion, Tone 4:
From infancy you diligently made wisdom as your sister,
O Voice of God, and, having perceived most radiantly, took
her as a chaste virgin wife. You adorned your mind and soul
with it like a gold yoke. You became a second Cyril, O blessed
one, with the name of reason and wisdom.
747

Menologion - February

Kontakion, Tone 2:
With firm and divinely inspired teaching, and enlightening
the world with an exceedingly bright dawn, flashing around
the universe like lightening, O Blessed Cyril, you spread the
most holy word of God, to the West and to the North and to
the South enlightening the world with wonders.
The Venerable Maron, Hermit and Wonder-worker
(c. 423).

The Holy Apostle Onesimus.

The Holy Martyrs, the Presbyter Pamphilius,

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.

Menologion - February

Kontakion, Tone 4:
To the frightful tortures prepared for them, the

who praise their struggle.

17

The Holy Great Martyr Theodore the Recruit
(306).
Troparion, Tone 2:

Great are the accomplishments of faith. The holy martyr
Theodore rejoiced in the fountain of flames just as if resting
in calm water. Consumed in the fire, he was offered up like
a sacrifice of sweet-breads to the Holy Trinity. Through his
prayers, O Christ God, save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Having accepted the faith of Christ in your heart like
a shield, you trampled down the adverse powers, O GreatSufferer. Therefore, you have been crowned eternally with a
heavenly crown, O Theodore, as one who is invincible.

Menologion - February

Kontakion, Tone 3:
Sitting on the throne of the priesthood, O Glorious One,
you stopped the mouths of the rational lions with divinelyinspired dogmas of the precious Trinity, and illumined your

been glorified as a divine mystic of the grace of God.

Menologion - February

Kontakion of Eustathius, Tone 3:
You preached that the Word was of one essence with

Kontakion, Tone 1:

Offering verbal fruits for a sacrificial offering of virtuous

by your words, sing to your praiseworthy memory, glorifying

The First and Second Finding of the Precious

The head of the Forerunner has shone from the earth

one voice to Christ our God.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
O Prophet of God and Forerunner of grace, your head has
come from the earth like a sacred rose. We are being healed
always; as of old, so now again, you preach repentance to the
world.

Our Father among the Saints Tarasius, Archbishop

Kontakion, Tone 3:

Having explained the dogmas of the Church to those who

to venerate and worship the honorable icon of Christ, you
vanquished the godless iconoclastic heresy. For this reason,
let us cry out to you: Rejoice, O wise father Tarasius.

Our Father among the Saints Porphyrius, Bishop

Alleluia, or the Troparion, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.
Or this, in the same tone:

Who can recount all your works and sufferings of piety,
O father? For you never ceased working day or night until
you washed Gaza clean of impurity and replaced its evil ways
with sound devotion. Thereby, you always stand guard over
your flock. So, holy Porphyrius, pray to Christ God that He
may save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Adorned by your dedicated habits, you glowed in
the vestments of the priesthood, O all-blessed God-wise

As a venerable monk, you depended on God, and
