756

March

1

The Holy Venerable Martyr Eudoxia (2nd Century).
If it is the Forty Days, we sing Alleluia.
If it is not, the Troparion, Tone 8:

You bound your soul to the love of Christ by purity of
heart, and you spurned perishable things as a disciple of the
Word. You brought your senses under control by fasting, and
then you shamed the enemy by enduring martyrdom. Because
of this Christ gave you a double crown, O glorious Eudoxia,
venerable martyr: pray to Christ God that He may save our
souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Having struggled well in asceticism during your suffering,
you sanctify us even after death with the pouring out of
wonders, O all-praised one. Those who hasten to you in faith
in the divine church and solemnly celebrate, we pray to you,
O venerable martyr Eudoxia, that we may be delivered from
spiritual infirmities and receive the grace of wonders.

757

Menologion - March

2

The Holy Priest-Martyr Theodotus, Bishop of Cyrene
(302).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 3:

Having denounced the depths of false belief, you also
wounded the godlessness of idolatry with true belief. Having
been a divine whole-burnt offering, you also refreshed the
ends of the earth with wonderworking. O father Theodotus
the hierarch, pray to Christ God to grant us great mercy.

3

The Holy Martyr Eutropius and his Companions,
Cleonicus and Basiliscus (308).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 1:

This trinity of martyrs confessed the Precious Trinity
before many nations. Undergoing their suffering of martyrdom,
they have been presented to the angels. Today we are honoring
them, celebrating their sacred and life-saving memory.
758

Menologion - March

4

Our Venerable Father Gerasimus of the Jordan (475).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 8:

Living a life angelic in fasting and powerful in prayer,
unwavering in faith, unceasing in vigil, and temperate in all
things, you astonished the angels and vanquished the legions
of devils, O father Gerasimus. You gladden the hearts of the
faithful, O blessed saint. The beasts were obedient to you for
all of this. Since you have achieved a place of honor before
the Lord, pray for the salvation of our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Having burned with care from above, you preferred the
harshness of the Jordan desert to all the sweet delights of
the world from where a wild beast served you in obedience
until your death, and died in grief on your grave, O father.
Therefore, God has glorified you and when you pray to Him
remember us, O father Gerasimus.

5

The Holy Martyr Conon (251).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:

With our hymns, let us praise Conon as a hard worker and
an unshakeable martyr. He is a blessed sufferer who received
power over devils. Let us praise him with hymns and cry out
to him: pray to Christ God that He may save our souls.
759

Menologion - March

Kontakion, Tone 3:
Having lived an angelic life on earth in your purity, you
were admitted in company with the angels in heaven. You
brought your parents to a knowledge of Christ and shed your
blood to profess the one God in the Trinity. Pray unceasingly
for all of us, O martyr Conon.

6

The Holy Forty-two Martyrs of Ammorium (848).
Allleuia, or the Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 2:

Let us all worthily crown with praiseworthy wreaths the
newly revealed stars of faith fervently suffering for Christ.
Praying to Christ for us, as true pillars they supported the
Christian realm.

7

The Holy Priest-Martyrs and Bishops of Cherson:
Basil, Ephrem, Capiton, Eugene, Etherius, and
others (4th Century).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
God of our fathers: see page 549.
760

Menologion - March

Kontakion, Tone 2:
The radiant day of the pastors who brightly ruled as
bishops in Cherson has dawned, so let us sing of the feast for
those who suffered for the sheep of Christ. O priest-martyrs,
pray to the chief shepherd Christ, that He may number us with
the sheep on His right hand, so that we may cry out to you:
rejoice, blessed fathers, who poured out your blood for Christ.

8

Our Venerable Father and Confessor Theophylactus,
Bishop of Nicomedia (845).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 6:

You attempted to live a hidden life, O most praise worthy
one, but Christ made you as a light upon the spiritual rational
lamp. He handed you the tablets of spiritual knowledge:
enlighten us through them.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You were revealed as a lamp to the ends of the world,

essence with the Father and the Spirit. You explained this to
the godly fathers of the council. You were revealed as a pleaser
of the Trinity; standing before the Trinity, pray unceasingly
for all of us.

Menologion - March

9

The Forty Holy Martyrs, martyred at Sebaste on
a frozen lake (320).
Troparion, Tone 1:

O forty soldiers of Christ and honorable passion-bearers,
you went through fire and water, O mighty warriors, and have
come to live with the angels. Join them in praying to Christ for
those who praise you. Glory to Him Who strengthened you!
Glory to Him Who crowned you! Glory to Him Who heals us
through you!
Or this, in the same tone:
O Lover of Mankind, accept the sufferings which Your
saints endured for You. As we pray, heal all our pains.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
Holy long-suffering forty martyrs of the Lord, you all left
the military life of the world to unite yourselves to the Master
of the Heavens. Blessed ones, you proceeded through fire and
water, worthily accepting your many crowns of glory.

Menologion - March

By enduring violence you slew the proud enemy as you

Quadratus. Therefore, we celebrate your honorable memory,

Our Father among the saints Sophronius, Patriarch

Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 8:
Guide to Orthodoxy: see page 555.
Kontakion, Tone 8:

Having struggled ascetically, with divine zeal, you spread

patriarchs of Jerusalem. You brought all wise words into

Menologion - March

Our Venerable Father and Confessor Theophane of

Our Father among the saints Gregory, Pope of Rome

Adorning your life with purity and disciplining your body,

unceasingly that He have mercy on our souls.
Troparion of Gregory, Tone 4:
You received divine grace from God, O glorious Gregory,
and strength from His divine power. You who willed to follow
the gospel, O all-blessed one, pray to Him that He may save

Kontakion of Theophane, Tone 2:
Having received divine revelation from above, you left
living fame with care. Having lived in solitude, O venerable
one, you accepted the wonder of action and the worthiness of
prophecy, having lost wealth and wife.
Kontakion of Gregory, Tone 4:
You became very much like the shepherds of Christ. You
led flocks of monks into the heavenly sheepfold. There you
taught your flock the law of Christ, O father Gregory, now
singing in the heavenly dwellings and rejoicing with them.

Kontakion, Tone 1:
The patriarchal choir honors your holy memory in praises

the sick, the banisher of enemies, and speedy intercessor for

The Holy Martyr Agapius and the Six Martyrs

The choir of seven holy martyrs suffered powerfully for

Menologion - March

17

Our Venerable Father Alexis, Man of God (411).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Elevated in virtuous works and purified in mind, you
attained the promised goal; having adorned your life with
passionlessness, and with a pure conscience, you took up
acceptable fasting; dwelling in prayer as if bodiless, you
shone like the sun in the world, all-blessed Alexis.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Having been like a foreigner in the house of your parents,
you were installed in it as a model of the poor. Receiving
the crown of glory after your repose, you were revealed
wonderful on earth, O Alexis, man of God, joy of both angels

Kontakion, Tone 1:

With your divinely inspired tongue, O wise one, you

in essence yet separate in persons. Therefore, rejoicing, we
celebrate your all-holy memory, offering you as an intercessor
before God.

Menologion - March

19

The Holy Martyrs Chrysanthus and Daria (c. 253).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 3:

Desiring the perfect Good, you pursued whatever good
you saw. By your golden words of truth, blessed Chrysanthus,

and shamed the enemy. Remember us with all who faithful
celebrate your memory.

20

Our Venerable Fathers of the Saint Sabbas
Monastery, killed by Saracens (796).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
God of our fathers: see page 549.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

You openly disdained the pleasure of earthly and
corruptible things, all-blessed ones, choosing a way of life in
the desert. You despised the most beautiful things of the world
and temporal food; hence you were granted the kingdom of
heaven, celebrating with the choirs of martyrs and ascetics.
Therefore, honoring your memory, we fervently cry out to
you: O fathers, deliver us from tribulations.

Menologion - March

21

Our Venerable Father and Confessor James, Bishop
of Catania (8th Century).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 8:
Guide to Orthodoxy: see page 555.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

You subjected your body by abstinence from food, O
most-blessed James. You abandoned the world and followed
Christ. You were given the holy anointing of the priesthood,
and now you stand with the heavenly choirs. Pray for all of us
who praise you.

22

The Holy Priest-Martyr Basilides, Priest of Ancyra
(363).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 8:

Having lawfully completed the race, you preserved the
faith, O priest-martyr. For this you were granted the crown
of martyrdom and you were revealed an unshakeable pillar
of the church, having confessed the undivided Trinity, the
Son co-eternal with the Father and the Spirit. Pray to Him, to
deliver those honoring you from distress, that we may sing to
you: Rejoice, O God-wise Basilides.
769

Menologion - March

23

The Holy Venerable-Martyr Nicon and his Students
martyred with him (250).
[Venerable father Method Dominic Trcka.]
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

Having first lived a venerable life, O Nicon, you assembled
a choir subjected to God, ever following you in God-fearing
devotion. From the east to the west you shine like the sun
dispersing darkness, and wash out deceit by the torrent of
your blood.

24

Pre-festive Day of the Annunciation of the most
holy Theotokos.
Our Venerable Father Zacharias.
Our Father among the Saints Artemon, Bishop of
Seleucia of Pisidia.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Today is the prelude of joy for all the world and hymns
are sung in anticipation. For, behold, Gabriel appears bringing
good news to the Virgin and exclaims to her: rejoice, O Full of
Grace, the Lord is with you.

770

Menologion - March

Kontakion, Tone 8:
By the descent of the All-Holy Spirit, at the sound of the
Archangel’s voice, O Theotokos, you conceived the One Who
shares the Father’s essence and His throne, and is Adam’s
restoration.

25

THE ANNUNCIATION OF OUR MOST HOLY
LADY, THE THEOTOKOS AND EVERVIRGIN MARY.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Today is the summit of our salvation, and what was hidden
from before all ages is revealed: the Son of God becomes a
virgin’s son, and Gabriel announces the good news of grace.
Therefore, let us exclaim with him to the Theotokos: Rejoice,
O Full of Grace, the Lord is with you.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O Theotokos, valiant
defender, your servants offer
you hymns of victory in
thanksgiving, for you have
delivered us. But since you
have invincible power, free
us from all peril, that we may
exclaim to you: Rejoice, O
Unwedded Bride.

771

Menologion - March

26

The Synaxis of the Holy Archangel Gabriel.
If it is the Forty Days, Alleluia. If it is not:
Troparion, Tone 4:

Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us by your prayers and to
shelter us beneath the wings of your sublime glory. Watch
over us who bow to you and cry out fervently: deliver us from
danger, for you are the commanders of the powers on high.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O Commander of the angels, you are the glorious servant
and intercessor of the all-radiant and honorable, and allvirtuous, infinite and awesome Trinity. Now ever pray that
we may be delivered from every tribulation and suffering, that
we may cry out to you: rejoice, O Protection of your servants.

Our Holy Mother Matrona of Thessalonica (c. 350).
Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb, O Jesus: see page 553.
Kontakion, Tone 5:

You served the Creator of all with devotion, O honorable
woman, not serving the unbelieving mistress. But you suffered
the assaults of her rage and being locked in the strong prison,
772

Menologion - March

and so were placed with God. O God-wise martyr Matrona,
pray for us who celebrate your memory.

Our Venerable Father Hilary the Younger (754).

Kontakion, Tone 5:

Like lamps shining like the sun, O fathers, your memory

who celebrate your memory and deliver us from temptations
of life, O all-honorable Hilarion and Stephen.

Our Venerable Father Mark, Bishop of Arethusa, the

God of our fathers: see page 553.

Menologion - March

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Having become a splendor of truth, you have illumined
the very ends of the earth. For this reason we bless you, O

30

Our Venerable Father John Climacus, Author of
“The Ladder” (649).
Troparion, Tone 4:

O venerable John, we have found your good deeds to be
a divine ladder leading us to heaven, for you were a model of
virtue. Therefore, pray to Christ God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
John, our teacher and father, the Lord has raised you to the
heights of abstinence, to be a true guiding star enlightening
the ends of the earth.
Or this, in the same tone:
O wise and blessed one, you gave us your teaching from
your book as fruits ever ripe to liven the hearts of those who
hear them well. Your doctrine is like a ladder that leads to
heavenly and everlasting glory the souls of those who honor
you.

Kontakion, Tone 1:

You shine over the earth, O holy father, Hypatius, and

Having poured out your blood, O wise one, you willed even

April

1

Our Venerable Mother Mary of Egypt (c. 530).
Troparion, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: see page 554.
Or this, in Tone 3:

Once, you who had been filled with all kinds of harlotry,
repentance has made you a bride of Christ. And by living the
angelic life, you destroyed the power of the devil with the
armor of the cross. By this you were revealed as the bride of
the King, O glorious Mary.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Having fled the gloom of sin and enlightened your heart
with the light of repentance, O glorious one, you went to Christ,
bringing His all-immaculate and holy Mother as a merciful
intercessor before Him, and from where you found remission
of your transgressions, ever-rejoicing with the angels.

Menologion - April

Kontakion of Joseph, Tone 4:
You are an inexhaustible source of repentance, an endless

Kontakion of George, Tone 3:
You wished to be the best friend of the Bridegroom, and

The Holy Martyrs Theodulus and Agathopodes and

Alleluia.
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 8:

Brothers by the grace of the Spirit, truly united as one
in pious faith, renowned indeed, you passed through life in
prayer and fasting, drawing people to divine knowledge.
Therefore, as brave soldiers, you imprisoned the deception of
the enemy; and suffering under the law, you were awarded
crowns: pray Christ God to grant remission of sins to those
who lovingly celebrate your holy memory.

The Holy Priest-Martyr Antipas, Bishop of

Alleluia.
782

Menologion - April

Troparion, Tone 4:
You abolished the temptations of the idols, O Antipas,
and trampled down the power of the devil; you fearlessly
confessed Christ before the impious: Therefore, being installed
in the highest with the angelic ranks, offering doxology to the
Master of all, you offered a thanksgiving prayer service for us,
bestowing healing grace. Therefore, we honor you, O priestmartyr Antipas, pray to Christ God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Sharing a throne with the Apostles you were also the
adornment of hierarchs, O blessed one; glorified as a martyr
you shone like the sun. Enlightening all, O dedicated Antipas,
you destroyed the deep night of impiety. Therefore, we honor
you as a divine priest-martyr and bearer of healing.

Menologion - April

for the Master. Therefore, Christ also gloriously encircles you

You set out firmly with priestly devotion and completed

The Holy Virgins and Martyrs Agape, Irene, and

Alleluia.
Troparion,  Tone 4:

You finished the race and kept the faith. O rational lambs,

Therefore, today, with spiritual joy, extolling Christ, we
properly celebrate your holy memory.
Kontakion of Irene, Tone 4:
O blessed one and brave soul, Irene, by faith you have set
up a defensive camp, clearly confusing the evil one; and you
have led many people out from darkness to Christ, bearing the
royal purple of their blood, you now rejoice with the angels.
Or this Kontakion, of the Martyrs, in the same tone:
Having pledged yourselves to the Lord so gracefully, you
made an offering of your blood at your martyrdom. O holy
martyrs, you have been admitted to heaven’s banquet hall, and
the splendid brilliance of the Light himself. As we celebrate
your holy memory, we bless the Savior and we cry out: pray
to the Lord for all of us.

THE HOLY, GLORIOUS AND VICTORIOUS

Troparion, Tone 4:

You fought the good fight with faith, O George, martyr

offered yourself as an acceptable sacrifice to God. Therefore,
you received a crown of victory, and through your prayers, O
holy one, you obtain forgiveness of sins for all.
Or this, in the same tone:
O victorious Great Martyr George, protector of the poor,
liberator of prisoners, physician of the sick, and champion of
kings, intercede with Christ God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Cultivated by God, you became an excellent gardener
of religion, harvesting sheaves of virtues for yourself. You
sowed in tears but reaped in joy. You fought to the shedding of
your blood, and through your prayers, O holy one, you obtain
forgiveness of sins for all.

The Holy Martyr Sabbas the General (272).

790

Menologion - April

one: Therefore, you were crowned with a beautiful wreath of

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Revealed as an invincible general, you conquered the

who faithfully honor you, O all-blessed Sabbas.

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Receiving the grace of the Spirit from on High, you

Menologion - April

Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 2:

Our Father among the saints Athanasius the

Menologion - May

Blaring trumpet of the Lord and flute of the Spirit, O great
Athanasius, O fiery mind, it is fitting to sing your praises with
hymns; for you taught us to honor the Trinity of one essence.

(286).

Your martyrs, O Lord: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

You suffered many kinds of wounds and received crowns

people; for He is the foundation of the faithful.
The Passing of our Venerable Father Theodosius
of the Monastery of the Caves (1074).

Troparion, Tone 8:
Having been raised on virtues, having loved the monastic
life from childhood, and having valiantly reached your desire,
796

Menologion - May

you settled in a cave and adored your life with the radiance of
fasting. You abided in prayer like a bodiless being, shining in

Christ god to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 3
Today let us honor a Slavic star who shone from the East
and came to the West. For this the whole land and all of us

4

The Holy Martyr Pelagia (287).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb Pelagia, O Jesus: see page 553.
Kontakion, Tone 3:

Having distained the temporal, you became a partaker of

from our tribulations.
Or this, Tone 1:
Having inflamed your soul with love for Christ, you
entered the boiling pot with strength of courage. You offered
yourself as a pleasing sacrifice to the Master. Therefore, we
honor your all-holy memory today and we sings hymns to
you.

The Holy and Glorious Martyr Irene.
Our Venerable Father Nicephorus, Hegumen of the
Medikion Monastery (14th Century).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb Irene, O Jesus: see page 553.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

Adorned with the goodness of virginity, O virgin, you

Or this, in the same tone:
Powerful in spirit, Irene, armed with faith, you were

6

The Holy and Just Job the Long-suffering.
Troparion, Tone 1:

Having beheld the riches of the virtues of Job, the enemy
waited to rob the righteous one in ambush, and having
attacked the pillar of the body, could not steal the treasures of
the spirit, for they discovered his soul armed and undefiled.
They stripped and chained me. As You warned me: Before
the end, deliver me from the seducer, O Savior, and save me.
798

Menologion - May

Kontakion, Tone 8:
You were revealed as true and righteous, pious and
blameless, sanctified, O all-glorious one. Being truly pleasing
to God, you enlightened the world by your patience, O most
patient and valiant one. Therefore, all of us sing to your
memory, O divinely-wise one.

The Appearance of the Sign of the Precious cross
in the heavens at the third hour of the day
in the Holy City of Jerusalem, before the
Emperor Constantius (357).
The Holy Martyr Acacius (303).
Troparion of the cross, Tone 8:

The image of Your cross is radiating now more brightly
than the sun, stretching from the holy mountain to the place
of execution, and You have shown Your strength through
the sign of the cross, O Savior; by this sign also confirm the
faithful emperor; and save them always in peace through the
prayers of the Theotokos, and save us, O Christ God.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
The heavens opened on the imprisoned, all-radiant beams
in the heavens, radiating the all-pure cross on earth: Therefore,
accepting the radiance of its action, guiding us to the eternal
light, in our struggles we have it as an armor of peace, an
invincible victory.

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Who shall declare your greatness, O virgin disciple? For

Menologion - May

The Translation of the precious Relics of our
Father among the saints Nicholas the
Wonderworker from Myra to Bari (1087).
Troparion, Tone 4:
The bright festive day has come, the city of Bari rejoices,
and the entire universe will exult with them in hymns and
spiritual songs: For today is the sacred celebration of the
translation of the honorable and much healing relics of the
bishop and wonderworker Nicholas. Like the never setting
sun shining with splendid rays, and dispersing the darkness
of temptations and troubles, from those who faithfully sing:
Save us great Nicholas.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
As a star goes from the East to the West, so do your
relics, O Hierarch Nicholas. The sea was consecrated with
your journey, and the city of Bari receives grace through you:
For you revealed to us works of a gracious, marvelous and
merciful wonderworker.

[Our Holy Father and Confessor Basil Hopko

who honor your memory.

Our Venerable Father Onuphrius the Great
(400).
Our Venerable Father Peter of Athos (734).
Troparion, Onuphrius, Tone 4:

God of our fathers: see page 549.
Or this, Tone 1:
You entered the desert, being led by spiritual yearning, O
God-wise Onuphrius, and you fought in it for many years like
a bodiless one. You are the equal of the Prophet Elijah and of
the Baptist, and you were delighted by the Sacred Mysteries
ministered by angel hands. Now that you have gone to them
in the light of the Holy Trinity, pray for us who honor your
memory.
Troparion of Peter, Tone 8:
The mountain of Athos rejoices, inviting all the monastic
choirs to praise you. We join them in singing to your memory,
O venerable Peter, and honoring you we pray: Ask for peace
in the world and great mercy for our souls from Christ God.
Kontakion of Onuphrius, Tone 3:
Enlightened by the light of the most Holy Spirit, O wise in
God, you already left the life of rumors. You have reached the
desert, O venerable father. You rejoiced in God, the Creator,
Who is over all. Therefore, Christ, the Great Giver of gifts,
glorified you, O blessed one.

822

Menologion - June

Kontakion of Peter, Tone 2:
Having removed yourself from human cohabitation, you
have even lived in caves of stone, with the divine desire and
love of your Lord, O Peter, from Whom you have received
your crown. Pray unceasingly for all of us to be saved.

13

The Holy Martyr Aquilina (293).
The Holy Triphyllus, Bishop of Leucosia [Nicosia]
on Cyprus (370).
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your lamb Aquilina, O Jesus: see page 553.
Troparion of the Hierarch, Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 2:

With the goodness of your virginity and pre-purified
soul, you flowed to the height of martyrdom, O all-honorable
Aquilina, when you were wounded with love for your
bridegroom Christ, with Whom you gladly stand among the
angels. Do not cease praying with them for all of us.
Kontakion of the Hierarch, Tone 8:
With the respectable way of life you accepted the purity
of virginity, O Tryphyllius, you were shown to be the firstenthroned of Leucosia. You were revealed to them as a
prophet and intelligent guide. For this reason we cry out to
you: Rejoice, O adorned hierarch.

823

Menologion - June

14

The Holy Prophet Elisha.
Our Holy Father Methodius, Patriarch of
Constantinople (847).
Troparion of the Prophet,  Tone 4:

An angel in the flesh, the foundation of the prophets, and
the second foreruner of Christ, the glorious Elijah from on
high sent grace to Elisha to cure sicknesses and cleanse lepers.
He likewise overflows with healing for those who honor him.
Troparion of the Hierarch,  Tone 4:
Your life has shown you: see page 549.
Or this, Tone 4:
Burning with zeal for the holy icons, O most wise saint,
you boldly opposed the malice of the king. You were locked
in a tomb and suffered torment, and for your labors you were
exiled. Do not forget us who sing of your fame, O most blessed
pastor Methodius.
Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
You were revealed a prophet of God, receiving augmented
grace truly worthy of you, for you were a contemporary with
Elijah, O blessed Elisha. Pray unceasingly with him to Christ
God for all of us.
Kontakion of the Hierarch, Tone 2:
You practiced asceticism on earth as if without flesh,
O Methodius, and you inherited heaven for explaining the
veneration of icons to the end. Although you continued
laboring more for the sick, you did not stop boldly accusing
those blotting out the icons of Christ.
824

Menologion - June

15

The Holy Prophet Amos.
The Venerable Jerome, Priest of Stridonium (420).
Troparion of the Prophet, Tone 2:
As we celebrate the memory: see page 548.
Troparion of Jerome, Tone 8:

Guide to Orthodoxy: see page 555.
Kontakion of the Prophet, Tone 4:
O Prophet, the Spirit purified your splendid heart, O
glorious Amos, and receiving the gift of prophecy from on
high, You cried with a loud voice to all the nations: This is our
God, and there is none beside Him.
Kontakion of Jerome, Tone 3:
Delighting in purity, O wise-in-God, you repressed the
urges of the flesh. You glowed with faith and bloomed like an
orchard in paradise, O priest and father Jerome.

16

Our Holy Father and Wonder-worker Tychon, Bishop
of Amathis (c. 425).
Troparion, Tone 1:
You made the wilderness your dwelling: see page 639.
Or this, Tone 4:

You first crucified yourself to the world by becoming
poor among the living. Then like a true shepherd, you put
your life at the disposal of your flock. Enriching your sheep
825

Menologion - June

with miracles, you became a bright light for the Church of
Amathis. By shedding light on it, you saved it from the fog of
deceit, O father Tychon. Through your prayers enlighten us
today as we praise you.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
O Holy One, you became God-beloved through fasting;
you received power from the Comforter on high to destroy the
idol of temptation, to save people, to cast out demons, and to
heal the infirm: Therefore, we honor you as the friend of God,
O blessed Tychon.

17

The Holy Martyrs Manuel, Sabel, and Ishmael
(c. 633).
Our Venerable Father Hypatius, Hegumen of the 		
Rufenianos Monastery.
Troparion,  Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 2:

Because of your perfect faith in Christ, O all-blessed
ones, and having drank this cup in faith you renounced
Persian service and boldness on earth, equal in number with
the Trinity, praying for us at all times.

18

The Holy Martyr Leontius (c. 73).

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyr Leontius, O Lord our God: see page 550.
826

Menologion - June

Kontakion, Tone 3:
You shamed the torturers as having evil tricks, and you
exposed the service of the Pagans as godless. You showed
the reason of God into all mankind through your teaching of
piety, O Godly-wise martyr. Therefore, we lovingly honor
your memory, O all-wise Leontius.

19

The Holy Apostle Jude, Brother of the Lord
according to the flesh.
Troparion, Tone 1:

Knowing you as the relative of Christ, O Jude, we praise
you as a firm martyr, O dedicated one. You preserved the
faith by trampling down temptation. Therefore, today, as we
celebrate your all-holy memory, through your prayers, may
we receive remission of sins.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
You were revealed a chosen disciple for your firmness of
mind, and an unshakeable pillar of the church of Christ. You
preached the word of Christ to the nations, telling them to
believe in one divinity. Being glorified by Him, you received
the gift of healing, to heal those infirm coming to you, O allpraised Apostle Jude.

827

Menologion - June

20

The Holy Priest-Martyr Methodius, Bishop of Patara
(311).
Troparion,  Tone 1:

Your blood, O wise one, quietly cries out from the
earth, like Abel to God, O Godly-wise bishop Methodius.
You clearly preached the incarnation of God; therefore, also
putting the flattery of Origen to shame, you were translated to
the heavenly bridal chamber. Pray to Christ God that He may
save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
As a server of the sacred mysteries of the Holy Trinity,
and as a preacher of the divine commandments beyond
comprehension, you were the confirmation of the true faith,
O Methodius. You denounced heretical ideas; you poured out
your blood as a priest-martyr for the sake of the true faith.
Standing before Christ with the angels, pray to save us.

21

The Holy Martyr Julian of Tarsus (290).
Troparion,  Tone 4:
Your martyr O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion, Tone 2:

Today, let us all worthily praise Julian, a pious invincible
warrior, seeker of truth and armorer, and cry out to him: Pray
to Christ God for all of us.
828

Menologion - June

22

The Holy Martyr Eusebius, Bishop of Samosata
(379).
Troparion,  Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Kontakion, Tone 4:

You lived piously as a bishop, and followed the path to
martyrdom. You put out the fire of sacrifice to idols, O holy
hierarch Eusebius. As you have boldness before Christ God,
pray to Him that our souls be saved.

23

The Holy Martyr Agrippina (275).
Troparion,  Tone 4:
Your lamb Agrippina, O Jesus: see page 553.
Or this, Tone 4:

You were overcome with love of the heavenly Lord and
turned from the world and the care of the flesh. You endured
the afflictions imposed upon you, saying: receive me into
Your love, O Christ, King of ages, for I am being consumed
for You. Make those who honor you happy in his mercy, O
most praiseworthy martyr Agrippina.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Your light-bearing asceticism draws near with light today,
on which the divine Church honors them, summoning all
joyfully to cry out to you: Rejoice, O all-honorable virgin
martyr Agrippina.
829

Menologion - June

24

THE NATIVITY OF THE HONORABLE,
GLORIOUS PROPHET, FORERUNNER,
AND BAPTIST OF THE LORD, JOHN.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Prophet and Forerunner of the coming of Christ, although
we honor you with love, we cannot give you worthy praise.
Through your glorious and holy birth, your mother was freed
from barrenness and your father from the loss of speech, and
the incarnation of the Son of God is proclaimed to the world.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Today she who once was barren gives birth to Christ’s
Forerunner. He himself is the fulfillment of all prophecy; for
in the Jordan, he imposed his hand upon the Word of God
Whom the prophets had foretold and was shown to be His
prophet, herald, and Forerunner.

25

The Holy Venerable Martyr Febronia (310).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb Febronia, O Jesus: see page 553.
Or this, Tone 8:

First you crucified yourself for the world through silence,
then the world was crucified for you when you entered the
feat of martyrdom. Therefore we sing to you, because you
received a crown from Christ, O Febronia, glorious martyr.
830

Menologion - June

Kontakion, Tone 6:
My bridegroom O sweetest Christ, cried Febronia, it is
not difficult for me to follow You. The sweetness of Your
love gives my soul wings of hope, and the beauty of Your
mercy sweetens my heart. May I drain the cup of suffering
in imitation of You, that You may find me worthy with the
wise virgins to dance for You in the bridal chamber. Therefore
venerable passion-bearer, honoring your ascetic labors, we
pray to you: Pray that we not find the doors of the bridal
chamber locked to us.

26

Our Venerable Father David of Thessalonica (540).
Troparion, Tone 8:
In you, O father: see page 550.
Or this, Tone 4:

Drowning out the noises of the world with hymns, you
took up your abode in a tree in the midst of an orchard, O
father. In your heart you left the world and ascended into
heaven by your good works. There you have taken up your
abode with angels. O David, look down on us who keep your
memory.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
Like an ever-blooming garden, offering the fruits of
virtues, you revealed yourself like a sweet-singing bird in a
tree of the garden. More than paradise, you accepted the Tree
of Life of the Lord in your heart, for having cultivated it, O
Godly-wise One, through which you give nourishment to us
by grace: Ever pray for us David, all blessed one.
831

Menologion - June

27

Our Venerable Father Sampson the Hospitaller (530).
Troparion, Tone 8:

O venerable father, you reaped your reward by your
patience, unceasing prayer, loving, and helping the poor. O
blessed, merciful Sampson, continue praying to Christ God to
save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
As you are a superior physician and well-received
intercessor, we are gathering at your divine shrine, O Godlywise venerable Sampson. Having come together with love,
rejoicing in Psalms and hymns, let us glorify Christ Who
granted you such a grace of healing.

The Translation of the Relics of the Holy 		
Unmercenary Physicians Cyrus and John (412).
[The Translation of the Relics of the Holy PriestMartyr Theodore Romzha, Bishop of
Mukačevo (2003).]
Troparion, Tone 5:

O Christ God, through the wonders of Your holy martyrs,
You have given us an invincible rampart. Through their prayers
disperse the council of the pagans, strengthen the rule of the
kingdom, for You alone are good and the Lover of Mankind.

Menologion - June

Kontakion: Tone 3:
Having received the gift of the divine grace of miracles,
O holy ones, you unceasingly work wonders in the world; you
remove all our sufferings invisibly by the work of your hands,
O God-wise Cyrus together with glorious John; you are truly
divine physicians.

30

The Synaxis of the Holy, Glorious and AllPraiseworthy Twelve Apostles.
Troparion, Tone 4:

Leaders of the apostles: see above.
Or this, Tone 8:
Your preaching has spread over the whole earth, because
you have received the Spirit in flaming tongues. You burned
down the lies of idolatry, and you have caught the straying
people with the model of faith. The heavens declare your
glory for this, and the firmament proclaims your works. We
join them in a song to your memory: through the prayers of
Your twelve apostles, save us, O God.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Today the rock of Christ brightly glorifies both the rock
of faith, the highest ranked of the disciples, and with Paul
the whole assembly of the twelve. faithfully celebrating their
memory, let us glorify the One Who glorified them.

July
The Holy Unmercenary Healers and
Wonder-workers Cosmas and Damian (284).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Today the people sing to God on high because He gave us
doctors who practiced without fee. Let us sing to Cosmas and
Damian: Since you have been given the gift of grace to cure,
give it freely among all who honor your memory.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Having received the grace of healing, you extend healing
to those in need, O glorious wonder-working physicians. But
through your visitation put down the insolence of warriors,
granting healing to the world through your wonders.
or the troparion and kontakion, see page 665.

2

The Deposition of the Precious Robes of our
most holy Lady, the Theotokos at [the church
of] Blachernae [Constantinople] (c. 465).
Troparion, Tone 8:
O Ever-Virgin Theotokos, protectress of mankind, you
835

Menologion - July

have given a majestic blessing to your city. The robe and
sash of your immaculate body remained incorrupt throughout
your seedless child-bearing: For time and nature are renewed
through you. Therefore, let us pray to you: Grant peace to
your city and great mercy to our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
O Pure One, full of the grace of God, you bestowed your
sacred robe with which you covered your holy body as a
garment of incorruption to all the faithful. O protection of all
mankind, let us lovingly celebrate its covering, and let us cry
aloud to you in awe: Rejoice, O virgin, praise of Christians.

The Holy Martyr Hyacinth (108).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyr Hyacinth, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion, Tone 6:

A tree of life of Your faith in the midst of his soul, O
Christ, guards Your martyr to be the most honorable in Your
Garden of Eden, a tree that fearlessly destroyed the serpent of
temptation by the spirit, being crowned in Your glory, great
in mercy.

Our Venerable Martha, Mother of our Venerable

Your life has shown you: see page 549.
Or this,  Tone 1:

You elevated the Church of Christ with your beautiful

Therefore, O Andrew, shepherd of Crete, we sing of you as
a mystical speaker, and we extol your memory glorifying the
friend of Christ among His saints.
and of the Venerable Woman, Tone 8:
In you, O mother, the divine image: see page 554.

By your love for the Theotokos and a holy life you were

Having clearly trumpeted divine sweet-singing, you were

Standing before the Lord in prayer, offering songs and

5

Our Venerable Father Athanasius of Athos
(1003).
Troparion, Tone 3:

While in the flesh, by your way of life, you were admired
by the angelic ranks. With a body you went out against the
invisible webs, O ever-glorious one, and wounded the demonic
regiments. Therefore, O Athanasius, Christ rewarded you with
rich gifts. Therefore, O Father, pray to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
As the immaterial existence is tolerable to the spectator
and the active teller of all that is true, your flock appeals to
you, O preacher of God. Do not weaken prayers for your
servants to be delivered from dangers and visitations, who
sing to you: Rejoice, O father Athanasius.

6

Our Venerable Father Sisoes the Great (c. 429).

Troparion, Tone 1:
You made the wilderness your dwelling: see page 639.
838

Menologion - July

Or this, Tone 2:
Having overcome carnal desires by abstinence, you
crucified yourself to the world. You leveled all lust by living
in the desert, and became like an angel on earth. This is why
we acclaim you as a guide for monks, father Sisoes, and beg
you: implore Christ God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Having struggled ascetically, you were seen as an angel
on earth, O venerable one, ever enlightening the thoughts of
the faithful with divine signs: Therefore, we honor you with
faith, O Sisoes.

7

Our Venerable Fathers Thomas of Maleum and
Acacius, mentioned in “The Ladder.”
Troparion, Tone 4:
God of our fathers: see page 549.
Or this, Tone 1:

Thomas is radiant in his miracles, and Acacius has
become famous for his obedience. They shine as lights for
the world and guiding stars for monks. We have recourse to
you as favorities of God to defend us in battle through your
prayers so that we might ask Christ to forgive our sins since
we honor your memory.
Kontakion of Thomas, Tone 4:
You courageously showed a great victory, inflamed with
839

Menologion - July

divine love. You spurned the mortal king and all earthly
beauty, completing your worldly travels on Mount Malea,
from where you went up to Heaven to the King of kings, O
Thomas, pray unceasingly for all of us.
Kontakion of Acacius, Tone 2:
From childhood, most holy and venerable Acacius, you
followed after Christ, forsaking the world. Imitating His
willing meekness, you overcame the proud torturer. Now pray
unceasingly for all of us.

8

The Holy Great Martyr Procopius (303).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyr, O Lord: see page 550.
Or this, Tone 8:

Receiving heaven’s invitation, O holy one, you turned
from the errors of your ancestors and their ancient ways to
be zealous for Christ like Paul. You endured many tortures
and wounds, and you have been repaid with a crown of glory.
Therefore, pray to Christ to save us, O great martyr Procopius.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
Set ablaze by divine zeal for Christ, and protected by the
might of the cross, Procopius, you cast down the insolence and
boldness of the enemy! You raised up an honorable Church,
excelling in faith and giving light to all of us!

Menologion - July

9

The Holy Martyr Pancratius, Bishop of Taormina.
Troparion,  Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Or this, Tone 8:

Like an arrow on fire, you were armed at Taormina to kill
the godless and to bring light to the faithful. You strengthened
them in the faith by your preaching, and you finished your
work by spilling your blood. O martyred priest Pancratius,
pray for your flock and for all who cherish your memory.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
You were revealed as a brilliant star, O Pancratius, for the
people of Taormina. You were shown also to be a sufferer for
Christ. Since you now stand before Him, O blessed one, pray
for those who honor you.

10

The Holy Forty-five Martyrs in Nicopolis in Armenia
(319).
Troparion, Tone 1:

You were united in mind and spirit O forty-five holy
sufferers, as you opposed the enemy. You proved victorious
and received crowns from Christ God, and the eternal reward
for your martyrdom. Pray that we also may attain them as we
honorably extol you with songs.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
O Martyrs, you have undergone many torments for the
sake of Christ and you have cut down all the idols to the many
841

Menologion - July

gods. You have destroyed every temptation of atheism and
you have corrected this by the power of Christ: Teach us all to
truly openly sing: Alleluia.
Our Venerable Father Anthony of the Monastery
of the Caves of Kiev (1073).
The holy martyred brothers Francis, Mutius,
Raphael, and their Companions, martyred
in Damascus (1860).
Troparion, Tone 4:
Having departed from worldly clamor, you left the world
and followed Christ according to the Gospel. You reached the
quiet refuge of the Holy Mountain of Athos, living there a
life equal-of-the-angels. With the blessing of the fathers, you
came to the hills of Kyiv. There, having fulfilled a life loving
of labors, you illumined your homeland. Having shown a
multitude of monastics the pathway leading to the heavenly
kingdom, you led them to Christ. Beseech Him, O venerable
Anthony, that He may save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Loving Him from your childhood, you surrendered
yourself to God and followed Him with all your heart and
soul, O venerable one. Scorning the passing corruption of the
world, you made a cave in the earth, and in it you struggled
against the unseen snares of the enemy. You illumined the ends
of the earth as a light-radiating sun. Therefore, with rejoicing,
you went over to the heavenly chambers. And now, standing
with the angels before the throne of the Master, remember us
who honor your memory that we may cry out to you: Rejoice,
Anthony our father.
842

Menologion - July

11

The Holy Most Praiseworthy Martyr, Euphemia
(451).
The Passing of Blessed Olga, Princess of Kiev,
named Helen at Holy Baptism (969).
[In Benedictine communities: The Translation of
the Relics of our Holy Father Benedict.]
Troparion, Tone 4:

Having loved Christ your Bridegroom, and having
prepared your bright lamp, you shone with virtues, O allpraised Euphemia. Therefore, you went in with Him to the
wedding, having received from Him a crown of suffering.
Deliver us, who in faith are honoring your memory, from
misfortunes.
Troparion, Tone 1:
Having fixed your mind with the wings of divine
understanding, you flew to Him Who surpasses the visible
creation. Having sought the God and Creator of All, and having
found Him, you received birth again by baptism. Satisfying
yourself of the tree of life, you abide forever incorrupt, O
ever-glorious Olga.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
You underwent struggles both in martyrdom and in faith
for Christ your Bridegroom. Now beseech the Master to
subjugate underfoot the shaking of the enemies of the faithful,
as He did for the six hundred and thirty God-bearing fathers,
accepting the definition of faith and preserving it, O allpraised One.
843

Menologion - July

Kontakion, Tone 4:
Today, let us sing the praises of God the Benefactor of this
world, who exalted the God-wise Olga in the land of Rus’. By
her prayers, may He grant remission of sin to our souls.

12

The Holy Martyrs Proclus and Hilarion.
Our Venerable Father Michael of Malein
(3rd Century).
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord: see page 551.
Or this, Tone 2:

The choirs of angels looked down and were amazed by
your sufferings. By your flesh you vanquished the invisible
power of the enemy, O holy ones, and speared him by the
power of the cross. Pray for us in our need, O Proclus and
Hilarion, that we too may conquer the enemy and save our
souls.
Troparion of Michael, Tone 8:
In you, O father, the divine image: see page 550.
Or this, in the same tone:
Having soared on mental wings to a vision of God, you
left behind all the noises of the world, O blessed saint. You
despised all the explanations according to the flesh but sought
the wisdom from on high. You present yourself as a model for
all of us, saying: it is a good thing to live with God.
844

Menologion - July

Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 4:
Like the morning star, your glorious sufferings enlighten
us with holy miracles. We celebrate your memory, Proclus
and Hilarion: Pray to God for us that He will save our souls.
Kontakion of Michael, Tone 2:
Your deeds purified the burden of the flesh, and your
enlightenment quickly plumbed the spirit, O Michael; and you
are revealed as a domicile hospitable for the Trinty, because of
your clear perception. Pray unceasingly for all of us.

13

The Synaxis of the Holy Archangel Gabriel.
Our Venerable Father Stephen the Sabbaite [of
the Saint Sabbas Monastery] (794).
Our Father among the saints Julian, Bishop of
Kenoman.
Troparion of the Archangel, Tone 4:

Leaders of the heavenly armies, although we are unworthy,
we always beseech you to fortify us through your prayers and
to shelter us beneath the wings of your sublime glory. Watch
over us who bow to you and cry out fervently: deliver us from
danger, for you are the commanders of the powers on high.
Or this, in the same tone:
O people, with a candlelight assembly let us sing the
praises of the leader of heaven’s hosts. He is the servant of
light sent from the Light divine to enlighten all who sing
with love: O Gabriel, leader of the angels, rejoice with all the
powers of heaven.
845

Menologion - July

Troparion of the Venerable, Tone 8:
Guide to Orthodoxy: see page 555.
Kontakion of the Archangel, Tone 2:
Seeing God in glory in the heavens, granting grace upon
earth from on high, O wise leader of angels, Gabriel, servant
of the glory of God, and divine defender of the world, save
and keep those who cry out to you; be our helper so that no
one defeats us.
Kontakion of the Venerable, Tone 4:
You sought the very depth of wisdom, O Stephen, and
great was your joy when you found that precious pearl. You
found understanding in your infirmities, most blessed Stephen.

The Holy Apostle Aquila.
Troparion, Tone 3:

O holy Apostle Aquila: see page 548.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Glorious Aquila, Apostle of the Lord, the Church, having
acquired you like a great sun, enlightens with the splendors of
your teaching those who honor you with faith.

Menologion - July

15

The Holy Martyrs Cyricus and Julitta his mother
(304).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your martyrs, O Lord: see page 551.
Or this, Tone 8:
As a fertile vine, honorable Julitta, you offered to God a
mature fruit, your son, the glorious Cyricus, who was adorned
richly by martyrdom, and filled by your blood. Therefore, the
highest reward was given to you in the highest. Remember us
who sing to you, O valiant martyrs.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Martyrs for Christ, Julitta and Cyricus, you were carried
into the embrace of the Father. Undergoing the brave ascetic
feats, you joyfully cried out: Christ is the praise of martyrs.
The Holy Great Prince Vladimir, Equal to the
Apostles, named Basil at Holy Baptism (1015).
Troparion, Tone 4:
You were like the merchant who sought the fine pearl, O
Vladimir. Distinguished in your rule and seated on the high
throne of Kyiv, the Mother of Cities, which has been saved by
God. Sending envoys to the Royal City to investigate the true
faith and put it to the test, you found Christ the Pearl without
price, Who chose you as a second Paul, and Who shook off
your blindness of soul and body in the holy font. Therefore,
we your people are here celebrating your falling asleep. Pray
that our authorities and God-loving people may be saved.
847

Menologion - July

Kontakion, Tone 8:
O all glorious Vladimir, in old age you imitated the great
Apostle Paul. You abandoned striving after idols as childish
wisdom, and as a fully grown man you adorned yourself with
the purple of divine baptism. Now standing before Christ the
Savior with rejoicing, pray that the leaders of Rus’ be saved
with those entrusted to them.

16

The Holy Priest-Martyr Athenogenes, [Bishop of
Sebaste,] and his Ten Disciples (311).

Troparion, Tone 8:
The holy Athenogenes offered his ten disciples like
a sacrifice to God. The shepherd and his sheep entered the
heavenly fold. By their work they vanquished the lies of
the pagans. O Christ God, save your flock from the wolves
through the prayer of your martyrs.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Priest-martyr Athenogenes, following the words of the
Master, as an excellent pastor you laid down your life for the
sheep of Christ. Therefore, we praise you, together with your
ten disciples who suffered with you, who were led by the fear
of God and your instruction. With His life-originating right
hand the Master has crowned you, for you were well-pleasing
to Him: Pray to Him for all of us.
Memory of the Holy Fathers of the First Six
Ecumenical Councils.
[If July 16 is a Sunday, we commemorate the Holy
Six Ecumenical Councils, If not, we commemorate the
memory of the Holy Fathers of the Six Ecumenical
Councils on the Sunday from July 13 to July 19]

Menologion - July

Troparion, Tone 8:
O Christ our God, You are above all praise. You have
established our fathers as beacons on the earth, leading us all to
the true faith through them. O most merciful Lord, glory to You!
Kontakion, Tone 8:
The preaching of the apostles and the teachings of the
Fathers have confirmed the one faith of the Church, which she
wears as the garment of truth, woven from the theology on
high, as she faithfully imparts and glorifies the great mystery
of devotion.

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your lamb, Marina, O Jesus: see page 553.
Kontakion, Tone 3:
Virgin and martyr Marina, you were adorned with the

You were soaked with the blood of martyrdom and were
glorified by your miracles of healing. Piously, you received
the prize of victory for your suffering.
[Troparion of Blessed Paul, Tone 4:]
[From your youth you loved Christ, the eternal Word. You
desired to serve Him quietly and in simplicity of heart, but the

849

Menologion - July

of faith and the unity of the Church, you offered yourself to

The Holy Martyr Hyacinth of Amastris (4th Century).
The Holy Martyr Emilian (362).

Burning with zeal for God, you did not dread the fire,

An angel in the flesh, the foundation of the prophets, and

He likewise overflows with healing for those who honor him.

Prophet and seer of the mighty deeds of our God, renowned

The Holy Myrrh-bearer Mary Magdalene, Equal

The Translation of the Relics of the Holy Priest

Troparion of Mary, Tone 1:

Keeping His statutes and laws, honorable Mary
Magdalene, you followed Christ Who was born for us from the
Virgin. Therefore, today, celebrating your all holy memory, let
us receive remission of sins through your prayers.
Troparion of Phocas, Tone 4:
You shared in the apostles’ way of life: see page 551.
Kontakion of Mary, Tone 3:
Standing before the cross of the Savior with many others,
and suffering with the mother of the Lord, and with tears
flowing, the most glorious Mary offered praise saying: What
is this strange wonder? The Creator of all creation chooses to
suffer. Glory to Your mighty power.
Kontakion of Phocas, Tone 6:
As a hierarch bringing an offering, O father, you offered
yourself as a living offering at the end. Having lawfully
witnessed to Christ God, strengthened by an angel and willing
death, you are with those who sing to you: Come, O Phocas,
be with us, and no one will be against us.

The Holy Martyrs Trophimus and Theophilus, and

[Repose of our Holy Father Basil Hopko, Bishop of

Troparion, Tone 4:
Your martyrs, O Lord our God: see page 551.
Or this, in the same tone:

O martyrs, you entered the tribunal of the unbelievers like

for the sake of the faith, professing Christ with fortitude.
Intercede with Christ for all we need.
Kontakion, Tone 1:
You embraced all your suffering with heroic stance, and

[Troparion of Blessed Basil, Tone 5:]

not fear the infernal malice of the powerful of this world; he
did not bow his head before the enemies of Christian unity.

martyr Basil, a luminary of our Church.]

The Holy Great Martyr Christine (c. 300).
The Holy Martyrs Boris and Gleb, named
Roman and David at Holy Baptism (1015).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your lamb Christine, O Jesus: see page 553.
Or this, in the same tone:
You became the bride of Christ through the call of the
Gospel, O glorious Christina, you rejected the glory of this
world and the passions of the flesh, and neglected the body
itself, bravely enduring torment. That is why we praise your
sufferings, O martyr of Christ.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
You were known as a light-seeing dove, having golden
wings, and you flew up to the heights of the heavens, O
honorable Christine. Therefore, we celebrate your glorious
feast, and venerate the place that holds your relics. Divine
healing flows out of them abundantly for soul and body of all.
Troparion, Tone 2:
As upright passion-bearers and true hearers of the Gospel
of Christ, O chaste Roman with innocent David, you did not
oppose the brother who was pulled down by the enemy, and
who killed your bodies while not able to touch your souls. Yet
the evil lover of power weeps, for you are rejoicing with the
angelic choirs, standing before the Holy Trinity praying for
the might of your relatives, that they may be pleasing to God,
and to save the sons of Rus’.

Menologion - July

Kontakion, Tone 3:
Shining today is your most glorious memory, O noble
passion-bearers of Christ, Roman and David, summoning us
for the praise of Christ our God. Therefore, hastening to the
shrine of your relics, we receive the gift of healing by your
prayers, O saints, for you are divine Physicians.

The Dormition of the Holy Anna, Mother of the
Most Holy Theotokos.
The Memory of the Holy Women Olympiada
and Eupraxia (early 5th Century).

Troparion, Tone 4:
Having given birth to life, you carried in your womb the

you were translated to the heavenly reception, where those
who are happy dwell; now rejoicing in glory, fervently ask
for the cleansing of sins for us, who lovingly honor you, O

Kontakion, Tone 2:
Let us celebrate the memory of the grandparents of Christ,
faithfully asking their help to deliver everyone from every
affliction, crying out: “Our God is with us, glorifying those as
it pleases Him.”

Menologion - July

Kontakion of the Priest-Martyr, Tone 4:
Having piously lived as a bishop, you also received a

thousand temptations, and granting the faithful independent

Our Father among the saints Clement, the

O holy passion-bearer and healer Panteleimon, pray to

Menologion - July

You received an invitation through the lips of Hermolaus

that we may honor you, O great-martyr Panteleimon.
Kontakion, Tone 5:
You are an imitator of the Merciful One, and He granted

cry out to you: Save us, O Lord.

31

Pre-festive Day of the Procession of the Precious
and Life-creating Cross of the Lord.
The Holy and Righteous Eudocimus (9th Century).
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 1:

Save Your people, O Lord, and bless your inheritance.
Grant victory to your Church over evil and protect Your
people by Your cross.
Troparion of Eudocimus, Tone 4:
Having called you from earth to the heavenly mansion,
the Lord preserves your body whole even after death, O holy
Eudocimus. For you inhabited the abode in both chastity and
purity, O blessed one, having not defiled the flesh. Therefore,
with boldness beseech Christ God to save us.
Kontakion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:
Heaven surpassed the sun in brilliance, for the cross
illumines everything by its radiance. Therefore, You Who are
the Lover of Mankind and the Savior of the world, enlighten
our minds and senses by its power. We have the cross as the
weapon of peace and as an ally.
Kontakion of Eudocimus, Tone 2:
Desiring the highest things, intimately uniting with the
highest, and like a fiery chariot with the divine ascent of virtue,
you perfected the soul, O all-blessed Eudocimus. Having lived
on earth as if bodiless, you pleased the Creator of all.

1

The Procession of the Wood of the Venerable and
Life-creating Cross.
The Holy Seven Maccabees, their Mother
Solomonia and the Elder Eleazar.

From this date we begin the Fast of the Theotokos, and
continue until the 15th day of this month, on the Feast of
the Dormition of the Most Holy Theotokos.
Troparion of the Cross, Tone 1:
Save Your people, O Lord: see page 564.
Troparion of the Martyrs, Tone 1:
We beseech You, O Lord; and through the sufferings these
saints endured for Your sake, we implore You to heal all our
infirmities.
Kontakion of the cross, Tone 4:
Christ our God, Who were willingly raised upon the cross,
grant Your mercies to the new people who bear Your Name.
By Your power grant joy to the Church. Give her victory over
evil with Your invincible trophy, the weapon of peace, as an
ally.

Menologion - August

Kontakion of the Martyrs, Tone 2:
Seven pillars of divine wisdom, seven beacons of divine

with devotion.

2

The Translation of the Relics of the Holy First
Martyr and Archdeacon Stephen (c. 415).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Your head was crowned with a royal crown for the suffering
you endured for Christ God, O proto-martyr Stephen. For
having accused the Judaic outrage, you beheld your Savior
at the right hand of the Father. Therefore, pray for our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 6:
O all-praised Stephen, you were the first to be sown on
earth by the heavenly Divine Gardener; O blessed one, you
were the first on earth to shed blood for Christ, you were the
first to receive the crown of victory from Him in the heavens;
O Proto-martyr, you were the beginning of the suffering
crowned martyrs.

Menologion - August

4

The Holy Seven Children of Ephesus.
The Holy Venerable Martyr Eudoxia (2nd Century).
Troparion, Tone 4:

Great is the wonder of faith, the seven holy youths lived
in the cave as in a royal chamber, and died without corruption;
after a long time they rose again as from sleep, verifying the
resurrection of all men: Therefore by their prayers, O Christ
God, have mercy on us.
Kontakion, Tone 4:
Rejecting the corruption of this world, and receiving
the gifts of incorruption, although they died, they remained
without corruption: Therefore after many years they arose,
burying all the unbelief of the wicked. Let us sing to Christ, O
faithful, as we praise them today.

5

Pre-festive Day of the Transfiguration.
The Holy Martyr Eusignius (362).
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:

Let us go forth to welcome the Transfiguration of Christ;
let the faithful joyfully anticipate the feast and exclaim: The
863

Menologion - August

day of divine gladness has arrived; the Lord ascends Mount
Tabor and the beauty of His divinity flashes like lightning.
Troparion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Your martyr Eusignius, O Lord our God: see page 550.
Kontakion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:
Today all mortal nature radiates divinity at the divine
Transfiguration and cries out with gladness: Christ is
transfigured, saving all.
Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 4:
Let us praise Eusignius the martyr who conquered evil
by the power of Christ. He clearly proclaimed his faith and
was subjected to vicious torments. But he vanquished the
harshness of the torturer and received a victor’s crown from
God Himself.

THE TRANSFIGURATION OF OUR LORD,
GOD, AND SAVIOR JESUS CHRIST.
Troparion, Tone 7:

You were transfigured on the mountain, O Christ our

they could behold. Through the prayers of the Theotokos, let
Your everlasting light also shine upon us sinners. O Giver of
Light, glory to You!
Kontakion, Tone 7:
You were transfigured on the mountain, O Christ our God,
and Your disciples beheld as much of Your glory as they could
864

Menologion - August

bear, that when they would see You crucified they would
understand that You suffered willingly, so they would preach

May Christ our true God, Who was transfigured in glory
on Mount Tabor in the presence of his holy disciples and
apostles:

7

The Holy Venerable Martyr Dometius (363).
Troparion of the Feast.
and of the Saint, Tone 4:

After disciplining yourself with prayer and fasting on
the mountain, you destroyed the hosts of spiritual enemies
with the weapon of the cross, O all-blessed one. You bravely
armed yourself again for martyrdom, having destroyed the
apostate with the sword of faith. For the sake of both, you
were crowned by God, O venerable martyr, ever-memorable
Dometius.
Kontakion of the Saint, Tone 6:
Turning from perishable goods and earthly thoughts which
destroy, O venerable martyr Dometius, you were shown to be
the great instructor of monks, not frightened by the fury of the
emperor, who did not want to honor Christ as the true God.
For this you died, singing the hymn: For God is with me, and
no one is against me.

Menologion - August

about the Holy Trinity to all, O all-blessed Maximus, clearly

Pre-festive Day of the Dormition.
The Holy Prophet Micah.
Troparion of the Pre-festive, Tone 4:

You were enlightened by the blessing of the Holy

Menologion - August

The Translation of the Relics of our Venerable
Father Theodosius, Hegumen of the
Monastery of the Caves.
Troparion, Tone 8:
Guide to Orthodoxy, teacher of piety and holiness,
luminary for the world, inspired adornments of monks, O wise
Theodosius, Harp of the Spirit, you enlightened all by your
teachings; intercede with Christ our God to save our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
You are a successor to the fathers, O holy monk, and
you followed them in your life and teachings, your character
and temperance, your prayer and intercession. Since you
have found favor with God, obtain the remission of our sins
and salvation for those who sing to you: Rejoice, O father
Theodosius.

THE DORMITION OF THE THEOTOKOS
AND EVER-VIRGIN MARY.
Troparion, Tone 1:

O Theotokos, in giving birth you preserved virginity;
and in your falling asleep you did not forsake the world. You
are the Mother of Life and have been transferred to life, and
through your prayers you deliver our souls from death.
Kontakion, Tone 2:
The grave and death did not detain the Theotokos. She
intercedes without rest and is our unfailing hope of protection;
for he who dwelt in the womb of the Ever-Virgin transferred
to life the Mother of Life.

The Holy Martyr Diomedes (298).
Troparion, Tone 2:

We bow before Your sacred image, O gracious Lord, and
beg forgiveness for our offenses, O Christ our God; for You,
of Your own good will, ascended the cross in Your human
nature to deliver from the enemy’s bondage those whom You
created. Therefore, we gratefully cry out to You: By Your

O indescribable Word of the Father, in Your inexpressible

Kontakion of the Martyr, Tone 2:
You vanquished the torturer and became a champion,
crowned with the laurels of victory, O Diomedes. You are an

unconquerable and faithful martyr.

The Holy Martyrs Florus and Laurus (2nd Century).
Troparion, Tone 4:

O faithful, let us fittingly praise the all-blessed Florus
together with the most honored Laurus, the all-beautiful,
divinely wise and most radiant pair who earnestly and openly
proclaimed the uncreated Trinity to all! Having suffered even
to the shedding of your blood and been crowned with the
most splendid crowns, entreat Christ God that He may save
our souls.
Kontakion, Tone 8:
Today, the whole world gloriously honors Florus and
Laurus as martyrs of devotion and divinely-wise athletes of
Christ. May we receive grace and mercy through their prayers
and be delivered from tribulations, dangers, wrath, and sorrow
on the day of Judgment.

You left behind the glory of earthly rank and inherited the

Kontakion of the Saints, Tone 2:
Standing before the Lord in prayer like a star before the
sun, you saw the desired treasure of the Kingdom, filled with
ineffable joy. Throughout the ages, General Andrew, you
forever sing with the angels to the immortal King. Together
with them, pray unceasingly for all of us.

as a suppliant for our souls.

THE COMMEMORATION OF THE
BEHEADING OF THE HOLY PROPHET,

Troparion, Tone 2:

The memory of the righteous is celebrated with praise,
but for you, O Forerunner, the Lord’s testimony is enough.
You were shown to be more honorable than the prophets since
you were deemed worthy to baptize in the waters the Lord you
had proclaimed. Therefore, you fought for the truth, and with
joy proclaimed the good news to those in Hades, that God has
appeared in the flesh to take away the sins of the world and to
grant us great mercy.

Menologion - August

The glorious beheading of the Forerunner was part of
God’s saving plan that the coming of the Savior might be
announced even to those in Hades. Let Herodias mourn for
she sought a lawless murder because she loved neither the
Law of God nor eternal life, but only this false and fleeting
life.

This is the
Hymn of Saint Ambrose,
Bishop of Milan:
We praise You, O God, we acknowledge You to be the
Lord, and all the earth worships You, the Father everlasting. To
You all angels, the heavens and all the powers, the cherubim
and seraphim, cry out in unison with their unceasing voice:
Holy, holy, holy, Lord God of hosts. Both heaven and earth
are full of the majesty of Your glory. The glorious chorus
of the apostles praises You. The praiseworthy company
of the prophets praises You. The white-robed army of the
martyrs praises You. The holy Church throughout the world
acknowledges You: the Father of an infinite majesty; Your
adorable, true, and only Son; and the Holy Spirit, the Paraclete.
You are the King of Glory, O Christ! You are the everlasting
Son of the Father. When You took upon Yourself to deliver
the human race, You did not disdain the Virgin’s womb. When
You had overcome the sting of death, You opened the kingdom
of heaven to all believers. You are seated at the right hand of
God, in the glory of the Father and we believe that You will
come to be our Judge. We, therefore, pray You to help Your
servants whom You have redeemed with Your precious blood.
Make them to reign with Your saints in glory everlasting. O
Lord, save Your people, and bless Your inheritance, govern
us and lift us up forever. Day by day we bless You, and we
883

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

praise Your Name forever, to the ages of ages. Grant, O Lord,
to keep us today without sin. Have mercy on us, O Lord, have
mercy on us. Let Your mercy, O Lord, be upon us, as we have
placed our hope in You. In You, O Lord, have we hoped; let us
never be confounded. Amen.

884

Introduction to the Monastic Rule of Prayer
for those who wish to make use of it
and who are living in the world.
Whether those persons, male and female, are illiterate
or for the sake of those persons who do not have the texts
of the church hymnody inasmuch as they are in villages or
countryside, or in cities where they are unable to go to hear
the church services, and the same Rule is not understood to
be burdensome work, but those who have a desire to please
God, and, through cleansing of the heart of thoughts by prayer
and fasting, that is, to make many repetitions of the prayer in
stillness.
Beginning this rule, make prostrations, and after having
made bows, stand again, and say this:
O God, be merciful to me, a sinner.
O God, cleanse me of my sins, and have mercy on me!
O Lord, You are my Creator, have mercy on me!
O Lord, forgive me, for I have sinned without number.
and:
O Virgin Lady, Theotokos, save me!
My holy guardian angel, protect me from all harm!
Holy (your patron saint) pray to God for me!
885

The Book of Hours: Časoslov

For the Evening Hymn, the Jesus Prayer:
Lord Jesus Christ, Son of God, have mercy on me, a
sinner. One hundred, and twenty-five prostrations.
For Compline, the Prayer: fifty, and twelve prostrations.
For the Canon and the Akathist of the Theotokos, the
Prayer: two hundred, and twenty-nine prostrations.
For the Canon and Parakleisis of the Theotokos, the
Prayer: seventy, and twelve prostrations.
For the Canon of the Guardian Angel, the Prayer: fifty,
and seven prostrations.
For a weekday Canon, the Prayer: thirty, and five
prostrations.
For the Midnight Service, the Prayer: one hundred, and
twenty-five prostrations.
For Matins, the Prayer: three hundred, and fifty
prostrations.
For the First Hour, the Prayer: fifty, and seven prostrations.
For the Third Hour, for the Sixth Hour, and for the Ninth
Hour, likewise the Prayer: fifty, and seven prostrations.
For the Typical Psalms, the Prayer: one hundred, and ten
prostrations.

The End, and Glory to God!

In glory and praise of Almighty God and all His Saints:
observing the order of the Holy Ecumenical
Pontiff Pope Pius XI, by His successor Pope Pius XII,
the labor of the Holy Congregation
for the Eastern Churches,
